<I,001>

{1}

<§ pratyakṣaparicchedaḥ>

[I,001,i]

namo mañjughoṣāya ॥

[I,001,ii]

	sa śrīmān akalaṅkadhīḥ svayam upetyāryo 'nujagrāha yaṃ 
	vyaktaṃ tasya na vetty ayaṃ jaḍamatir loko garīyaḥ padam /
	tatropāsitalokabhartari kṛtā svalpāpy anarthodayā 
	sammohād avadhīraṇeti kṛpayā tannītir uddyotyate // <1.0>

[I,001,iii]

hitāhitaprāptiparihārayor niyamena samyagjñānapūrvakatvād aviduṣāṃ tadvyutpādanārtham idam ārabhyate ॥

[I,001,iv]

tad dvividhaṃ samyagjñānaṃ
	pratyakṣam anumānaṃ ca	...
iti । na hy ābhyām arthaṃ paricchidya pravartamāno 'rthakriyāyāṃ visaṃvādyate । <I,002> nanv anyad api śābdopamānādikaṃ pramāṇam asti । pramāṇasya sato 'traivāntarbhāvāt
							... pramāṇe	...
eva
										... sadṛśātmanā /
	apratyakṣasya sambandhād anyataḥ pratipattitaḥ // <1.1>
dvividha eva hy arthaḥ pratyakṣaḥ parokṣaś ca । tatra yo jñānapratibhāsam anvayavyatirekāv ātmano 'nukārayati, sa pratyakṣaḥ । tadasādhāraṇaṃ vasturūpaṃ svalakṣaṇam । anyas tu buddhau sākṣātsvabhāvopādhānasāmarthyarahito 'yuktapratipattir eva । na cānyadarśane 'nyakalpanā yuktā, atiprasaṅgāt । tasya nāntarīyakatāyāṃ tu syāt । sa hi pratibaddhasvabhāvo yathāvidhaḥ siddhaḥ, tathāvidhasannidhānaṃ sūcayati । sāmānyena ca sambandhino 'rthasya pratipattir anumānam iti dve eva pramāṇe, anyathā pratipattyayogāt ॥

<I,003>

[I,003,i]

na vai pratibandha eva liṅgalakṣaṇam, kiṃ tarhi grāhyadharmaṇi dharmiṇi ca darśanam । na caitacchabdānām astīti kathaṃ na pramāṇāntaram । te tarhi tatrādṛṣṭāḥ kam artham upanayanty apanayanti vā । yatprāgdṛṣṭaṃ tatra smṛtim ādadhāti । sā kim aśabdaliṅgā svayaṃ kathañcid anusmarate na bhavati । asti vānayor avasthayor viśeṣaḥ । tad ime kvacit kiñcid asiddham anupanayanto 'napanayanto vā kathaṃ kasyacit sādhanam । na ca tebhyo 'rthasiddhiḥ, teṣāṃ tatra pratibandhāsiddheḥ । vaktur abhipretaṃ tv arthaṃ sūcayeyur iti sa eva ca tathāpratipādyamāna āśrayo 'stu ॥

[I,003,ii]

tadbhāvabhāvānupalabdhī tarhi prabhavābhāvasādhane nānumānam, ananvayāt । na hy atra dṛṣṭānto 'sti, sādhanāntarābhāvāt tat sādhanatve ca nidarśanānavasthāprasaṅgāt । na, tatra viṣayadarśanena viṣayiṇo vṛttasambandhasya smaraṇāt । na hy anvayavyatirekābhyām anyo hetuphalayos tadbhāvaḥ । tathā yuktopalambham anupalabhamānā nāstīty āhuḥ । tannimittopadarśanenānupalabdhenāstīti vyavahāraḥ sādhyate mūḍhaṃ prati, jananakhyātyā <I,004> pitṛtvavat । adṛśyānupalambhe 'pi nimittābhāvāt sadvyavahārapratiṣedhaḥ, ajananakhyātyā 'pitṛtvavat । tasmāt sarvaṃ svato 'siddham anyatsādhanam avyabhicāryātmasambandham apekṣata iti nāpratyakṣaṃ pramāṇam anumānād vyatiriktam asti ॥

[I,004,i]

nāpratyakṣaṃ pramāṇam astīty aparaḥ । tad ayuktam, yasmāt
	pramāṇetarasāmānyasthiter anyadhiyo gateḥ /
	pramāṇāntarasadbhāvaḥ pratiṣedhāc ca kasyacit // <1.2>

[I,004,ii]

sa khalu pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇaṃ nānumānam iti bruvāṇaḥ kāsāñcij jñānavyaktīnāṃ pravṛttau saṃvādaṃ visaṃvādaṃ copalabhya tallakṣaṇaṃ vyāptyā kathayed yathopaddeśaṃ pravartamānasyāvipralambhārtham । tadyathā dṛṣṭasādharmyāt tathā prasādhitaṃ nānumeyatām atipatati । tac cāsiddham iti na kiñcit pramāṇam apramāṇaṃ vā 'nyatrānubhūtaviṣayābhyo 'nirdeśyalakṣaṇābhyo jñānavyaktibhyaḥ । na ca tābhiḥ svasantānabhāvinībhir alakṣitābhir ayaṃ paraṃ vyavahārayitum īśa ity apraṇayanam eva śāstrasya । praṇayan vā svām eva vṛttiṃ svavācā <I,005> viḍambayati । parāvabodhārthaṃ ca śāstraṃ praṇayann anumānaṃ pratikṣipatīty ayuktam, tasyāprāmāṇye vṛttivaiphalyāt ॥

[I,005,i]

na ca śarīram eva buddhiḥ, tatsiddhāv api buddhivikalpe saṃśayāt । nainam anyasambandhinaṃ puruṣamātrapratyakṣam anveti ॥

[I,005,ii]

pratiṣedhaṃ cāyaṃ kvacit kurvāṇo na pratyakṣeṇa kartum arhatīti, tasyābhāvaviṣayatvavirodhād arthasāmarthyāpekṣaṇāt, anapekṣāyāṃ vyavadhānādibhāve 'pi bhāvaprasaṅgāt । pratyakṣasyaiva nivṛtter abhāvaniścaya iti cet, byāhatam etat — tac ca nāsti tena ca pratipattir iti । nivṛtter vāsyāsad iti kutaḥ, niyamābhāvāt । bhāve vā sa evāvyabhicāro 'nupalabdher iti sā tenābhāvaṃ pratipādayantī liṅgam eva ॥

[I,005,iii]

kasyacit saṃvāde 'pi tajjātīyasya vyabhicāradarśanād anāśvāsa iti cet, na, tadrūpānupalakṣaṇāt । svabhāvapratibandho hi liṅgalakṣaṇam । <I,006> na ca tasya vyabhicāraḥ, tadabhāve svabhāvābhāvāt । tathā hi
	arthasyāsambhave 'bhāvāt pratyakṣe 'pi pramāṇatā /
	pratibaddhasvabhāvasya taddhetutve samaṃ dvayam // <1.3>

[I,006,i]

pratyakṣam apy arthāvisaṃvādād eva pramāṇam । sa cāvisaṃvādas tasmād ātmalābhāt, anyato bhavato 'bhavato vā bhāve niyamena tatsamvādāyogāt । nārthavyabhicārād arthasaṃvādanaṃ pratyakṣasya, kiṃ tarhy arthadarśanād iti cet, tat punar arthadarśanam arthabhāvo vā syāt । arthabhāvaś cet, sarve 'rthāḥ pratyakṣā iti sarvaḥ sarvadarśī syāt । jñānabhāvaś cet, katham anyasya bhāve 'sambaddhasya bhāvaniyamaḥ । darśanād bhāvasiddhir iti cet, nanu tad evedaṃ paryanuyuktam — kim idaṃ darśanaṃ nāmeti । tasmāj jñānabhāvād arthabhāvam icchatā jñānasya tatpratibandho vācyaḥ । sa ca kāryasvabhāvayor liṅgayor anumāne 'pi tulya iti na pramāṇalakṣaṇam anumānaṃ nānveti ॥

<I,007>

[I,007,i]

tatra
	pratyakṣaṃ kalpanāpoḍham abhrāntam	...

[I,007,ii]

timirāśubhramaṇanauyānasaṃkṣobhādyanāhitavibhramam avikalpakaṃ jñānaṃ pratyakṣam । kā punar iyaṃ kalpanā ॥

[I,007,iii]

										... abhilāpinī /
	pratītiḥ kalpanā	...
abhilāpasaṃsargayogyapratibhāsā pratītiḥ kalpanā । tayā rahitam । na hi sendriyajñāne sambhavati,
						... arthasya sāmarthyena samudbhāvāt // <1.4>

[I,007,iv]

tad dhy arthasāmarthyenotpadyamānaṃ tadrūpam evānukuryāt । na hy arthe śabdāḥ santi tadātmano vā, yena tasmin pratibhāsamāne te 'pi pratibhāseran । na cāyam arthāsaṃsparśī saṃvedanadharmaḥ, artheṣu tanniyojanāt, tato <I,008> 'rthānām apratītiprasaṅgāt । tasmād ayam upanipatya vijñānaṃ janayannānātmanāntarīyakaṃ pratibhāsaṃ punaskartuṃ yukto rasādaya iva parasparam । nāpi tadbalenodīyamānaṃ vijñānam arthāntaram anusartuṃ yuktaṃ rasādijñānavat । sato 'pi vā tadātmana indriyāntarajñānotpattāv asāmarthyād atiprasaṅgāc ca । vikalpakaṃ tu manovijñānam arthaśaktisannidhānānapekṣaṃ vikalpavāsanotthāpitam aniyatendriyārthagrāhi kutaścid anubhavasambandhāt saha pṛthag vā gṛhṇīyāt ॥

[I,008,i]

api ca
	arthopayoge 'pi punaḥ smārtaṃ śabdānuyojanam /
	akṣadhīr yady apekṣeta so 'rtho vyavahito bhavet // <1.5>
na hi saṅketakālabhāvitam abhilāpasāmānyam asmaratas tadyojanā sambhavati, śabdāntara iva । na cārthābhipātakṛte 'satyāntare vikāre śabdaviśeṣe smṛtir yuktā, tasyā atatkṛtatve tannāmāgrahaṇaprasaṅgāt । tataḥ smṛtyā vyavadhānān nārthopayogo 'nantaravyāpāraphalaḥ syāt ॥

<I,009>

[I,009,i]

ataś ca
	yaḥ prāg ajanako buddher upayogāviśeṣataḥ /
	sa paścād api	...
syāt । ātmābhedena sāmarthyāviśeṣān naikasyaikatra kriyākriye syātām ॥

[I,009,ii]

					... tena syād arthāpāye 'pi netradhīḥ // <1.6>

[I,009,iii]

arthasya sākṣād buddhāv anupayogāt smṛtiprabodhe copayuktatvān nāsyānupakāriṇo buddhir bhāvam apekṣeta । arthābhipātakṛte ca buddhijanmany abhilāpasmṛtyantarābhāvāt siddham avikalpakaṃ pratyakṣam ॥

[I,009,iv]

kiṃ ca
	viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyaṃ ca sambandhaṃ laukikīṃ sthitim /
	gṛhītvā saṅkalayyaitat tathā pratyeti nānyathā // <1.7>

[I,009,v]

kiñcit kenacid viśiṣṭaṃ gṛhyamānaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatatsambandhalokavyavasthāpratītau tatsaṅkalanena gṛhyate daṇḍyādivat । nānyathā, arthasambandhādhidhānavyavasthāparijñāne <I,010> 'bhāvāt । jātiguṇakriyāvatām etan na sambhavaty eva, rūpavivekasambandhayor apratibhāsanena ghaṭanāyogāt kṣīrodakavad detadvedini । yatrāpi vivekapratipattir asti, tasyāpi grahaṇam ॥

[I,010,i]

	saṅketasmaraṇopāyaṃ dṛṣṭasaṅkalanātmakam /
	pūrvāparaparāmarśaśūnye tac cākṣuṣe katham // <1.8>
na hīdam iyato vyāpārān kartuṃ samartham, sannihitaviṣayabalenotpatter avicārakatvāt । vicārakatve cendriyamanovijñānayor abhedaprasaṅgāt । abhede cātītānāgatavastuprabhedagrahaṇāgrahaṇohānūhārthabhāvāpekṣānapekṣādiprasaṅgaḥ ॥

[I,010,ii]

manovijñānābhisaṃskṛtam indriyajñānaṃ pratyetīti cet, na, yathoktāgrāhiṇas tathāpratipattyayogād aviṣaye 'pravṛtter jātyādisambandhātītaśabdavyavahārādīnām indriyajñānāviṣayatvāt । tasmān nendriyajñānam arthasaṃyojanāṃ kalpanām āviśati ॥

<I,011>

[I,011,i]

	vikalpotthāpitā sā ca nivartyetecchayā matiḥ /
	nārthasannidhim īkṣeta	...

[I,011,ii]

api ceyaṃ viśeṣaṇādivikalpotthāpitā satī pravṛttāpi samagrasāmagrīkā punar icchayā nivartyeta tadanyavikalpavat । śakyante hi kalpanāḥ pratisaṅkhyānena nivartayitum, nendriyabuddhiḥ, sāmagrīsākalye 'pi vinivartya gobuddhim aśvam api kalpayato gor darśanāt । nāpīyam arthasannidhim apekṣeta । na hi gavādivikalpo 'rthasannidhāv eva bhavati ॥

[I,011,iii]

							... nānyathedantayeti cet // <1.9>
na hy ayaṃ gaur ity asannihite 'rthe bhavati । idaṃ ca naḥ pratyakṣaṃ, sannihitārthaniścayalakṣaṇatvāt । naitad asti, yasmāt
	avidyamānābhede 'pi tadakṣāgocaratvataḥ /
	spṛśato 'py asti sā buddhiḥ	...
ko hīndriyāviṣayasyārthasya tadindriyajñānotpattāv avidyamānād bhedaḥ, tatsāmarthyasya tataḥ sarvathā sākṣād vinivṛtteḥ, paramparopayogasyātītād <I,012> api darśanāt । tad ayam aviṣayatvād abhūtāviśiṣṭam api spṛṣṭvā 'yaṃ ghaṭa iti pratipannapratyakṣībhavitum arhati ॥

[I,012,i]

							... dravyaṃ tat spārśanaṃ yadi // <1.10>

[I,012,ii]

tan na । spārśanam api dravyaṃ spṛṣṭvā gṛhṇātīti cet,
	nāyaṃ ghaṭa iti jñāne varṇapratyavabhāsanāt /
na hy ayaṃ ghaṭa iti jñānaṃ sparśanendriyajaṃ yuktam, tathāsamanvāhāre varṇasyāpi pratyavabhāsanāt । tena rūpasparśavijñānānvayo mānasam eṣa smārto vikalpaḥ ॥

[I,012,iii]

api ca
	yatsannidhāne yo dṛṣṭas taddṛṣṭes taddhanau smṛtiḥ // <1.11>
	yuktā tadgatyabhāve tu śabdabhede smṛtiḥ katham /
	tadasmṛtau ca tenārthaṃ saṃsṛṣṭaṃ vetty asau katham // <1.12>

<I,013>

[I,013,i]

yady eṣa niyamaḥ — svābhidhānaviśeṣaṇāpekṣā evārthā vijñānair vyavasīyanta iti, nivṛttedānīm indriyavijñānavārttā, abhidhānaviśeṣe amṛter ayogāt । sati hy arthadarśane 'rthasannidhau dṛṣṭe śabde tataḥ smṛtiḥ syāt, agnidhūmavat । na cāyam aśabdakam arthaṃ paśyati, apaśyaṃś ca na śabdaviśeṣam anusmarati, ananusmarann na yojayati, ayojayan na pratyetīty āyātam āndhyam aśeṣasya jagataḥ ॥

[I,013,ii]

abhipatann evārthaḥ prabodhayatyāntaraṃ saṃskāram । tena smṛtiḥ, nārthadarśanād iti cet, na, tatsambandhasyāsvabhāvikatvāt, samayādarśane 'bhāvāt । puruṣecchāto 'rthānāṃ svabhāvāparāvṛtter na samayakālotpattiḥ svabhāvasya । parāvṛttau ca tasya tādātmyād anyasyāsamayadarśino 'pi syāt । na hi pratipuruṣam arthānām ātmabhedaḥ, nairātmyaprasaṅgāt, ātmasthiter abhāvāt । tasmād ayam aśabdasaṃyojanam evārthaṃ paśyati darśanāt ॥

[I,013,iii]

atha vā pratyakṣasādhana evendriyadhiyaḥ kalpanāvirahaḥ । yataḥ
<I,014>
	saṃhṛtya sarvataś cintāṃ stimitenāntarātmanā /
	sthito 'pi cakṣuṣā rūpam īkṣate sākṣajā matiḥ // <1.13>
apratibhāsamānābhijalpāpratibhāsamānā pratyakṣaiva sarvaprāṇinām indriyabuddhir iti kim atrānyena sādhanena । na cemāḥ kalpanā apratisaṃviditā evodayante vyayante vā, yena satyo 'py alakṣitāḥ syuḥ । tathā hi
	punar vikalpayan kiñcid āsīn me kalpanedṛśī /
	iti vetti na pūrvoktāvasthāyām indriyād gatau // <1.14>

[I,014,i]

sa punaḥ pratisaṃhārād vyutthitacittaḥ kiñcid vikalpayan svacittadhārāḥ saṅkalayaty evaṃ caivaṃ ca kalpanā mamāsīd iti । tad imāḥ kalpanāḥ pratyakṣabhāvinyaḥ kathaṃ saṃhṛtavikalpe darśane 'vibhāvitā nāma । tad ayam asaṃsṛṣṭavikalpo vā pratyakṣo darśanātmā dṛśyātmano vā vikalpasya darśane 'dṛṣṭir vikalpakalpanām indriyajñāne pratihanti ॥

[I,014,ii]

na vai buddhiḥ pratyakṣā, yenendriyajñānasya vikalpopagame bādhā <I,015> syāt । sa eva tāvad ayaṃ vikalpaḥ saṃvidita upayann āpayaṃś ca kvāntarbhāvyatām arthe buddhau vā । nārthe, adhyātmaṃ parisyandādīhāvaśenodayāstamayāyogāc ca । buddhir atra vivarteta, sā cāpratyakṣatā vivṛttāpi na prakāśeta । na ca prakāśo 'rthas tathāvṛttiḥ । nāpy anyaḥ kaścid ihānuṣaṅgīty abhāva evārthābhilāpānukāriṇo 'nubhavātmano vikalpasya । sukhādisaṃvedanaṃ ca buddhiḥ । sā ca parokṣeti nānugrahopaghātau tataḥ syātām, puruṣāntarasaṃvedanavat । ananuyaṃś caiṣāṃ pratyakṣeṇa katham ātmanyanviyāt ॥

[I,015,i]

ajñāte 'rthe buddher asiddhes tajjñāne 'numānād anvetīti cet, jitaṃ jaḍaijayaghoṣaṇām avaghuṣya, yenaivaṃvadino 'py avadheyavacaso loke । arthajñānaṃ ca nāma buddhisādhanaṃ pratyeti na buddhim iti ślāghanīyaprajño devānāṃ priya iti ॥

[I,015,ii]

nārthajñānaṃ buddher liṅgam, kiṃ tarhīndriyārthāv iti cet, avyabhicārī hetuḥ । mana iti cet, tad api pūrvakam evānantaravijñānahetuḥ vijñānaṃ vidmaḥ, tasya viṣayāntarāvadhānavaiguṇye 'nyatra vijñānanutpatteḥ । tac <I,016> cāsiddham । vyakto viṣaya iti cet, nanu sā vyaktir buddhir eva । tadupādhiḥ so 'py asiddha eva । na vyaktir buddhir arthātmeti cet, sa kiṃ abuddhijanmā buddhiṃ gamayet, pratibandhābhāvat । arthāt manaś ca sādhāraṇatvād anyabuddher apy anumanaprasaṅgaḥ । siddhe 'pi hi liṅge 'siddhayā buddhyā sambandhābhāvād ananumānam । tasmāt pratyakṣeyamanabhilāpā ca pratibhātīti ॥

[I,016,i]

	śabdenāvyāpṛtākṣasya buddhāv apratibhāsanāt /
	arthasya dṛṣṭāv iva tadanirdeśyasya vedakam // <1.15>

[I,016,ii]

tac cedaṃ pratyakṣam anabhilāpyaviṣayam, avyāpṛtendriyasya darśanavad buddhau śabdenāpratibhāsanāt । na hi sa śabdārthaḥ, yaḥ śābde na pratibhāsate । na ca śabdaviṣaya eva vastu, ākārāntareṇa darśane pratibhāsanād etāvanmātranibandhanatvāc cātattvasya । vastvabhāve 'pi śābdapratibhāsāpracyuter asadarthapratibhāsāviśeṣāt saty api pratītir atadātmagrāhiṇī, tadbhāvābhāvayor ananukārāt, rasabuddhivad gandhasya cakṣurbuddhivac ca rūpasya । ākārārpaṇakṣamaṃ hi kāraṇaṃ vijñānasya viṣayaḥ । nānanukṛtānvayavyatirekaṃ <I,017> kāraṇam, nākāraṇaṃ viṣayaḥ । tasmān na vastuviṣayāḥ śābdavikalpāḥ ॥

[I,017,i]

arthapratipattaye ca śabdāḥ prayujyante । na cendriyārtho 'nvayī, yataḥ sabdena dṛṣṭasambandho vyavahāre pratīyeta । tathā hi
	ekatra dṛṣṭo bhedo hi kvacin nānyatra dṛśyate /
na hi vyaktyātmānaḥ parasparam anuyanti, śaktipratibhāsādibhedāt ॥

[I,017,ii]

	na tasmād bhinnam asty anyat sāmānyaṃ buddhyabhedataḥ // <1.16>

[I,017,iii]

na hi vyaktyātmano vyatiriktam anvayinam erthaṃ paśyāmaḥ, yaṃ śabdo 'nudhāvet । arthanānātve hi buddhinānātvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ bhūtaguṇavat । tadabhede 'py arthabhedakalpanāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ । sarvātmasv ekatvāniścayād anānātvapratipatter anānaikaṃ jagat syāt ॥

[I,017,iv]

athāpi syāt, pratibhāsamānam api sāmānyam anupalakṣaṇān na vivekena niścīyata iti । tad ayuktam, yasmāt
	dhīśabdavṛtter anyatra tato nānupalakṣaṇam /

[I,017,v]

abuddhiśabdānvatabhājo hi bhedān ayaṃ sāmānyadarśanabalenānvayan <I,018> katham anupalakṣako nāma । na hi yato yatra jñānābhidhānavṛttiḥ, tadanupalakṣaṇe tasya tathāpratītir daṇḍivat ॥

[I,018,i]

	tasmād viśeṣaviṣayā sarvaivendriyajā matiḥ // <1.17>
tatra sāmānyāpratibhāsanāt pratibhāsināṃ cānanvayād viśiṣṭam evānabhilāpyaṃ vasturūpam indriyatayaḥ pratyāviśanti । kathaṃ tarhīdānīm aniścayātmanaḥ pratyakṣād vyavahāraḥ । niścinvanhīdantayā sukhaduḥkhasādhanayoḥ prāptiparihārāya pravartate । nāyaṃ doṣaḥ, yasmāt
	taddṛṣṭāv eva dṛṣṭeṣu saṃvitsāmarthyabhāvinaḥ /
	smaraṇād abhilāṣeṇa vyavahāraḥ pravartate // <1.18>

[I,018,ii]

arthālocanamātre 'pi pratyakṣe 'nubhavasāmarthyabhāvino 'nubhūtapratisandhāyinaḥ smaraṇāt taddṛṣṭāv eva dṛṣṭeṣv abhilāṣetarābhyāṃ vyavahāro bhavati । <I,019> vastudharmo hy eṣa yad anubhavaḥ paṭīyān smṛtibījam ādhatte, tādṛśadarśanād asya prabodho 'bhilāṣavāsanāvivṛttir ato vṛttiś ca ॥

[I,019,i]

	mānasaṃ cākṣavijñānānantarapratyayodbhavam /
	tadarthānantaragrāhi	... <1.19ac>

[I,019,ii]

pratyakṣam iti vartate । mānasam apīndriyajñānena samanantarapratyayena svaviṣayānantarakṣaṇasahakāriṇā janitaṃ pratyakṣam । ata eva ca nānindriyadṛṣṭir nāpi viṣayāntarasya ॥

[I,019,iii]

svajñānakālabhāvī tadatulyakriyākālo narthaḥ sahakārīti cet, na, ubhayos tulyakālatvāt । asataḥ prāgasāmarthyāt sāmarthyakāle ca kāryaniṣpatter anupayogāj jñānahetor viṣayasya sahabhāvo viruddhaḥ ॥

[I,019,iv]

	bhinnakālaṃ kathaṃ grāhyam iti ced grāhyatāṃ viduḥ /
	hetutvam eva yuktijñā jñānākārārpaṇakṣamam // <1.20>
ity antaraślokaḥ ॥

<I,020>

[I,020,i]

na cedaṃ pūrvapramāṇaviṣayagrāhi, anadhigataviṣayatvāt pramāṇasya, anyathā cātiprasaṅgāt, abhraṣṭadarśanasaṃskārasya gṛhītagrahaṇasya smārtād aviśeṣāt । niṣpāditakriye karmaṇy aviśeṣādhāyi sādhanam ity api sādhananyāyam atipatati । kramabhāvavirodhaś ca sarvāsāṃ tadarthahetūnāṃ buddhīnām, anyair akāryabhedasyāpekṣāyogād anapekṣāc ca kramotapattyayogāt । ādheyabhedatve cānyatvam । kṣaṇikatvād arthānām atipātāc ca nāsatāṃ grahaṇam । tasmād arthāntaram eva pratyayaviśeṣotpatter manaḥ pratyeti ॥

[I,020,ii]

							... sukhādīnāṃ svavedanam // <1.19d>
sukhādīnāṃ svasaṃvedanam api pratyakṣam । sukhādigrahaṇam spaṣṭasaṃvedanapradarśanārtham, sarvajñānānām ātmasaṃvedanasya pratyakṣatvāt । na hi sukhādīnām ātmasaṃvedane vikalpāḥ saṃbhavati, yasmad
	aśakyasamayo hy ātmā sukhādīnām ananyabhāk /

[I,020,iii]

nānuditaḥ pratiniyataḥ sukhādyātmā viṣayīkriyate saṃvittyā, <I,021> tasyās tadātmarūpatvāt । nainam iyam abhilāpena saṃsṛjati, tathāvṛtter ātmani virodhāt, tadrūpasya prāgadarśanād abhilāpābhoge ca viṣayapratyastamayāt tadvivekena saṃvido 'py agrāhyahrāhakasya ca samayasyābhāvāt, anyenāpy atītarūpasyāsaṃvedanāt, apunarbhāvini samayasya vaiyarthyāc ca ॥

[I,021,i]

	teṣām ataḥ svasaṃvittir nābhijalpānuṣaṅgiṇī // <1.21>

[I,021,ii]

aśakyasamayatvān na sukhādīnām ātmasaṃvittir āviṣṭābhilāpā । sā pratyakṣaṃ pramāṇam ॥

[I,021,iii]

naivaṃ sukhādayaḥ saṃvedanarūpāḥ । ekārthasamavāyinā tu jñānena saṃvedyanta ity eke । teṣām api
	tadatadrūpiṇo bhāvas tadatadrūpahetujāḥ /
	tatsukhādi kim ajñānaṃ vijñānābhinnahetujam // <1.22>

[I,021,iv]

tadatatsvabhāvānāṃ bhāvānāṃ tādrūpyam atādrūpyaṃ ca paryanuyuktā hetuprakṛtim eva te 'py ālamberan tadrūpahetujās tadrūpā atadrūpahetujā atadrūpāḥ, yathā śālibījādibhyas tatprasavās tadanyebhyo 'nya iti, ākasmikatve <I,022> deśakālaprakṛtiniyamāyogāt ॥

[I,022,i]

tatra sukhādyutpattir nāviṣayā, yathāsvaṃ viṣayopanibandhanānāṃ sukhādīnāṃ tatsannidhānābhāve 'bhāvāt । nāpy anindriyāḥ, rūpādyanuṣaṅgiṇāṃ tadviṣayendriyavirahe 'darśanād anupahatendriyopanidhau ca punaḥ sambhavāt । nāpy amanaskārāḥ, ubhayasannidhāv api middhādiviplutadhiyo 'bhāvāt । etāvān eva vijñānotpatter api kāraṇakalāpaḥ । tatprakṛtes tatkāryasvabhāvaniyame nānupalambhātmanaḥ sukhādayaḥ । saṃskārān niyama iti cer, na, tasya sāmarthyādarśanāt । tanmātrabhāvino 'nyahetutvakalpanāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ । saṃskāra ity āpi pūrvakam eva yogyaṃ vijñānam utpaśyāmaḥ, antaḥkaraṇābhipātināṃ sukhādīnāṃ vijñānabhāvanāpaṭumandatādibhedānuvidhānāt । hetusāmyāt sukhādibhedābhāvaprasaṅga iti cet, na, tasyāḥ sāmagryā evāntaraviśeṣakṛtatvāt saṃśayanirṇayādibhedavat ॥

[I,022,ii]

nāntarāḥ sukhādayo nāpi cetanāḥ । tadātmanāṃ śabdādīnām anubhavāt tadanubhavakhyātir ity aparaḥ । tasyāpi
<I,023>
	aviśeṣe 'pi bāhyasya viśeṣāt prītitāpayoḥ /
	bhāvanāyā viśeṣeṇa nārtharūpāḥ sukhādayaḥ // <1.23>
yadi hi śabdādyātmānaḥ sukhādayaḥ syuḥ, śabdādyaviśeṣe bhāvanāviśeṣāt prītiparitāpaviśeṣo na syān nīlādyābhāsaviśeṣavat । te 'napekṣitatadatiśayā bhāvanānurodhino bauddhā eva prajñādivat ॥

[I,023,i]

	cetanāś cāpi vedyatvād atadrūpāpravedanāt /
cetanāś caite sukhādayaḥ saṃvedyatvāt । na hi yad yadviṣayākāraṃ saṃvedanaṃ na bhavati, tat tasya vedakam, aparaspararūpam iva sukhādisaṃvedanam, idam asya saṃvedanam iti sambandhasyābhivyaktinimittatvāt । indriyādiṣv api prasaṅgāt sārūpyam eva tadvedanalakṣaṇam ॥

[I,023,ii]

sārūpyam apy atadātmanaḥ prāk paścād apy ātmāpracyuteś caitanyasya katham iti cet, ayam aparo 'sya doṣo 'stu । na tv asarūpaṃ vedakaṃ nāma । na hi vittisattaiva tadvedanā yuktā, tasyāḥ sarvatrāviśeṣāt sarvavedanāprasaṅgāt । <I,024> tāṃ tu sārūpyam āviśatsarūpayatnaṃ ghaṭayet । idam eva ca naḥ sukhaṃ yatsātaṃ saṃvedanam iti siddhāḥ sukhādayaś cetanāḥ ॥

[I,024,i]

viṣayasārūpyāt saṃvedanasya tādātmye 'saṃvedanāḥ sukhādaya iti cet, na, tvatpakṣe 'py asti sukhādisaṃvedanam iti darśanārthatvād apakṣepasya । tatrāpi saṃvedanam evaikam āntaraṃ prītiparitāparūpaṃ paśyāmaḥ । na cāsyāyam ātmāparopadhāno yuktaḥ, tadaviśeṣe 'pi svabhāvābhyāsaviśeṣāt tadātmātiśayasiddheḥ । buddhir atiśayavatī na saṃvedanam iti cet, keyaṃ buddhiḥ । adhyavasāyaḥ । kim idaṃ saṃvedanam । anubhavaḥ । ko 'nayor bhedaḥ । viṣayākāraḥ padārtho 'saṃvedano 'nyā saṃvit । asaṃvedanaṃ sārūpyaṃ buddhilakṣaṇam ity anyasyāpi tatsarūpasya tatprāptir viśeṣo vā vācyaḥ । antaḥkaraṇatvādayo 'pi tannibandhanā na vā 'pratipattyaṅgam ity anughoṣyāḥ, tathāvidhasyānyatrāpi svacchatvāder viśeṣasya bhāvāt । saṃvinniṣṭāś <I,025> ca viṣayavyavasthitayaḥ । tāḥ katham avetano 'rtho vyavasthāpayet, atiprasaṅgat । atiśayavac ca bauddhaṃ sukhaṃ anariśaye 'pi śabādisukhā ity api vārttāmātram, ekatra yugapad anayor virodhāt । tasmān na caitanyād anyātiśayavatī buddhiḥ ॥

[I,025,i]

	tadrūpavyatirekeṇa buddher anupalakṣaṇāt // <1.24>

[I,025,ii]

ekam evedaṃ saṃvidrūpaṃ harṣaviṣādādyanekākāravivartaṃ paśyāmaḥ । tatra yatheṣṭaṃ sañjñāḥ kriyantām ॥

[I,025,iii]

apratyakṣā saṃvitpratyakṣo buddhivivarta iti cet, pratyakṣo viṣayopabhogaḥ, tadapratyakṣatve 'nyapratyakṣavat sarvāpratyakṣatvaprasaṅgāt । viṣayo 'stīti ca viṣayopabhogaḥ prāptaḥ, tadbhogasyāpratyakṣatvād asiddheḥ sato 'py asadaviśeṣāl laiṅgikopabhogasya cābhogatvād anyabhogavat । liṅgāyogād ato 'py asiddhir eva, yathoktaṃ prāk । tatra ca pratyakṣe viṣayopalambhe <I,026> samāpto vyavahāra ity apārthakam aparaṃ caitanyam । taṃ caikarūpam eva paśyāma iti nānyā buddhir anyo 'nubhavaḥ ॥

[I,026,i]

	saṃsargād avibhāgaś ced ayogolakavahnivat /

[I,026,ii]

vibhaktāv api cetanādhyavasāyau saṃsargavipralabdho 'yaṃ na vivecayaty ayogolakam iva vahneḥ, tadrūpasparśādhyavasāsāt ॥

[I,026,iii]

	bhedābhedavyavasthaivam utsannā sarvavastuṣu // <1.25>

[I,026,iv]

sarvārthopalambheṣu saṃsargaśaṅkayaikatvān adhyavasāyād bhinnopalambhayor api sukhādinīlādyākārayor anānātvāt kaṃ batāyam āśritya hetuṃ bhadābhedau vyavasthāpayet ॥

[I,026,v]

	abhinnavedanasyaikye yan naivaṃ tadvibhedavat /
	sidhyed asādhanatve 'sya na siddhaṃ bhedasādhanam // <1.26>
	bhinnābhaḥ sitaduḥkhādir abhinno buddhivedane /
	abhinnābhe vibhinne ced bhedābhedau kimāśrayau // <1.27>
<I,027>
iti saṅgrahaślokau ॥

[I,027,i]

ayogolake 'pi vahnisambandhād arthāntaram eva tattathotpannam ekaṃ dṛśyate, na nānārūpayor dravyayoḥ saṃsargād avibhāgaḥ । punas taddravyasantānasthitikāraṇavicchedāt tannivṛttis tadupādānakāraṇāpekṣiṇaś ca śītasparśāder aparotpattiḥ ॥

[I,027,ii]

tasmād antarāḥ sukhādayaḥ saṃvedanāś ca ॥

[I,027,iii]

	bhāvanābalataḥ spaṣṭaṃ bhayādāv iva bhāsate /
	yaj jñānam avisaṃvādi tat pratyakṣam akalpakam // <1.28>

[I,027,iv]

yoginām api śrutamayena jñānenārthān gṛhītvā yukticintāmayena vyavasthāpya bhāvayatāṃ tanniṣpattau yat spaṣṭāvabhāsi bhayādāv iva, tad avikalpakam avitathaviṣayaṃ pramāṇaṃ pratyakṣam, āryasatyadarśanavad yathā nirṇītam asmābhiḥ pramāṇavārttike ॥

[I,027,v]

	kāmaśokabhayonmādacaurasvapnādyupaplutāḥ /
<I,028>
	abhūtān api paśyanti purato 'vasthitān iva // <1.29>
	yathāviplavamāvegapratipattipradarśanāt /
	parokṣagatisañjñāyāṃ tathāvṛtter adarśanāt // <1.30>
	tasmād bhūtam abhūtaṃ vā yad yad evābhibhāvyate /
	bhāvanāpariniṣpattau tat sphuṭākalpadhīphalam // <1.31>
ity antaraślokāḥ ।

[I,028,i]

tathā hy aśubhapṛthivīkṛtsnādikam abhūtaviṣayam api spaṣṭapratibhāsaṃ nirvikalpakaṃ ca bhāvanābalaniṣpannam iṣyate ॥

[I,028,ii]

astu nāma bhāvanābalena spaṣṭābham, nirvikalpakaṃ tu katham । yasmān
	na vikalpānubaddhasya spaṣṭārthapratibhāsitā /

[I,028,iii]

pratyastamitārthavaiśadyo hi sarva eva viplutadhiyo 'pi saṃsṛṣṭābhilāpaḥ pratyayaḥ । tan nāyaṃ sphuṭapratibhāso vikalpako bhavitum arhati । tathā hi
	svapne 'pi smaryate smārtaṃ na ca tat tādṛgarthavat // <1.32>

<I,029>

[I,029,i]

middhopaplutānām apy anubhūtasmaraṇākārā vikalpā bhavanti । na ca te tathāvabhāsinaḥ smaryante । tan na viplavo 'nyo vā vikalpaṃ sphuṭayati । avikalpaka eva sphuṭāvabhāsa iti ॥

[I,029,ii]

svapnajñānaṃ tarhi viśadābhaṃ pratyakṣaṃ bhavatv avikalpanāt । na, abhrāntam iti nirdeśāt । ata eva
	vikalpo 'vastunirbhāsād visaṃvādād upaplavaḥ /
	pratyakṣābho	...
dvividha ucyate । vastupratibhāsaṃ hi pratyakṣam, tadabhāve tadābhāsapracyuter ity uktam । na caivaṃ vikalpaḥ, tatpratibhāsasya vastuny ananurodhāt । tasmāt pratyakṣābhāsaḥ । viplavaś ca
					... 'kṣajatve 'pi tadanyebhyo 'viśeṣataḥ // <1.33>

[I,029,iii]

yo 'pi kaścid viplava indriyajaḥ, tadanyendriyajāviśeṣāt, asāv api vastvananurodhipratibhāso vipralambhāt pratyakṣābhāsaḥ । etena mānaso 'pi viplavo vyākhyātaḥ ॥

<I,030>

[I,030,i]

naiva dvicandrādibhrāntir indriyajety eke । tan na, aindriye bhāvābhāvānurodhasya tattvalakṣaṇatvāt tasyehāpi tulyatvāt, indriyavikāre ca vikārāt, tannibandhanatvāc cāśrayasthiteḥ, sarpādibhrāntivan manobhrānter akṣavikṛtāv api nivṛttiprasaṅgāt, tathākṣavikāranivṛttāv apy anivṛttiprasaṅgāt । tasmād indriyajam apy etad bhrānter apratyakṣam । ata eveti karaṇavyavacchinnād vikalpavargāt pṛthaktaimiropalakṣitaṃ viplavaṃ pratyakṣābhāsam āha sāpavādatvasūcanārtham, anyatra cakṣurādiparamāṇūnāṃ dvicandranīlādyābhāsavijñānahetutvavacanāt ॥

[I,030,ii]

kiṃ punar asya pramāṇasya phalam । prameyādhigatiḥ । sā hi jñānam, tac ca phalam iti kim idānīṃ pramāṇaṃ । yata iyaṃ prameyādhigatir avyavadhānā tattvaṃ pratilabhate । tatra
<I,031>
	arthena ghaṭayaty enāṃ na hi muktvā'rtharūpatām /
	tasmāt prameyādhigateḥ pramāṇaṃ meyarūpatā // <1.34>

[I,031,i]

na hi kriyāsādhanam ity eva sarvaṃ sarvasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ sādhanam, kiṃ tu yā yataḥ । tatrānubhavamātreṇa sadṛśātmano jñānasya sarvatra karmaṇi tenātmanā bhavitavyam, yenāsyedam iti pratikarma vibhajyate । anātmabhūtaś cāsyendriyārthasannikarṣādiṣu hetuṣu vidyamāno 'pi bhedo bhinne karmaṇy abhinnātmano jñānasya na bhedena niyāmakaḥ, kriyānibandhanatvāt karaṇatattvasya tadaviśeṣe tasyā api viśeṣāsiddheḥ, sato 'pi vā viśeṣasya tadanaṅgatayā'karaṇatvāt । tasmād yato 'syātmabhedād asyeyam adhigatir iti ayam asyāḥ karmaṇi niyamaḥ, tat sādhanam । na ceyam arthaghaṭanā'rthasārūpyād anyato jñānasya sambhavati । na hi paṭumandatādibhiḥ svabhedair bhedakam apīndriyādy arthenaitad ghaṭayati, tatra pratyāsattinibandhanābhāvāt । asty anubhavaviśeṣo 'rthakṛtaḥ, yata iyaṃ pratītiḥ, <I,032> na sārūpyād iti cet, atha katham idānīṃ sato rūpaṃ na nirdiśyate । nedam idantayā śakyaṃ nirdeṣṭum । anirūpitena nāmāyam ātmanā bhāvān vyavasthāpayatīdam asyedaṃ neti suvyavasthitā bhāvāḥ ॥

[I,032,i]

	tasmāt prameyādhigateḥ sādhanaṃ meyarūpatā /
	sādhane 'nyatra tatkarmasambandho na prasidhyati // <1.35>
	sā ca tasyātmabhūtaiva tena nārthāntaraṃ phalam /
	dadhānaṃ tac ca tām ātmany arthādhigamanātmanā // <1.36>
	savyāpāram ivābhāti vyāpāreṇa svakarmaṇi /
	tadvaśāt tadvyavasthānād akārakam api svayam // <1.37>
ity antaraślokāḥ ॥

[I,032,ii]

etenendriyasannikarṣārthālocanaviśeṣaṇajñānāni pratyuktāni, tataḥ karmasambandhāsiddheḥ, avyavadhānābhāvāt kārakātiśayāsiddheḥ, sarvakārakopayoge 'pi kriyāyām antyasya tasyaiva bhedakasya sādhakatamatvāt । satsv apīndriyādiṣv abhinnasya prativiṣayaṃ bhedakam asya karaṇam iti । na hīndriyāṇi bhedakāni, sarvajñānahetutvāt । nārthālocanam, <I,033> atādrūpye tasyaiva tadarthālocanatvāsiddheḥ । tathā viśeṣaṇajñānam, aviṣayakṛtaviśeṣasya viśeṣaṇajñānaviśeṣyajñānāviśeṣād vyavasthāsiddheḥ । kriyāsādhanayor viṣayanānātvavirodhāc ca । abhinnaviṣayatvedvayaṃ vyartham । kramabhāvaś cābhinnanimittayoḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ । sakṛdbhāve sādhyasādhanatā'bhāvaḥ, jñānāṃśayos tu sādhyasādhanabhāvo vyavasthāśrayatvāt । vastvabhedāt kriyākaraṇayor aikyavirodha iti cet, na, dharmabhedābhyupagamāt । abhinne 'pi vastuni śaktibhedena vyavasthābhedadarśanāc ca nāyaṃ vastusanniveśī vyavahāraḥ । nāpi sannikarṣaḥ pramāṇam, sarvātmanā sannikṛṣṭasyāpi kaiścid eva dharmaiḥ pratipatteḥ । tadaviśeṣe 'py eṣa viśeṣo buddhipratibhāsakṛta iti tasyaiva prāmāṇyaṃ yuktam ॥

[I,033,i]

atha keyam arthasaṃvid yā pramāṇaphalam । yad evedaṃ pratyakṣaṃ prativedanam । astīdaṃ vedanam, tadarthavedanaṃ kena । utpattisārūpyābhyām । <I,034> anantaraṃ tarhi vijñānaṃ tulyaviṣayaṃ viṣayaḥ prāpnoti । kva tarhīdānīm ayam anubhavaḥ । nanv asyaiva rūpaṃ vayam apy anububhutsavaḥ । idaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ veti darśanaśravaṇābhyāṃ yatrāvasāyapratyayaḥ, te tasyānubhava iti cet, nanu saiva tayoḥ pratyāsattir atra vicāryate — kathaṃ tat tasya darśanam iti । tayor hi sambandham āśritya draṣṭur eṣa viniścayaḥ । sa tadabhāve na syāt । na ca viṣayasārūpyaṃ vijñānasya, tatpratibhāsinaḥ sthūlākārasya pratyekaṃ paramāṇuṣv abhāvāt । ekaś cāyaṃ jñānasanniveśīti na ca bahūni rūpāṇi sañcitāni tathā pratibhāntīti yuktam, ekarūpasya bāhulyavirodhāt । bahuṣu ca tathāvidho nāstīti na tayoḥ sārūpyam ॥

[I,034,i]

nāpi sthūla eko viṣayas tathāvabhāsī, pāṇyādikampe sarvasya kampaprāpteḥ । akampane vā calācalayoḥ pṛthaksiddhiprasaṅgād vastrodakavat । ekasya cāvaraṇe sarvasyāvaraṇaprasaṅgaḥ, abhedāt । na vā kasyacid āvaraṇam ity avikalaṃ dṛśyeta । avayavasyāvaraṇam, nāvayavina iti cet, ardhāvaraṇe 'py anāvṛtatvāt prāgvad asya darśanaprasaṅgaḥ । <I,035> avayavadvāreṇa taddarśanād adṛṣṭāvayavasyāsyāpratipattir iti cet, na, bhedābhāvena sarvathā'pratipattiprasaṅgāt । sarvāvayavānāṃ ca yugapad draṣṭum aśakyatvāt sarvadā cāsyādarśanaprasaṅgaḥ । katipayāvayavapratipattau darśane 'lpāvayavadarśane 'pi tathā sthūlasya darśanaṃ syāt । rakte caikasmin rāgaḥ, araktasya vā gatiḥ । avayavarāge vā'vayavirūpam araktam iti raktāraktaṃ dṛśyeta । tasmān naikaḥ kaścid arthaḥ, yo vijñānaṃ sarūpayati ॥

[I,035,i]

ata eva
	nānyo 'nubhāvyo buddhyāsti tasyā nānubhavo 'paraḥ /
	grāhyagrāhakavaidhuryāt svayaṃ saiva prakāśate // <1.38>
vyastaṃ hi viṣayalakṣaṇam iti na kvacid anubhavo nāpy asya kaścit, tatrāpi grāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇavaidhuryāt । tasmād ātmaiva buddher anubhavaḥ । sa ca nānyasya kasyacit । pratyakṣaprativedyatvam apy asyāṃ tadātmataiva । sā ca tādātmyāt svayaṃ prakāśate । tenātmanaḥ prakāśikety apy ucyate prakāśavat । <I,036> nīlādyanubhava ity api tatsvabhāvo 'nubhava eva ॥

[I,036,i]

	avedyavedakākārā yathā bhrāntair nirīkṣyate /
	vibhaktalakṣaṇagrāhyagrāhakākāraviplavā // <1.39>
	tathākṛtavyavastheyaṃ keśādijñānabhedavat /
	yadā tadā na sañcodyagrāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇā // <1.40>
ity antaraślokau ॥

[I,036,ii]

	tadā'nyasaṃvido 'bhāvāt svasaṃvit phalam iśyate // <1.41ab>

[I,036,iii]

yeṣāṃ bhuddhir evopadarśitagrāhyagrāhakākārotpadyate, teṣām anyasya saṃvedyasyābhāvāt svasaṃvedanaṃ phalam, tatsvabhāvatvād arthapratipatteḥ । yadi hīṣṭākāraḥ so 'nubhavo 'niṣṭākāro vā, tadeṣṭo 'niṣṭo vā viṣayaḥ pratividito bhavati । vidyamāne 'pi hi bāhye 'rthe yathāsvasaṃvedanam evārthaniṣpattes tad eva phalam yuktam । na hy arthasya yathāsvabhāvaṃ vyavasthitiḥ, sarvajñānānām ekākāratvaprasaṅgāt । anekākārās tu vijñaptayaḥ, yenaikaṃ rūpam ekasya manaāpamanyasyāmanaāpaṃ dṛṣṭam ॥

<I,037>

[I,037,i]

iṣṭāniṣṭāvabhāsinyaḥ kalpanā nendriyabuddhaya iti cet, na, tatrāpy ariṣṭādāv apratisandhānadarśanāt, anyatrāpi śabdagandharasaviśeṣair abhinnaiḥ prāṇiviśeṣāṇām aindriyakasyaiva sukhāsukhasyotpatteḥ । tasmāt svasaṃvedanarūpaivārthapratītiḥ । tasyāś ca viṣayākārataiva sādhanam, yathākāram asyāḥ prathanāt । arthasthiteḥ svasaṃvedanarūpatvāt svavid apīyam arthavid eva kāryato draṣṭavyā । ata eva na pramāṇaphalayor viṣayabhedaḥ । svabhāvacintāyāṃ tādātmyād arthasaṃvidaḥ svasaṃvit phalam ucyate ॥

[I,037,ii]

	tathā'vabhāsamānasya tādṛśo 'nyādṛśo 'pi vā /
	jñānasya hetur artho 'pīty arthasyeṣṭā prameyatā // <1.42>
	yathā kathañcit tasyārtharūpaṃ muktvā'vabhāsinaḥ /
	arthagrahaḥ kathaṃ satyaṃ na jāne 'ham apīdṛśam // <1.43>
ity antaraślokau ॥

<I,038>

[I,038,i]

kathaṃ punar asati bāhye 'rthe pramāṇaprameyaphalasthitiḥ । uktam atra — yathādarśanam iyaṃ vyavasthā, na tu yathātattvam iti । viṣayākāraḥ kaścit paricchedaś cāntaraḥ svasaṃviditarūpo jāyamāno lakṣyate । tatra yathālakṣaṇam eveyaṃ meyamānaphalasthitiḥ ॥

[I,038,ii]

	avibhāgo 'pi buddhyātmā viparyāsitadarśanaiḥ /
	grāhyagrāhakasaṃvittibhedavān iva lakṣyate // <1.44>
	mantrādyupaplutākṣāṇāṃ yathā mṛcchakalādayaḥ /
	anyathaivāvabhāsante tadrūparahitā api // <1.45>
	tathaivādarśanāt teṣām anupaplutacakṣuṣā /
	dūre yathā vā maruṣu mahān alpo 'pi dṛśyate // <1.46>
	yathānudarśanaṃ ceyaṃ meyamānaphalasthitiḥ /
	kriyate 'vidyamānā'pi grāhyagrāhakasaṃvidām // <1.47>
	anyathaikasya bhāvasya nānārūpāvabhāsinaḥ /
	satyaṃ kathaṃ syur ākārās tadekatvasya hānitaḥ // <1.48>
	anyasyānyatvahāneś ca nābhedo 'rūpadarśanāt /
<I,039>
	rūpābhedaṃ hi paśyantī dhīr abhedaṃ vyavasyati // <1.49>
	bhāvā yena nirūpyante tadrūpaṃ nāsti tattvataḥ /
	yasmād ekam anekaṃ ca rūpaṃ teṣāṃ na vidyate // <1.50>
	sādharmyadarśanāl loke bhrāntir nāmopajāyate /
	atadātmani tādātmyavyavasāyena neha tat // <1.51>
	adarśanāj jagat yasmin nekasyāpi tadātmanaḥ /
	astīyam api yā tv antarupaplavasam udbhavā // <1.52>
	doṣodbhavāt prakṛtyā sā vitathapratibhāsinī /
	anapekṣitasādharmyadṛgādis taimirādivat // <1.53>
ity antaraślokāḥ ॥

[I,039,i]

bhavatu nāma yathādarśanaṃ pramāṇādivyavasthā, vijñaptimātratāyāṃ saiva kathaṃ sidhyati । uktam atra — grāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇāyogād iti ॥

[I,039,ii]

api ca
	sahopalambhaniyamād abhedo nīlataddhiyoḥ /
<I,040>
na hi bhinnāvabhāsitve 'py arthāntaram eva rūpaṃ nīlasyānubhavāt tayoḥ sahopalambhaniyamād dvicandrādivat । na hy anayor ekākārānupalambhe 'nyopalambho 'sti । na caitatsvabhāvaviveke yuktam, pratibandhakāraṇābhāvāt । rūpālokayos tu tajjñānotpādanayogyatāpratilambhalakṣaṇo 'sti pratibandha indriyayogyatotpattilakṣaṇo veti nānāloko rūpopalambhaḥ syāt, kāryasya kāraṇāvyabhicārāt । nāntarīyakatayālokaḥ saha rūpeṇa grāhyalakṣaṇatvād gṛhyeta । na vā kevalasyāpy ālokasya darśanād anālokasya vā rūpasya kaiścit prāṇiviśeṣair iti na tayor api sahopalambhaniyamaḥ । nīlākārasaṃvedanayos tu niyama eva । na sa nānātve yuktaḥ, nīlapītavat ॥

[I,040,i]

viṣayasya vijñānahetutayopanidheḥ prāgupalambhaḥ paścāt saṃvedanasyeti cet,
	apratyakṣopalambhasya nārthadṛṣṭiḥ prasidhyati // <1.54>
<I,041>
na hi viṣayasattayā viṣayopalambhaḥ, kiṃ tarhi tadupalambhasattayā । sā cāprāmāṇikā na sattānibandhanān vyavahārān anuruṇaddhi । tadaprasiddhau viṣayasyāpy aprasiddhir ity astaṅgataṃ viśvaṃ syāt । sato 'py asiddhau sattāvyavahārāyogyatvāt । tasmān nānupalabhamānaḥ kasyacit saṃvedanaṃ vedayate nāma kiñcit ॥

[I,041,i]

upalabhyate saṃvedanam anyeneti cet, sa tāvad viṣayaḥ svopalambhakāle na siddhiḥ siddher asiddheḥ, anyopalambhakāle tu siddha ity upalambhe 'pi tadā na siddho 'nyadā viparyaye siddha iti suvyāhṛtam । anyenāpi saṃvedanopalambhe so 'py asiddhaḥ saṃvedanaṃ na sādhayatīty upalambhāntarānugamaḥ । tan na tāvad ayaṃ puruṣaḥ kaścid arthaṃ pratyety upalambhaniṣṭhāṃ pratīkṣamāṇaḥ, ekāsiddhau sarvāsiddheḥ । na copalambhānām utpattiniṣṭhety andhamūkaṃ jagat syāt । kvacin niṣṭhāyāṃ sa svayam ātmānaṃ viṣayākāraṃ ca yugapad upalabhata iti tadanye 'pi tathā syuḥ, viśeṣahetvabhāvāt । <I,042> tat siddhaḥ sahopalambhaniyamaḥ, ekavyāpāre kramāyogāt, tasyāviśeṣāt ॥

[I,042,i]

saṃvedanam ity api tasya tādātmyāt tathāprathanam, na tadanyasya kasyacid ātmasaṃvedanavat । tato 'pi na tadarthāntare yuktam । anarthāntaratve tu nīlāder anubhavāt tadātmabhūtaḥ prakāśate tatheti nīlādyanubhavaḥ syāt ॥

[I,042,ii]

sa ca tādātmyāt tathāprakāśamāno 'pi svaparātmanoḥ prakāśakaḥ syāt, prakāśavat । tasmād grāhakākāraḥ svasaṃvidaḥ sādhanam iṣṭam, tato 'syās tadbhāvavyavasthāpanāt ॥

[I,042,iii]

	tatrātmaviṣaye māne yathā rāgādivedanam /
	iyaṃ sarvatra saṃyojyā mānameyaphalasthitiḥ // <1.55>
	tatrāpy anubhavātmatvāt te yogyāḥ svātmasaṃvidi /
	iti sā yogyatā mānam ātmā meyaḥ phalaṃ svavit // <1.56>
	grāhakākārasaṅkhyātā paricchedātmatātmani /
<I,043>
	sā yogyateti ca proktaṃ pramāṇaṃ svātmavedanam // <1.57>
ity antaraślokāḥ ॥

[I,043,i]

	bāhye 'py arthe tato 'bhedo bhāsamānārthatadvidoḥ /

[I,043,ii]

saty api bāhye 'rthe sahopalambhavedanābhyāṃ bhāsamānasya nīlādes tatsaṃvidaś cāvivekaḥ siddhaḥ ॥

[I,043,iii]

	dvairūpyaṃ taddhiyaḥ	...

[I,043,iv]

viṣayajñānarūpābhyām ato dvirūpā buddhiḥ siddhā bhavati । yadi bhāsamāno viṣayākāro buddher abhinnaḥ, tato bhinnam astīti kutaḥ ॥

[I,043,v]

							... bāhyasiddhiḥ syād vyatirekataḥ // <1.58>

[I,043,vi]

satsu samārtheṣu anyeṣu hetuṣu jñānakāryāniṣpattiḥ kāraṇāntaravaikalyaṃ sūcayati । sa bāhyo 'rthaḥ syāt, yady atra kaścid upādānaviśeṣābhāvakṛtaṃ kāryavyatirekaṃ na brūyāt । so 'pi kathaṃ sarvajñānānāṃ viṣayaṃ vyatirecayan nupaplavetarayoḥ pramāṇetaratāṃ brūyāt, viśeṣābhāvāt । upaplavavāsanāvisandhidoṣād aprabuddhasyāpy anāśvāsikaṃ vyavahāram <I,044> utpaśyan nekam apramāṇam ācakṣīta, aparam āsaṃsāram aviśliṣṭānubandhaṃ dṛḍhavāsanatvād iha vyavahārāvisaṃvādāpekṣayā pramāṇam । sāṃvyavahārikasya caitat pramāṇasya rūpam uktam, atrāpi pare mūḍhā visaṃvādayanti lokam iti । cintāmayīm eva tu prajñām anuśīlayanto vibhramavivekanirmalam anapāyi pāramarthikapramāṇam abhimukhīkurvanti । tad api leśataḥ sūcitam eveti ॥

<॥ pramāṇaviniścaye pratyakṣaparicchedaḥ prathamaḥ>

<I,045>

{2}

<§ svārthānumānaparicchedaḥ>

[I,045,i]

	anumānaṃ dvidhā ...
svārthaṃ parārthaṃ ca ॥

[I,045,ii]

jñānābhidhānarūpatvān na prāprapratipattinibandhane । apṛthagvacanaṃ śabdasya viśeṣābhāvād iti cet, na, pravṛttibhedāt । artho hi liṅginaṃ gamayati, talliṅgaṃ śabda iti । na, lakṣaṇāntarasyāvācyatvāt । yat kvacid adṛṣṭam, tasya yatra pratibandhas tadvidas tasya tadgamakaṃ tatreti vastugatiḥ । tatra gamakalakṣaṇavidhānena pratipipādayiṣorvacanānukramadarśanaṃ kṛtam eva, anyathābhidhāne gamakadharmādyotanāt । na hi ye yathā yam arthaṃ vidanti vacanajñāḥ, te tatpratipādane punarupadeśāntaram apekṣante । satyam etat, tathāpi bālavyutpattinimitto 'yam ārambhaḥ । yathāvastupratipadyamānā api taddharmāvyāptivyatirekābhyāṃ nigadanto dṛṣṭāḥ, avinābhāvāvacanād upamānasādhyatadāvṛttivacanānāṃ ca prayogāt ॥

<I,046>

[I,046,i]

tatra
					... svārthaṃ trirūpāl liṅgato 'rthadṛk /
trilakṣaṇāl liṅgād yad anumeye 'rthe jñānam, tat svārtham anumānam ॥

[I,046,ii]

pratyakṣavad asya phalavikalpo vijñeyaḥ ॥

[I,046,iii]

tad etad
	atasmiṃs tadgrahād bhrāntir api sambandhataḥ pramā // <2.1>
svapratibhāse 'narthe 'rthādhyavasāyena pravartanād bhrāntir apy arthasambandhena tadavyabhicārāt pramāṇam । na hi svabhāvaḥ kāryaṃ vā bhāvakāraṇavyatireke bhavataḥ, abhedād ātmaniṣpatteś ca । tathā tayor abhāve tajjaṃ jñānaṃ tatprabhavā vā bhāvakāraṇapratipattiḥ । tathā sati dṛśye vastuny avikalatadanyakāraṇasya darśanasya vrāvṛttiḥ । <I,047> na ca sa eva pratibhāso 'rtho yuktaḥ, tasya punaḥ pratyakṣenānyathā darśanāt ॥

[I,047,i]

	yo hi bhāvo yathābhūtaḥ sa tādṛgliṅgacetasaḥ /
	hetus tajjā tathābhūte tasmād vastuni liṅgidhīḥ // <2.2>
	liṅgaliṅgidhiyor evaṃ pāramparyeṇa vastuni /
	pratibandhāt tadābhāsaśūnyayor apy avañcanam // <2.3>
	tasyās tadrūpaśūnyāyās tadrūpādhyavasāyataḥ /
	tadrūpāvañcakatve 'pi kṛtā bhrāntivyavasthitiḥ // <2.4>
	maṇipradīpaprabhayor maṇibuddhyābhidhāvataḥ /
	mithyājñānāviśeṣe 'pi viśeṣo 'rthakriyāṃ prati // <2.5>
	yathā tathāyathārthatve 'py anumānatadābhayoḥ /
	arthakriyānurodhena pramāṇatvaṃ vyavasthitam // <2.6>
iti saṅgrahaślokāḥ ॥

<I,048>

[I,048,i]

ata eva
	pramāṇyaṃ vastuviṣayaṃ dvayoḥ	...
pratyakṣānumānayoḥ, arthakriyāyogyaviṣayatvād vicārasya । sukhaduḥkhasādhane jñātvā yathārhaṃ pratipitsavo hi kiñcit parīkṣante prekṣāpūrvakāriṇaḥ, na vyasanitayā । na cānumānapratibhāsa evārthasādhanam, niruddhe 'py arthasādhane vastuni tasyānirodhāt tataś ca kasyacid arthasyāsiddheḥ । ata eva sad api sāmānyaṃ nārthaḥ । tasmād vasturūpāvisaṃvādanam evāsyāpi pramāṇyam, tatpratibaddhavastuliṅgāpekṣaṇāc ca ॥

[I,048,ii]

ācāryaḥ punar
									... arthabhidāṃ jagau /
	pratibhāsasya bhinnatvād ekasmiṃs tadayogataḥ // <2.7>
na hy ekasya tāv anyonyavilakṣaṇāv ākārau yujyete । tadālambanaviṣayabhedāt pramāṇayor viṣayabhedam āha, na pramāṇavyāpāraviṣayabhedāt । bheda ity apy asyābhedapratiṣedha eva draṣṭavyaḥ, na nānāviṣayatā, anumānavikalpasya nirviṣayatvāt, tatpratibhāsasya svaviṣayasammatānvayavyatirekānanuvidhānāt pratyakṣavat sāmānyasya ca vastuno 'nyatvenāvācyatvāt ॥

<I,049>

[I,049,i]

katham idānīṃ dvayor api prāmāṇyasya vastuviṣayatve sāmānyasya pratipattir liṅgād anyataḥ svalakṣaṇasyety āha —
	atadrūpaparāvṛttavastumātraprasādhanāt /
	sāmānyaviṣayaṃ proktaṃ liṅgaṃ bhedāpratiṣṭhiteḥ // <2.8>
yatprayojanā hy arthā jñātum iṣṭāḥ, tadviparyayavyatirekiṇo 'rthamātrasyopanidhāyakaṃ liṅgam iti sāmānyaviṣayaṃ proktam, tato bhedāpratiṣṭhānāt, na vastusattāviprakarṣāt, liṅgapratipatter api tathārūpatvād anvayāpekṣaṇāc ca । itarat punar bhedāntaravimarśavivekena pratiṣṭhitenaiva rūpeṇākriyata iti svalakṣaṇaviṣayam, aparasmād arthapratipatteḥ । na tv evaṃ parāṅgāt pratītiḥ, tasyāsāmarthyāt । arthāvisaṃvādas tu dvayor api tulya iti vastuviṣyaṃ prāmāṇyam ॥

<I,050>

[I,050,i]

tat punas trairūpyam
	anumeye 'tha tattulye sadbhāvo nāstitāsati /
	niścitā	... <2.9ac'>
anumeyo 'tra jijñāsitaviśeṣo dharmī । tatra darśanaṃ pratyakṣato 'numānato vā । tathā tattulya eva ca ॥

[I,050,ii]

dharmiviśiṣṭasyānyatra vṛttivirodho 'viśeṣaṇe vā nānumeyadharmateti cet, na, ayogavyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt ॥

[I,050,iii]

	ayogaṃ yogam aparair atyantāyogam eva ca /
	vyavacchinatti dharmasya nipāto vyatirecakaḥ // <2.10>
	viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyābhyāṃ kriyayā ca sahoditaḥ /
	vivakṣāto 'prayoge 'pi tasyārtho 'yaṃ pratīyate // <2.11>
	vyavacchedaphalaṃ vākyaṃ yataś caitro dhanurdharaḥ /
	pārtho dhanurdharo nīlaṃ sarojam iti vā yathā // <2.12>
	pratiyogivyavacchedas tatrāpy artheṣu gamyate /
	tathā prasiddheḥ sāmarthyād vivakṣānugamād dhvaneḥ // <2.13>
<I,051>
	tadayogavyavacchedād dharmī dharmaviśeṣaṇam /
	tadviśiṣṭatayā dharmo na niranvayadoṣabhāk // <2.14>
ity antaraślokāḥ ॥

[I,051,i]

anyayogavyavacchedena ca viśeṣaṇa ekasya tadbhāve 'nyasyātattvaṃ syād viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoginaś ca nipātasyāviśeṣaḥ । etena sādhyadharme 'pi viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāva unneyaḥ । tena saty api viśeṣaṇe nānanvayaḥ । tathā sāmānyaṃ ca sādhyam । na ca siddhasādhanam, tadayogavyavacchedasyāsiddheḥ ॥

[I,051,ii]

tattulya evety avadhāraṇād dharmiṇy avṛttir iti cet, na, anyaniṣedhārthatvāt । tatra vṛttau labdhāyāṃ samuccīyamānāvadhāraṇam anyad vyavacchinnatti, 
	“naraṃ ca nārāyaṇam eva cādasu svataḥ sutau dvau janayāṃ babhūva //”
iti yathā ॥

<I,052>

[I,052,i]

tasya sādhyasajātīyavṛttino liṅgasyāsati nāstitā tṛtīyaṃ rūpam । sā ca niścitā । ante vacanān niścitatvaṃ triṣv api rūpeṣu draṣṭavyam । arthāntarasvabhāvayoḥ prabhavatanmātrānubandhasiddhau kāraṇabhāvānupalabdhyā grāhyaviṣayayā siddhā, netarayeti yāvat । anupalabdhāv api viparyaye pratyakṣavṛttir vyatirekaniścayaḥ ॥

[I,052,ii]

tattulya evāstīti vyatireke siddhe 'sati nāstitābhidhānam asaty eva nāstitā nānyatra na viruddha iti niyamārtham ity āha । tatrāsambhavād eva nānyadharmavṛttiniṣedhāśaṅkā । viruddhaniṣedhe 'pi tatraiva niṣedhe doṣaḥ syāt । na ca tattulya eva vṛttir ity atattulyo viruddha eva, yena tata eva vyatirekād agnir auṣṇyaṃ na gamayet । kiṃ tarhi tattulyavyatireko 'pi । tenāyam adoṣa ity avācyam eva tṛtīyaṃ rūpaṃ syāt । prayogadarśanārthatvād adoṣaḥ — anvayavyatirekayor niścitavyāptikam ekam api rūpaṃ prayuktam arthāpattyā dvitīyaṃ gamayatīti । ata ekasya prayogaḥ syād iti ॥

<I,053>

[I,053,i]

nanu śrāvaṇatvaṃ vyatireky apy agamakam । na, avyatirekāt । na hi śrāvaṇatvaṃ kutaścid vyaticiyate, sandehasādhanāt । vyatirekiṇaś ca sandehāyogāt kṛtakatvādivānityatve, vastudharmasya sarvavastuno vyāvṛttivirodhāt । vṛttiśaṅkayaiva tataḥ saṃśayaḥ । anvayas tu na dṛṣṭa iti vyatirekī kathyate । na caivaṃvidho vyatireko gamakaḥ । yas tu gamakaḥ, sa saṃvarṇita eva । sa ca nāsaty anvaye śakyo darśayitum, tadbhāvahetubhāvayor darśanasādhanatvāt ॥

[I,053,ii]

dvirūpaṃ tarhi liṅgam । na, anvayavyatirekayoḥ pṛthagrūpatvāt । te tv ekenāpi vākyena śakye darśayitum iti prayogasamāsa ucyate na rūpasamāsaḥ । tathā hy āha — arthāpattyā vānyatareṇobhayapradarśanād iti ॥

[I,053,iii]

nāsati nāstitāsiddhiḥ, asato hy adhikaraṇatvādyayogād ity aparaḥ । paśavo 'pi hi tāvad yad ayuktaṃ paśyanti, na tadaiva tad ācaranti । so 'yaṃ paśor api paśuḥ । mahato 'pi mahīyaso yad avamanyata iti kim anyadanātmajñatāyāḥ । <I,054> so 'yaṃ tair evārthavyatirekasamāveśibhiḥ padair asatsu vyavahārāyogaṃ darśayan paraṃ pratiruṇaddhīti vyaktam etadrājaśāsanam । na ca svayam abrūvan paraṃ bodhayitum īśo brūvan vā doṣam imaṃ parihartum । asati hetor apratiṣedhe vidhiḥ prāptaḥ, abhāvavyatirekalakṣaṇatvād asya । saiva tāvad asato na nivṛttir iti nivṛtter nivṛttiḥ katham iṣṭā ॥

[I,054,i]

	nivṛttyabhāvas tu vidhir vastubhāvo 'sato 'pi san /
	vastvabhāvas tu nāstīti paśya vāndhyavijṛmbhitam // <2.15>
	nivṛttir yadi tasmin na hetor vṛttiḥ kim iṣyate /
	sāpi na pratiṣedho 'yaṃ nivṛttiḥ kiṃ niṣidhyate // <2.16>
	vidhānaṃ pratiṣedhaṃ ca muktvā śabdo 'sti nāparaḥ /
	vyavahāraḥ sa cāsatsu neti prāptātra mūkatā // <2.17>
	satāṃ ca na niṣedho 'sti so 'satsu ca na vartate /
	jagaty anena nyāyena nañarthaḥ pralayaṃ gataḥ // <2.18>
<I,055>
	deśakālaniṣedhaś ced yathāsti sa niṣidhyate /
	na tathā na yathā so 'sti tathāpi na niṣidhyate // <2.19>
	tasmād āśritya śabdāthaṃ bhāvābhāvasamāśrayam /
	abāhyāśrayam atreṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ vidhiniṣedhanam // <2.20>
	tābhyāṃ sa dharmī sambaddhaḥ khyātyabhāve 'pi tādṛśaḥ /
	śabdapravṛtter astīti so 'pīṣṭo vyavahārabhāk // <2.21>
	anyathā syāt padārthānāṃ vidhānapratiṣedhane /
	ekadharmasya sarvātmavidhānapratiṣedhanam // <2.22>
	anānātmatayā bhede nānāvidhiniṣedhavat /
	ekadharmiṇyasaṃhāro vidhānapratiṣedhayoḥ // <2.23>
	ekaṃ dharmiṇam uddiśya nānādharmasamāśrayam /
	vidhāv ekasya tadbhājam ivānyeṣām upekṣakam // <2.24>
	niṣedhe tadviviktam ca tadanyeṣām apekṣakam /
	vyavahāram asatyārthaṃ prakalpayati dhīr yathā // <2.25>
	taṃ tathaivāvikalpyārthabhedāśrayam upāgatāḥ /
	anādivāsanodbhūtaṃ bādhante 'rthaṃ na laukikam // <2.26>
	tatphalo 'tatphalaś cārtho bhinna ekas tatas tataḥ /
	tais tair upaplavair nītasañcayāpacayair iva // <2.27>
<I,056>
	atadvān api sambandhāt kutaścid upanīyate /
	dṛṣṭiṃ bhedāśrayais te 'pi tasmād ajñātaviplavāḥ // <2.28>
ity antaraślokāḥ ॥

[I,056,i]

etallakṣaṇā
			... 'nupalambhātmakāryākhyā hetavas trayaḥ // <2.9c'd>
eva । anupalabdhiḥ svabhāvaḥ kāryaṃ ceti trīṇy eva liṅgāni । yathā pradeśaviśeṣe kvacin na ghaṭa upalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptasyānupalabdheḥ, yadi hi syāt, upalabhyasattva eva syān nānyatheti, vṛkṣo 'yaṃ śiṃśapātvāt, agnir atra dhūmāt । atra dvau vastusādhanāv ekaḥ pratiṣedhahetuḥ ॥

[I,056,ii]

svabhāvapratibandhe hi saty artho 'rthaṃ na vyabhicarati । sa ca tadātmatvāt ॥

[I,056,iii]

tadātmatve sādhyasādhanabhedābhāva iti cet, na, dharmabhedaparikalpanāt । tathā cāha — sarva evāyam anumānānumeyavyavahāro buddhyārūḍhena <I,057> dharmadharminyāyeneti । dharmadharmitayā bhedo buddhiparikalpito nārtho 'pi vikalpabhedānāṃ svatantrāṇām anarthāśrayatvāt । tatkalpitaviṣayād arthapratītāv anarthapratilambhaḥ syāt ।
	sarvabhāvāḥ svabhāvena svasvabhāvavyavasthiteḥ /
	svabhāvaparabhāvābhyāṃ yasmād vyāvṛttibhāginaḥ // <2.29>
	tasmād yato yato 'rthānāṃ vyāvṛttis tannibandhanāḥ /
	jātibhedāḥ prakalpyante tadviśeṣāvagāhinaḥ // <2.30>
	tasmād yo yena dharmeṇa viśeṣaḥ sampratīyate /
	na sa śakyas tato 'nyena tena bhinnā vyavasthitiḥ // <2.31>
ity antaraślokāḥ ॥

[I,057,i]

kāryasyāpi svabhāvapratibandhaḥ, tatsvabhāvasya tadutpatter iti ॥

[I,057,ii]

etau dvāv anumeyapratyayau sākṣādanutpatter atatpratibhāsitve 'pi tadutpattes tadavyabhicāriṇāv iti pramāṇaṃ pratyakṣavat ॥

[I,057,iii]

	asattāniścayaphalo 'nupalambhaḥ	... <2.32ab'>
<I,058>
asadvyavahārapravartanaphalo 'nupalambhas tadavyabhicārī, siddhe vyavahāre sato viṣayasyāvyabhicārāt ॥

[I,058,i]

anupalabdher liṅgād asattāyāṃ sādhyāyām upalabdher abhāvo 'py anyayānupalabdhyā sādhyata ity anavasthānād apratipattiḥ syāt । athopalabdhyabhāvo vinānupalabdhyā syāt, tathā sattā 'bhāvo 'pi syād ity apārthikānupalabdhiḥ । athānyopalabdhyā 'nupalabdhisiddhir iti pratyakṣasiddhā nānupalabdheḥ । tathānyasattayā 'sattā kiṃ na sidhyati । yadā punar evaṃvidhānupalabdhir evāsatām asattā, tadā siddhena viṣayeṇa viṣayiṇo 'sañ jñānaśabdavyavahārān pratipadyate pratipādayati ca, viṣayapradarśanena samaye pravartanāt, yathā — gaur ayaṃ sāsnādisamudāyātmakatvād iti । tathā ca dṛṣṭāntāsiddhicodanāpi prativyūḍhā, viṣayapratipattāv apy apratipannaviṣayiṇāṃ darśanāt ॥

[I,058,ii]

bhāvavyatireko hy abhāvaḥ, anupalabdhir upalabdheḥ । sā katham asattā bhāvasya, upalambhanivṛttyā vā katham abhāvaḥ, kāryavyatireke 'pi kāraṇābhāvāsiddheḥ । <I,059> upalambhanibandhanā hi tādṛśāṃ sattāprajñaptir upalabdhiyogyasvabhāvasyānyahetusākalye tadavyabhicārāc copalambhaḥ sattocyate । sāmagrīpariṇām āpekṣatvāt syād vyabhicāro 'pīti, na, kāryakāle 'bhāvapratipatteḥ, anyopalambhe tadanupalambhasiddheḥ । prabhāvavato 'dhiṣṭhānāt sato 'py anupalabdhir iti, na, viṣayendriyayor ekasya dvayor vānanyathātve 'yogād adhiṣṭhānasya । tatsaṃskāre tu syād anupalambhaḥ । tadāpi tathāvidhendriyagrāhyābhāvo 'sty eva । tasmāj jñānaṃ tadyogyatā vāsya sattā, tadvyatireko 'nupalabdhir asattā । tayā viṣayī sādhyate । eteneha kāraṇasya kāryavyabhicāraḥ pratyuktaḥ । atrāpy anupalabdhyā tannimittaḥ siddho vyavahāro 'pi tannimittasattā sādhyate, anyanaimittikavat ॥

[I,059,i]

saiva tāvad anupalabdhiḥ kathaṃ siddheti cet, etad uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ ॥

[I,059,ii]

sa cāyam anupalmbhaś
<I,060>
									... caturvidhaḥ // <2.32b'>
pravṛttibhedāt । yāvān kaścit pratiṣedhaḥ sa sarvo 'nupalabdheḥ । tathā hi sa dividhā kriyate, kasyacid vidhinā pratiṣedhena vā ॥

[I,060,i]

vidhau viruddho vā vidhīyetāviruddho vā । aviruddhasyāpi sahabhāvavirodhābhāvād apratiṣedho viruddhasyāpy anupalabdhim antareṇa virodhāpratipattiḥ । tathā hy aparyantakāraṇasya bhavato 'nyabhāve 'bhāvād virodhagatiḥ । sa cānupalabdheḥ । anyonyavyatirekasthitalakṣaṇatā vā virodho nityāniyatvavat । tatrāpy ekopalabdhyānyānupalabdhir evocyate, anyathā hy aniṣiddhopalabdher abhāvāsiddeḥ ॥

[I,060,ii]

ekaniṣedhenānyābhāvasādhane siddhaivānupalabdhiḥ, niṣedhasyānupalabdhirūpatvāt । tatrāpy arthāntaraniṣedhe sādhye kāryakāraṇayor anubhayasy vā niṣedho hetuḥ । tatrāpy anubhayasyāpratibandhāt tadabhāve 'nyābhāvo na yuktaḥ ॥

<I,061>

[I,061,i]

kāryānupalabdhāv pai nāvaśyaṃ kāraṇāni tadvanti bhavantīti kutas tadabhāvaḥ । śaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ nāśaktam । na ca śaktiḥ kenacit pratibandhuṃ śakyate, antyāvasthāyāṃ pariṇāmābhāvāt kṣaṇasyāvivekāt । kāryotpattiviguṇotpādanalakṣaṇatvāt pratibadhasya, anyathā 'kiñcitkarasyāpratibandhāt । bhavaty eva tādṛśasya kāraṇasya kāryavivekād abhāvagatiḥ, yathā — nehāpratibaddhasāmarthyāni dhūmakāraṇāni santi dhūmābhāvād iti । tatkāryaṃ hetuvyāptyavyatirekāt tatsvabhāvāviśiṣṭam iti tadanupalambhaḥ svabhāvānupalambha evoktaḥ । tathā tadviruddhopalambhaḥ, yathā — nehāpratibaddhasāmarthyāni śītakāraṇāni santy agner iti kāraṇadravyasāmānyam abhipretya kāryānupalmbho 'gamaka ucyate, yathā — nāgnir atra dhūmābhāvād iti . kāraṇānupalabdhir abhāvaṃ gamayati । svabhāvānupalabdhis tu svayam asattaiva । tatra kevalaṃ viṣayī sādhyate 'bhāvo vā tadbhāvavyāpinaḥ kāryasyābhāvena । yadāpi vyāpakadharmānupalabdhyā vyāpyābhāvam āha, tadāpy abhāva eva ॥

<I,062>

[I,062,i]

tad evaṃ vidhipratiṣedhābhyāṃ kasyacin niṣedhe sarvagamakānām anupalabdhī rūpam । nāparaḥ partiṣedhahetuḥ ॥

[I,062,ii]

seyaṃ pratiṣedhaviṣayānupalabdhiḥ prayogabhedena caturdhā bhvati । viruddhasiddhyā, yathā — na śītasparśo 'trāgner iti । etena vyāpakaviruddhasiddhir uktā veditavyā, yathā — na tuṣārasparśo 'trāgner iti । viruddhakāryasiddhyā, yathā — na śītasparśo 'tra dhūmād iti । hetvasiddhyā, yathā — na dhūmo 'trānagner iti । svabhāvāsiddhyā, yathā — nātra dhūmo 'nupalabdher iti । etena vyāpakasvabhāvāsiddhir uktā veditavyā, yathā — nātra śiṃśapā vṛkṣābhāvād iti । sarvatra cāsyām abhāvavyavahārasādhanyām anupalabdhau dṛśyātmanām eva teṣāṃ tadviruddhānāṃ ca sannihitānyopalambhakāraṇād asiddhiḥ siddhiś ca veditavyā, anyeṣāṃ hetuphalabhāvābhāvavirodhāsiddheḥ ॥

<I,063>

[I,063,i]

	dṛśyasya darśanābhāvakāraṇāsambhave sati /
	bhāvasyānupalabdhasya bhāvābhāvaḥ pratīyate // <2.33>
iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ ॥

[I,063,ii]

yadi viruddhakāryopalabdhyāpy abhāvasiddhiḥ, tatkāraṇopalabdhyā kiṃ na sidhyati । na, tadvyabhicārāt, yathā — na śītasparśo 'tra kāṣṭhād iti । kāraṇānāṃ kāryārambhāniyamān nāvaśyaṃ śītabādhako 'gniḥ, yatas tadabhāvo gamyeta । antyasyāvasthāviśeṣasyāvyabhicāra iti cet, na, tataḥ kāryotpatter akṣepāt । ā antyalakṣaṇotpatteḥ pratibadhaḥ sambhāvyate । antyalakṣaṇe 'pratibandhaḥ । talliṅgadarśanāt sambandhasmṛtyapekṣiṇo 'numeyapratipattau taduptpatteḥ prāk kāryam evāntyakṣaṇānantaratvād utpannaṃ pratyakṣībhavati । na cāpratyakṣe kārye kāraṇabhāvagatiḥ, yataḥ kāranāt tat pratīyeta । tasmān na kāraṇāt kāryasiddhiḥ ॥

[I,063,iii]

nimittayoḥ punar virodhe gamikaiva, yathā — nāsya romaharṣādiviśeṣāḥ santi sannihitadahanaviśeṣaviruddhasya <I,064> paritāpasya hetor agneḥ śītena virodhāc chītavicchede tatkāryasyāpy abhāva iti । etena tatkāryād api tadviruddhakāryābhāvagatir uktā veditavyā, yathā romaharṣādiviśeṣayuktapuruṣavān ayaṃ pradeśo dhūmād iti । itthaṃ ca hetvasiddhyaiva tadviruddhasiddhiḥ prāg eva nirdiṣṭetīyaṃ prayogabhedād daśāvidhānupalabdhiḥ ॥

[I,064,i]

	itthaṃ viruddhakārye 'pi deśakālādyapekṣaṇam /
	anyathā vyabhicāri syād bhasmevāśītasādhane // <2.34>
ity antaraślokaḥ ॥

[I,064,ii]

nāsattāniścayo viprakarṣiṇām । trividhā hi viprakarṣiṇo deśakālasvabhāvaviprakarṣair na teṣv anupalambho 'bhāvaṃ gamayati ॥

[I,064,iii]

sad avaśyaṃ kenacid upalabhyate vyatītāsamprāptopalambhaṃ vā । tat kathaṃ nānupalambhād abhāvaḥ । na, sarvopalambhanivṛtter atrāliṅgatvāt, ātmaparayor apratipatteḥ । tasmād ayam ātmopalambhanivṛttim eva pramāṇayan pratikṣipati । sā vipakṛṣṭeṣv apy asti, na ca te na santy eva ॥

<I,065>

[I,065,i]

tatrāpi sati pratyakṣānumānāgamānām ekasya vṛttir iti cet, na, śāstrasya kvacid anadhikārāt । śāstraṃ hi pravartamānaṃ puruṣārthasādhanaṃ kvacid upāyam āśritya pravartate । anyathāsambaddhapralāpasyāprāmāṇyāt । tatra ca prakaraṇe bahavo 'rthā nāvaśyaṃ nirdeśyāḥ, yathā pratyātmaniyatāḥ kāścana puruṣāṇāṃ cetovṛttayo 'niyatanimittabhāvinyo deśakālavyavahitā vā prakaraṇānupayogino dravyaviśeṣāḥ । na tān śāstraṃ viṣayīkaroti । na ca teṣāṃ tathāviprakṛṣṭānāṃ svasāmarthyopadhānāj jñānotpādanaśaktiḥ । na cāvaśyam eṣāṃ kāryopalambho yenānumīyeran । na ca te pramāṇatrayanivṛttāv api na santīti śakyante vyavasātum ॥

[I,065,ii]

yo 'pi jñāpakābhāvād atīndriyaḥ partikṣipyate 'rthaḥ svabhāvaviśeṣo vā, yathā — nāsti virakaṃ ceto devatāviśeṣo vā, nāsti dānahiṃsādiviraticetanānām abhyupadayahetuteti । pratyakṣe 'py arthe phalasyānantaryābhāvād atatphalasādharmyāt tadviparyāsa eṣaḥ । vyavahitānām api hi hetoḥ phalānām utpattirdarśanān mūṣikālarkaviṣavikāravat । tadbhāvavirodhābhāvād atrānupalabdhimātram apramāṇam । bhāve kiṃ pramāṇam iti cet, ata eva saṃśayo 'stu, bhaved vā pramāṇam ity apratikṣepaḥ । tad atra keṣāñcit <I,066> svabhāvānām arthānāṃ vā darśanapāṭavābhāvāt kāraṇānāṃ kāryotpādananiyamābhāvāc ca bhavej jñāpakāsiddhiḥ । neyatā tadabhāvaḥ । punaḥ paryāyeṇa keṣāñcid abhivyakteḥ ॥

[I,066,i]

nāpi śabdā yathābhāvaṃ vartante, yatas tebhyo 'rthaprakṛtir niścīyeta । te hi vaktur vivakṣāvṛttaya iti tannāntarīyakās tām eva gamayeyuḥ । na ca puruṣecchāḥ sarvā yathārthabhāvinyaḥ । na ca tadapratibaddhasvabhāvo bhāvo 'nyaṃ gamayati ॥

[I,066,ii]

yathārthadarśanādiguṇayuktaḥ puruṣa āptaḥ, tatpraṇīta āgamo 'visamvādīti cet,
	iṣṭo 'yam arthaḥ śakyeta jñātuṃ so 'tiśayo yadi // <2.32cd>

[I,066,iii]

sarva evāgamam anāgamaṃ vā pravṛttikāmo 'nveṣate prekṣāpūrvakārī, na vyasanena । tasya puruṣaparīkṣayā pravṛttāv apravṛttir eva. tathābhūtasya jñātum aśakyatvāt । nāniṣṭeḥ, tādṛśām avitathābhidhānāt । tathā hi nānyaguṇadoṣaniścaye liṅgam asti । te hi cetodharmatvenātīndriyatvāt <I,067> svaprabhavakāyavāgvyavahārānumeyāḥ syuḥ । vyavahārāś ca prāyaśo buddhipūrvam anyathāpi kartuṃ śakyante, puruṣecchāvṛttitvāt teṣāṃ ca citrābhisandhitvāt । tad ayaṃ liṅgasaṅkarāt katham aniścinvan pratipadyeta ॥

[I,067,i]

mā bhūt puruṣāśrayaṃ vacanam āgamaḥ, praṇetur duranvayatvāt । apauruṣeyam avitathaṃ syāt । na, tasyāyogād arthābhidhāne puruṣopadeśāpekṣatvāc ca । upalambhayogyāyogyātmanoḥ prāptiparityāgayoḥ svabhāvāntarotpattihānināntarīyakatvāt, nityaṃ tadātmatāyāṃ kadācid upalambhānupalambhābhāvaprasaṅgāt । nāpi parāpekṣā, tasya tatrākiñcitkaratvāt, anyakaraṇe tasyeti sambandhāyogāt । upakārasya tatsambandhe kaḥ sambandho 'nupakāryopakārakayoḥ । ādhārādheyabhāvaś cet, so 'pi tadātmānupakāre na sidhyati । parātmani tulyaḥ paryanuyogo 'navasthā ca । janyajanakabhāve so 'napekṣasya nityaṃ syāt । apekṣāyāṃ ca pūrvavat prasaṅgaḥ । tasmāt kādācitkaḥ śabdasyopalambhayogya ātmā, sa ca <I,068> puruṣavyāpārānvavyatirekānuvidhāyī pauruṣeyaḥ । anyathāpi nāntarīyakatābhavān na parātmanaḥ pratipattir arthasya ॥

[I,068,i]

na hi sattā śabdasyārthaviśeṣe pratibaddhā, tasyāḥ sarvatrāviśeṣāt । indriyaviṣayavat parasparayogyatā niyāmiketi cet, na, tatrāpy ekapratiniyamasya tajjanmalakṣaṇatvāt tadupakṛtam indriyaṃ jñānaṃ janayatītya, anyathānupakāriṇo 'napekṣā syād viṣayāntaravat । tenaiva kasmād upakriyata iti cet, atra vastusvabhāvair uttaraṃ vācyam, ya evaṃ bhavanti । tathā hi na yavāṅkuraḥ śālibījād bhavati, api tu yavabījāt । evaṃ śabdānām api yady arthebhyo janma syāt, syād yogyatāniyamaḥ । tadabhāve 'syedam iti na sidhyati । nāpy arthavattā । arthebhyo jñāpanecchā, tayārthajñāpanāya prayujyanta iti tas tadvantaḥ syuḥ kāyavijñaptyādivat । atadāgamebhyo na tatra pratītir ākāśād iva ghaṭādiṣu ॥

[I,068,ii]

na vai śabdasvabhāvo niyato 'rtheṣu, yatas tadutpattiḥ । kiṃ tarhi jñāpanaśaktir ayam asyaiva pratipādaka iti । sāpi tatra pratibaddhā bhāvābhāvābhyāṃ <I,069> kāryatāṃ nātipatati, tanmātralakṣaṇatvād anyeṣv apy asyāḥ, tadyvatirame ca niyamāyogāt । śakteś cānarthāntaratvāt sa eva svabhāvaniyamaḥ । arthāntaratve tato 'rtheṣu jñānotpattir iti śabdo 'vācakaḥ syāt tasyeti sambandhaś ca na sidhyati । tasmāt sarvathā sarva eva kvacin niyamaḥ svabhāvabhūtaḥ svahetuprakṛter niyāmakasya janakatām eva dīpayati ॥

[I,069,i]

na vai nāntarīyakatayā śabdād arthapratipattiḥ, api tu yogyatayā pradīpād iva rūpe । tadbhāvābhāvayor darśanādarśanasmṛtyapekṣe hi śabdaliṅge svaviṣayaṃ pratipādayataḥ, adarśanasmṛtivipramoṣayor apratipatteḥ, sandehe sandehād bahuṣu darśane ca, ekatra draṣṭur abhāvāt, punardarśane ca bhāvāt, viśeṣāntaradṛṣṭāv anyathā prayoge viparyayāt, yathādarśanapratīter darśanaparāvṛttau cārthāntaraparigrahāt, kalimāryādiśabdānām iva mattakālātiśayavarṣopasargādiṣu dramiḍāryadeśayoḥ ॥

<I,070>

[I,070,i]

tasmād ime darśanam adarśanaṃ cāpekṣamāṇas tatsādhanam avyabhicāram eva pratipādane liṅgavad avalambante, anupadeśād apratipatter upadeśe ca śabdānām artheṣv anāvaraṇāt tad eva puruṣecchāyāḥ svātantryaṃ vyavasthāṃ vidhurayati । vistareṇa cāyam asmābhir vādaḥ pramāṇavārttike pratiṣiddha iti neha pratanyante ॥

[I,070,ii]

	svayaṃ rāgādimān nārthaṃ vetti vedasya nānyataḥ /
	na vedayati vedo 'pi vedārthasya kuto gatiḥ // <2.35>
	tenāgnihotraṃ juhuyāt svargakāma iti śrutau /
	khādecchvamāṃsam ity eṣa nārtha ity atra kā pramā // <2.36>
	prasiddho lokavādaś cet tatra ko 'tīndriyārthadṛk /
	anekārtheṣu śabdeṣu yenārtho 'yaṃ vivecitaḥ // <2.37>
	svargorvaśyādiśabdaś ca dṛṣṭo 'rūḍhārthavācakaḥ /
	śabdāntareṣu tādṛkṣu tādṛśyevāstu kalpanā // <2.38>
	aprasiddhārthayogasya tatprasiddhiprasādhane /
	nāsiddhārthaḥ svayaṃ śaktas tulyaḥ paryanuyogataḥ // <2.39>
<I,071>
	prasiddhiś ca nṛṇāṃ vādaḥ pramāṇaṃ sa ca neṣyate /
	tataś ca bhūyo 'rthagatiḥ kim etaddviṣṭakāmitam // <2.40>
	atha prasiddhim ullaṅghya kalpane kiṃ nibandhanam /
	prasiddher apramāṇatvāt tadgrahe kiṃ nibandhanam // <2.41>
	utpāditā prasiddhyaiva śaṅkā śabdārthaniścaye /
	yasmān nānārthavṛttitvaṃ śabdānāṃ tatra dṛśyate // <2.42>
	na yuktibādhā yatrāsti tadgrāhyaṃ laukikaṃ yadi /
	gṛhyate vātaputrīyaṃ kiṃ na yuktyā na bādhitam // <2.43>
	āgamārthāśrayā yuktir atyakṣeṣu na cetarā /
	tadarthasyāpratiṣṭhānād yukter atra na sambhavaḥ // <2.44>
	anyathā 'sambhavābhāvān nānāśakteḥ svayam dhvaneḥ /
	avaśyaṃ śaṅkayā bhāvyaṃ niyāmakam apaśyatām // <2.45>
	eṣa sthāṇur ayaṃ mārga iti vaktīti kaścana /
	anyaḥ svayaṃ bravīmīti tayor bhedaḥ parīkṣyatām // <2.46>
<I,072>
	sarvatra yogyasyaikārthadyotane niyatiḥ kutaḥ /
	jñātā vā 'tīndriyāḥ kena vivakṣāvacanād ṛte // <2.47>
	vivakṣā niyame hetuḥ saṅketas tatprakāśanaḥ /
	apauruṣeye sā nāsti tasya saikārthatā kutaḥ // <2.48>
	svabhāvaniyame 'nyatra na yojyeta tayā punaḥ /
	saṅketaś ca nirarthaḥ syād vyaktau ca niyamaḥ kutaḥ // <2.49>
	yatra svātantryam icchāyā niyamo nāma tatra kaḥ /
	dyotayet tena saṅketo neṣṭām evāsya yogyatām // <2.50>
ity antaraślokāḥ ॥

[I,072,i]

ekadeśāvisaṃvādanam apy āgamalakṣaṇam āhuḥ । tadvipakṣe 'darśanāmātrād avyabhicārāsiddhyāniścitārtham । nanu prayogasāmarthyād evārthānubandhaḥ siddhaḥ śabdānām, asati viṣaye 'prayogāt । yuktam etat, kiṃ tu tathā prasiddhāv apīcchāyā anivāraṇād anyathāpi loke vyavahāro dṛṣṭa iti saṃśayaḥ । tasmān nāgamasyāpi nivṛttir arthābhāvaṃ gamayati ॥

<I,073>

[I,073,i]

pratyakṣanivṛttir evānupalabdhir abhāvasādhanī, sakalakāraṇasyāsyārthasattāyām abhāvāsambhavāt । tatrārvāgdarśanasyātmapratyakṣanivṛttipramāṇayatas tadgrahaṇayogyapratiṣedho yuktaḥ, na ca sarvam evam ity apratiṣedhaḥ sarvatra ॥

[I,073,ii]

	pravṛtter buddhipūrvatvāt so 'pravṛttiphalo mataḥ /
so 'yaṃ viprakṛṣṭaviṣayaḥ pratyakṣānumānābhāvaḥ sañjñānaśabdavyavahārapratiṣedhaphalaḥ, upalabdhipūrvakatvāt teṣām ॥

[I,073,iii]

	anyaḥ pravartanaphalas tannimittasya darśanāt // <2.51cd>
pūrvakaḥ punar anupalambho 'sañjñānaśabdavyavahārapravartanaphalo 'pi, viṣayadarśanena prasiddhasya vyavahārasya sādhanāt । dvayor apy anupalabdhyoḥ svaviparyayahetvabhāvābhāvābhyāṃ sadvyavahārapratiṣedhaphalatvaṃ tulyam, ekatra saṃśayād anyatra viparyayāt । tatra dvitīyā sadvyavahāraniṣedhopayogāt pramāṇam uktā । na tu vyatirekadarśanādāv upayujyate, saṃśayāt, aniścitajñāpanāṅgād <I,074> pratīteḥ । prathamā tv atra pramāṇam, niścayaphalatvāt ॥

[I,074,i]

	tadbhāvamātrānvayini svabhāvo hetur ātmani /
tādātmyaṃ hy arthasya tanmātrānurodhiny eva, nānyāyatte, tadbhāve 'bhūtasya paścāt tādātmyavirodhāt kāraṇānāṃ ca kāryavyabhicārāt । tasmāt tadbhāvamātrānubandhinaṃ evātmanaḥ svabhāvo gamakaḥ ॥

[I,074,ii]

sa cāyaṃ hetutvenopādīyamāna
	upādhyapekṣaḥ śuddho vā nāśe kāryatvasattvavat // <2.52cd>
upādīyate । apekṣitaparavyāpāro hi svabhāvaniṣpattau bhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ । teneyaṃ kṛtakaśrutiḥ svabhāvābhidhāyiny api paropādhim enam ākṣipati । etena pratyayabhedabheditvādayo 'pi vyākhyātāḥ । evam upādhibhedāpekṣaḥ kvacit svabhāvo hetur ucyate, kvacid anapekṣo yathā 'nityatva eva sattvam, <I,075> kvacit svabhāvabhūtadharmabhedaprigraheṇa yathā tatraivotpattiḥ । anayā diśā 'nye 'pi svabhāvahetupravibhāgā draṣṭavyāḥ ॥

[I,075,i]

tasya ca svabhāvasya svena sādhyadharmeṇa vyāptir yadi pramāṇena niścīyate, tadā gamakaḥ, aniścitāyāṃ tu vyāptau dharmisamāśraye vā tatsvabhāvatayā gamakasyāgamakatvāt । na hi prakāśatayā prakāśayan pradīpas tadrūpāpratipattau svām arthakriyāṃ karoti । tasmān niścito vyāpyo gamako vyāpako gamyaḥ । tasya vyāpyasyāyaṃ nivartako vyāpakadharmaḥ svayaṃ nivartamānaḥ । evaṃ hy ayam asya vyāpakaḥ siddho bhavati, yady asyābhāve na bhavet । tad anena dvividhasyāpi hetur gamyagamakatālakṣaṇam uktaṃ veditavyam ॥

[I,075,ii]

dvividho hi hetuḥprayogataḥ sādharmyavān vaidharmyavāṃś ca । nānayor vastutaḥ kaścid bhedo 'nyatra prayogabhedāt । taddarśanāt svayam api pratipattau tathā syād iti svārthe 'py anumāne vibhajyocyate । sādharmyeṇāpi hi <I,076> prayoge 'rthād vaidharmyagatiḥ, asati tasmin sādhyena hetor anvayābhāvāt । tathā vaidharmyeṇāpy anvayagatiḥ, asati tasmin sādhyābhāve hetvabhāvasya sandehād iti vakṣyāmaḥ tau punar hetū yat kiñcit kṛtakaṃ tat sarvam anityam, yathā ghaṭādayaḥ, śabdaś ca kṛtaka ity anvayī । sāmarthyād evātrānityaḥ śabda iti bhāvaḥ । tasmān nāvaśyaṃ pakṣanirdeśaḥ kartavyaḥ । vyatireky api nānityatvābhāve kṛtakatvaṃ bhavati, śabdaś ca kṛtaka iti । siddhatatsvabhāvatayā tadabhāve na bhavataḥ kṛtakatvasya śabde ca bhāvakhyātau tadātmanaḥ sato bhāva iti sāmarthyāt tatsiddher nānumeyavacanam । anvayas tv arthāpattyā siddhaḥ । na hy atadātmaniyatasya tannivṛttyā nivṛttiḥ । tasmān niyamaṃ prasādhya nivṛttir vaktavyā ॥

[I,076,i]

katham idānīṃ kṛtako 'vaśyam anitya iti pratyetavyaḥ, yenaivam ucyate । yasmād
	ahetutvād vināśasya svabhāvād anubandhitā /
na hi bhāvā vinaśyantas tadbhāve hetum apekṣante, svahetor eva naśvarāṇāṃ <I,077> bhāvāt । tasmād yaḥ kaścit kṛtakaḥ sa prakṛtyaiva naśvaraḥ । tathā hi
	sāpekṣāṇāṃ hi dharmāṇāṃ nāvaśyambhāvitekṣyate // <2.53>
nirapekṣo bhāvo vināśe । sāpekṣatve hi ghaṭādīnāṃ keṣāñcin nityatāpi syāt । yady api bahulaṃ vināśakāraṇāni santi, teṣām api svapratyayādhīnasannidhitvān nāvaśyaṃ sannidhānam iti kaścin na vinaśyed api । na hy avaśyaṃ hetavaḥ phalavantaḥ, vaikalyapratibandhasambhavāt ॥

[I,077,i]

	etena vyabhicāritvam uktaṃ kāryāvyavasthiteḥ /
	sarveṣāṃ nāśahetūnāṃ hetumannāśavādinām // <2.54>
ity antaraślokaḥ । tad ayaṃ bhāvo 'napekṣas tadbhāvaṃ prati tadbhāvaniyataḥ, asambhavatpratibandheva kāraṇasāmagrī svakāryotpādane ॥

[I,077,ii]

nanv anapekṣāṇām api keṣāñcit kvacin nāvaśyaṃ tadbhāvaḥ, bhūmibījodakasāmagryām api kadācid aṅkurānutpatteḥ । na, tatrāpi santānapariṇāmāpekṣatvāt । naivaṃ bhāvasya kadācid apekṣā । tatrāpy antyā sāmagrī <I,078> yāvyavahitā kāryotpatteḥ, sā phalavaty eva । saiva tatrāṅkurahetuḥ, pūrvaḥ pariṇāmas tadarthaḥ । na ca tāṃ kaścit pratibandhuṃ samartha ity uktaprāyam ॥

[I,078,i]

nanu yavabījādayo 'pi śālyaṅkure janye 'napekṣāḥ, tadutpattipratyayānāṃ kadācit tatrāpi sannidhānāt । kathaṃ na sāpekṣāḥ । yāvatā sa evaiṣāṃ svabhāvo nāsti yas tadutpādanaḥ śālibījasyeti tatsvabhāvāpekṣāḥ । evaṃ tarhi kṛtakānām api keṣāñcit satāṃ vā sa eva svabhāvo nāsti yo vinaśvaraḥ । tatsvabhāvāpekṣatvān na naśvarāḥ । śālyādibījānām api sa svabhāvaḥ svahetor iti yo na taddhetuḥ so 'tatsvabhāvaḥ syāt । niyataśaktiś ca sa hetuḥ svarūpeṇa pratīta eva । na ca svabhāvaniyamo 'rthānām ākasmiko yuktaḥ, anapekṣasya deśakāladravyaniyamāyogāt । tathātrāpi kaścin niyamahetur vaktavyo yata ime kecin naśvarātmāno jātāḥ । na cātra kaścin niyāmakaḥ svabhāvasyāsti, sarvajanmināṃ vināśasiddheḥ । janmisvabhāvo nāśīti cet, na vai janma nāśisvabhāvasya hetuḥ, na cāhetoḥ svabhāvaniyamaḥ । tasmān nātra kaścid dhetoḥ svabhāvapravibhāgaḥ । tadabhāvāt phalasyāpi nāstīty asamānam ॥

<I,079>

[I,079,i]

nanv idam apy aniśceyam eva — sarvasāmagrījanmāno naśyantīti, tāsām aniḥśeṣadarśanāt । vicitraśaktayo hi sāmagryo dṛśyante । tatra kācit syād api yānaśvarātmānaṃ janayet । na, arthakriyāśaktilakṣaṇatvād vastunaḥ । sarvasāmarthyopākhyāvirahalakṣaṇaṃ hi nirupākhyam ॥

[I,079,ii]

caramasya tarhi kṣaṇasyānupākhyatāprasaṅgaḥ । na, sattvasaṅkhyātakṣaṇāntarānupādānatālakṣaṇatvāc caramatvasya । bhavaty eva hi tasyāpi jñeyavyāpini jñāne 'ntaśaḥ sāmarthyaṃ virūpe 'pi dhātau । dhātvantare tv anekopakāra eva syāt । anābhoge 'sāmarthyam iti cet, na, anābhogāsambhavāt, ekadharmasyāpy ajñāne parārthavṛtteḥ kāryākāryānavabodhāt, sarvatra śaṅkotpatteḥ, sarvasya kvacit kathañcid upakārāt, tadajñāne tadaṅgavikalatvād akṣūṇavidhānāyogāt । nāpi caramasyāsāmarthyam eva, kasyacit karaṇāt । akāriṇo 'pi pratyayavaikalye syāt । sākalye tu karoty eva ॥

<I,080>

[I,080,i]

naivam akṣaṇikasya, sarvathāsambhavāt । na hi tasyākṣaṇikasyārthakriyā sambhavati, kramayaugapadyavirodhāt । akramaḥ, anapekṣasya kartuḥ svasattāmātreṇa kṣepāyogāt, prāg akartuḥ paścād api svabhāvāparāvṛtteḥ । apekṣāyāṃ coktam । nāpi yugapat kriyā, tatsvabhāvasya paścād apy akriyāyogāt । tad ayaṃ bhāvo nivṛttasarvasāmarthyaḥ sattālakṣaṇam atipatati ॥

[I,080,ii]

	arthakriyāsamarthaṃ yat tad atra paramārthasat /
	asanto 'kṣaṇikās tasyāṃ kramākramavirodhataḥ // <2.55>
iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ ॥

[I,080,iii]

skandhadhātvāyatanalakṣaṇasya vā kṛtakasyānityatāsādhanād adoṣaḥ, atadrūpasyāpramāṇatayāsiddher anvayavidhānāyogāt । tad eva ca naḥ kṛtakaṃ yathoktam abhidharme — katame dharmāḥ saṃskṛtāḥ । pañcaskandhā iti । tatra pañcendriyāṇi svabhāvacyutimanti, tatkāryavijñānavicchedavikāradarśanāt, tādavasthye ca teṣāṃ tadayogād apekṣāvirodhāc ca । tathā viṣayāḥ <I,081> sukhaduḥkhe nimittopalakṣaṇaṃ rāgādayo viṣayopalambhaś ca pratividitaivopayantyapayantīty anityāḥ । ta evamprakṛtayaḥ svahetuprakṛtim evaṃrūpāṃ sādhayantas tathāvidhajanmanām anyeṣāṃ ca svabhāvam enam ālagayanti । etena dhātvāyatane vyākhyāte । dharmadhātvāyatane 'pi skandhatrayasvabhāva eveti na virodhaḥ । etena sattā vyākhyātā ॥

[I,081,i]

kiṃ tarhīdānīṃ vināśe 'napekṣāyāḥ sāmarthyam, yāvatā skandhādayo 'nyair eva hetubhir anityāḥ sādhyante । keṣāñcid anityatvasiddhau tathāvidhānāṃ tadvyāptir anapekṣāyāḥ । hetusattve tu vināśasya kasyacit tathābhāve 'py anyatra hetor vaikalyād avināśo 'pi syād ity avyāptiḥ । seyaṃ nirapekṣatā vināśasya kvacit kadācic ca bhāvavirodhinī tadabhāvaṃ svabhāvena sādhayati । yo hi svabhāvo nirapekṣaḥ, sa yadi kadācid bhavet kvacid vā tatkāladravyāpekṣa iti nirapekṣa eva na syāt ॥

[I,081,ii]

sa tarhi vinaśvarasvabhāvo nirapekṣa ity ahetukaḥ syāt । nāhetukaḥ, sattāhetor eva bhāvāt tathotpatteḥ, sato hi bhavatas tādṛśasyaiva bhāvāt । <I,082> nāvaśyaṃ sataḥ kutaścid bhāva iti cet, ākasmikī tarhi satteti neyaṃ kasyacit kvacit kadācid viramet । tad dhi kiñcid upalīyeta na vā yasya yatra kiñcit pratibaddham apratibaddhaṃ vā । seyaṃ sattāpratibandhinī cet, na niyamavatī syāt । tasmān neyam ākasmikī kvacit । kathaṃ tarhīdānīm ahetuko vināśaḥ, jātasya tadbhāve 'nyānapekṣaṇāt । api ca na vināśo nāmānya eva kaścid bhāvāt, kiṃ tu bhāva eva vināśaḥ, sa eva kṣaṇasthāyī jāta iti । tam asya mandāḥ svabhāvam ūrdhvaṃ vyavasyanti, na prāk, darśane 'pi pāṭavābhāvād iti tadvaśena paścād vyavasthāpyate, vikāradarśaneneva viṣamajñaiḥ । tad ayaṃ sattāvyatirekeṇa nānyat kiñcid vināśo 'pekṣata iti tadvyāpī ॥

[I,082,i]

kathaṃ punar etad gamyate — nirapekṣo vināśa iti ॥

[I,082,ii]

	asāmarthyāc ca taddhetoḥ	...
abhāvakāriṇaḥ kriyāpratiṣedhāc ceti caśabdāt । katham asāmarthyam । siddhe hi bhāve kārako na taṃ karoti । nāpy anyakriyāyāṃ tasya kiñcit, tādavasthyāt । atas tannāśano nānyakārī । tenāyaṃ tadatadrūpākaraṇād akiñcitkaro nāpekṣyate ॥

<I,083>

[I,083,i]

kathaṃ kriyāpratiṣedhaḥ । vināśa iti hi bhāvābhāvaṃ manyante । tad ayaṃ vināśahetur abhāvaṃ karotīti prāptam । tatra yady abhāvo nāma kaścit kāryaḥ syāt svabhāvaḥ, sa eva bhāva iti nābhāvaḥ syāt । tadabhāvaṃ karotīti bhāvaṃ na karotīti kriyāpratiṣedho 'sya kṛtaḥ syāt । tathāpy ayam akiñcitkaraḥ kim ity apekṣata iti siddhā vināśaṃ praty anapekṣatā bhāvasya ॥

[I,083,ii]

tasmād
								... bhavaty eṣa svabhāvataḥ /
	yatra nāma bhavaty asmād anyatrāpi svabhāvataḥ // <2.56>
so 'yaṃ kvacid bhavan dṛṣṭo 'napekṣatvāt svabhāvata eva bhavati । tathānyatrāpi svabhāvabhāvī, viśeṣābhāvāt ॥

[I,083,iii]

evam anye 'pi svabhāvahetavo yathāsvaṃ pramāṇaiḥ siddhatanmātrānubandha eva sādhyadharme gamakā veditavyāḥ । yo hi bhāvamātrānubandhī svabhāvaḥ, tatraivāvinābhāvo bhāvasya । bhāvamātrānurodhī svabhāva iti sa eva svayaṃ vastuto bhāvaḥ । sa cātmānaṃ parityajya katham anyatra <I,084> bhaved iti ॥

[I,084,i]

arthāntare tu gamye kāryaṃ hetuḥ, avyabhicārāt । na hy atadutpatter avyabhicāraḥ, anāyattarūpāṇāṃ sahabhāvaniyamābhāvāt ॥

[I,084,ii]

yady arthāntaraṃ hetuḥ, kathaṃ tarhīdānīṃ sa tasya dharmaḥ । tadāśrayāt । kathaṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ । ata eva, anyathāśrayāsiddheḥ । nanu ca pradeśa āśrayo 'gniḥ kāraṇaṃ dhūmasya । so 'pi hi dhūmasya tatkāraṇānāṃ vā pratiṣṭhānād dhetur eva ॥

[I,084,iii]

yadi tadutpatteḥ kāryaṃ gamakam, tadā sarvathā gamyagamakabhāvaḥ, sarvathā janyajanakabhāvāt । na, tadabhāve bhavatas tadutpattiniyamābhāvāt । tasmāt
	kāryaṃ svabhāvair yāvadbhir avinābhāvi kāraṇe /
teṣāṃ
	hetuḥ	...
tatkāryatvaniyamāt । tair eva dharmair ye tair vinā na bhavanti । aṃśena janyajanakatvaprasaṅga <I,085> iti cet, na, tajjanyaviśeṣagrahaṇe 'bhimatatvāl liṅgaviśeṣopādhīnāṃ ca sāmānyānām । aviśiṣṭasāmānyavivakṣāyāṃ vyabhicārān neṣyate ॥

[I,085,i]

katham idaṃ gamyate — na dhūmo 'gniṃ vyabhicaratīti ॥

[I,085,ii]

			... tadvyabhicāre 'sya hetumattāvyatikramāt // <2.57>
yeṣām upalambhe tallakṣaṇam anupalabdhaṃ yad upalabhyate, tatraikābhāve 'pi nopalabhyate, tat tasya kāryam । tac ca dhūme 'py asti । sa sakṛd api tathādarśanāt tatkāryaḥ siddhaḥ । akāryatve 'kāraṇāt sakṛd apy abhāvāt ॥

[I,085,iii]

nanv araṇinirmathanādiṣv asaty apy agnau bhāvād akāryam । na, indhanavikārahetor uṣṇasparśaviśeṣasyāgnitvāt । kāryasya ca kāraṇam antareṇa bhāve 'hetutaiva syāt । na hi yasya yam antareṇa bhāvaḥ, sa tasya hetur bhavati । bhavati ca dhūmo 'gnim antareṇa, tan na taddhetuḥ syāt । anyahetukatvān nāhetuka iti cet, na, tatrāpi tulyatvāt — tadabhāve 'py agnau bhavatīti । kathaṃ ca tato 'nyato vātajjananasvabhāvād bhavet । svayam atatsvabhāvasyājananāt <I,086> tasyāhetutā syāt ॥

[I,086,i]

na vai sa eva bhavati, tādṛśasya bhāvāt । anyādṛśād bhavan kathaṃ tādṛśaḥ । tādṛśād dhi bhavaṃs tādṛśaḥ syāt । anyādṛśād api tādṛśodbhave tacchaktiniyamābhāvān na hetubhedo bhedaka ity akāraṇaṃ viśvasya vaiśvarūpyaṃ syāt । tatra cokto doṣaḥ । sarvaṃ ca sarvasmāj jāyet । tasmāt kāraṇabhedābhedābhyāṃ kāryabhedābhedau । tan na dhūmo 'rthād dṛṣṭākāravijātīyād bhavati, ahetutvaprasaṅgāt ॥

[I,086,ii]

tathā ca
	nityaṃ sattvam asattvaṃ vāhetor anyānapekṣaṇāt /
	apekṣāto hi bhāvānāṃ kādācitkatvasambhavaḥ // <2.58>
sa hi dhūmo 'hetur bhavan nirapekṣatvān na kadācin na bhavet, tadbhāve vaikalyābhāvād iṣṭakālavat । tadāpi vā na bhavet, abhāvakālāviśeṣāt । apekṣayā hi bhāvāḥ kādācitkā bhavanti, bhāvābhāvakālayos tadbhāvayogyatāyogyatāyogāt, tulyayogyatāyogyatayor deśakālayos tadvattetarayor niyamāyogāt । sā ca yogyatā hetubhāvāt kim anyat । tasmād ekadeśakālaparihāreṇānyadeśakālayor vartamāno bhāvas tatsāpekṣo <I,087> nāma bhavati । tathā hi tathāvṛttir evāpekṣā, tatkṛtopakārānapekṣasya tanniyamāyogāt । tan niyatadeśakālatvād dhūmo yatra dṛṣṭaḥ sakṛd vaikalye ca punar na dṛṣṭaḥ, tajjanyo 'sya svabhāvaḥ, anyathā sakṛd apy abhāvāt । sa tatpratiniyato 'nyatra kathaṃ bhavet । bhavan vā na dhūmaḥ syāt tajjanito hi svabhāvaviśeṣo dhūma iti । tathā hetur api tathābhūtakāryajananasvabhāvaḥ । anyato 'pi bhāve na sa tasya svabhāva iti sakṛd api na janayet । na vā sa dhūmaḥ, adhūmajananasvabhāvād bhāvāt । tatsvabhāvatve ca sa evāgnir ity avyabhicāraḥ ॥

[I,087,i]

	agnisvabhāvaḥ śakrasya mūrdhā yady agnir eva saḥ /
	athānagnisvabhāvo 'sau dhūmas tatra kathaṃ bhavet // <2.59>
	dhūmahetusvabhāvo hi vahnis tacchaktibhedavān /
	adhūmahetor dhūmasya bhāve sa syād ahetukaḥ // <2.60>
iti saṅgrahaślokau ।

[I,087,ii]

kathaṃ tarhīdānīṃ bhinnāt sahakāriṇaḥ kāryotpattir yathā cakṣūrūpāder vijñānasya । na vai kiñcid ekaṃ janakaṃ tatsvabhāvaṃ vā । kiṃ tu sāmagrī janikā <I,088> tatsvabhāvā । saivānumīyate । saiva ca sāmagrī svabhāvasthityāśrayaḥ kāryasya । ata eva sahakāriṇām apy aparyāyeṇa jananam ॥

[I,088,i]

yad api kiñcid vijātīyād bhavad dṛṣṭaṃ gomayādeḥ śālūkādiḥ, tatrāpi tathābhidhāne 'py asty eva svabījaprabhavāt svabhāvabhedo hetusvabhāvabhedāt, yathā kadalī bījakandodbhavā । sphuṭam eva tādṛśaṃ bhedaṃ loko vivecayaty ākārabhedāt ॥

[I,088,ii]

anantaraṃ vā kāraṇaṃ kāryam anumāpayati । tattulyarūpāṇāṃ kāryadravyāṇāṃ tulyam, yathā pravṛddhayoḥ kadalyoḥ kandodbhavaḥ । yatra tu sākṣād dhetubhedaḥ, tatra rūpabhedo 'pi, yathā tayor eva bījakandodbhavayoḥ । nāpy ākārabheda eva tadatattve nibandhanam, api tu svabhāvāntaram api । kṛtrimākṛtrimāṇām iva maṇimuktāpravālādīnām । kvacit puṣpe bhede nīletarakusumayor iva sūryayoḥ, kvacit phale vandhyetarayor iva karkoṭakayoḥ, kvacid rase vanyetarayor <I,089> iva trapuṣayoḥ, kvacit prabhāve sparśopayogasraṃsinyor iva harītakyoḥ । tasmān na suvivecitaṃ kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ vyabhicarati । hetuviśeṣe 'pi kāryāviśeṣe doṣāt ॥

[I,089,i]

	anvayavyatirekād yo yasya dṛṣṭo 'nuvartakaḥ /
	svabhāvas tasya taddhetur ato bhinnān na sambhavaḥ // <2.61>
	kāryakāraṇabhāvād vā svabhāvād vā niyāmakāt /
	avinābhāvaniyamo 'darśanān na na darśanāt // <2.62>
	avaśyambhāvaniyamaḥ kaḥ parasyānyathā paraiḥ /
	arthāntaranimitte vā dharme vāsasi rāgavat // <2.63>
iti saṅgrahaślokāḥ ॥

[I,089,ii]

api ca
	arthāntaranimitto hi dharmaḥ syād anya eva saḥ /
na hi tasmin niṣpanne 'niṣpanno bhinnahetuko vā tatsvabhāvo yuktaḥ । ayaṃ hi bhedo bhedahetur vā bhāvānāṃ yad uta viruddhadharmādhyāsaḥ kāraṇabhedaś <I,090> ca । tataś cen na bhedasiddhiḥ, na kasyacit kutaścid bheda ity ekaṃ dravyaṃ viśvaṃ syāt । tataḥ sahotpattivināsau sarvasya ca sarvatropayogaḥ syāt । anyathaikam ity eva na syān nāmāntaraṃ vā, arthabhedam abhyupagamya tathābhidhānāt ॥

[I,090,i]

nanv anarthāntarahetutve 'pi bhāvakāle 'nityatāniṣpattes tulyātatsvabhāvatā । na vai kācid anityatā nāmānyā yā paścān niṣpadyeta । sa eva hi bhāvaḥ kṣaṇasthitidharmānityatety uktaprāyam । vacanabhede 'pi dharmidharmatayā nimittaṃ bhedāntarākṣepānākṣepāv ityādiprasaṅgaḥ pramāṇavārttike nirṇītaḥ । tam asya svabhāvaṃ mandabuddhiḥ paśyann api na vyavasyati sattopalambhena sarvadātadbhāvaśaṅkāvipralabdhaḥ sadṛśāparotpattivipralabdho vā । antyakṣaṇadarśināṃ niścayāt paścād asyānupalabdhyāsthitipratipatter niścayakāla iti tadānityatā vyavasthāpyata ity apy uktam । anyathārthāntaram <I,091> evānityatā syād anyanimittatve 'nimittatve vā । tathā ca bhāvas tadvān na syāt, anupayogāt । upayoge vā sa evāsya svātmabhūtānityateti kim anyayā, svabhāvena vācalasyārthāntarayoge 'pi tadbhāvānupapatteḥ । sa cārthāntarād bhavann anityatānyo vā dharmo hetuḥ phalaṃ vā syāt, ahetuphalasyāsambandhāt tatra bhāvānumānasyāsambhavāt । tatra
	paścād bhāvān na hetutvaṃ phale 'py ekāntatā kutaḥ // <2.64>
sa hi niṣpanne bhāve 'rthāntarataḥ paścādbhavan kathaṃ tasya hetuḥ syāt । phalasyāpi paropaskārāpekṣiṇo nāvaśyaṃ hetau bhāva iti tadbhāvahetor anaikāntikatvam । bhāvamātrabhāvitve siddhānyānapekṣaṇād ahetutā tanmātrānubandhaś ca । tato 'pi kasyacid bhāve tadanupayogād apracyutir iti pūrvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ । tan nāvināśasvabhāve bhāve tadanumānam ॥

[I,091,i]

kathaṃ nānumānaṃ yāvatā nānityatābhāve kvacid utpattir dṛṣṭā, adarśanāc <I,092> ca vipakṣe vyatirekaḥ, tato 'vyabhicāra iti ॥

[I,092,i]

	na yuktādṛṣṭimātreṇa vipakṣe 'vyabhicāritā /
	sambhāvyavyabhicāratvāt sthālītaṇḍulapākavat // <2.65>
na hi bahulaṃ pākadarśane 'pi sthālyantargatamātreṇa pākaḥ sidhyati, vyabhicāradarśanāt । etāvat tu syāt — evaṃsvabhāvā etatsamānapākahetavaḥ pakvā iti । anyathā śeṣavad etad anumānaṃ vyabhicāri ॥

[I,092,ii]

kiṃ punar etac cheṣavat ॥

[I,092,iii]

	yasyādarśanamātreṇa vyatirekaḥ pradarśyate /
sa tasya vyatireko 'niścita iti vipakṣe vṛttir āśaṅkyate । vyatirekasādhanasyādarśanamātrasya
	tasya saṃśayahetutvāc cheṣavat tad udāhṛtam // <2.66>
na hi sarvānupalabdhir abhāvapratipādikā । tasmād ekanivṛttyānyanivṛttim icchatā tayoḥ kaścit svabhāvapratibandho 'py eṣṭavyaḥ । anyathāgamako <I,093> hetuḥ syāt ॥

[I,093,i]

	hetos triṣv api rūpeṣu niścayas tena varṇitaḥ /
	asiddhaviparītārthavyabhicārivipakṣataḥ // <2.67>
na hy asati pratibandhe 'nvayavyatirekaniścayo 'sti । tena tam eva darśayan niścayam āha — prasiddhas tu dvayor api sādhanam iti । tatrānvayaniścayena viruddhatatpakṣyāṇāṃ nirāsaḥ, vyatirekaniścayenānaikāntikasya । dvayor ity ekaprasiddhapratiṣedhaḥ, prasiddha iti sandigdhayoḥ śeṣavadasādhāraṇayoḥ sapakṣavipakṣayoḥ ॥

[I,093,ii]

asaty api pratibandhe 'darśanamātreṇa vyatireke yad āha — eṣa tāvan nyāyo yad ubhayaṃ vaktavyaṃ viruddhānaikāntikapratipakṣeṇeti, yad vaidharmyavacanam anaikāntikapratipakṣeṇa, yadi tena vipakṣe 'darśanaṃ khyāpyate, tad anukte 'pi gamyate । na hi tasya prāg darśanabhrāntiḥ, yā vacanena nivartyeta । smṛtir vācādarśane kriyata iti cet, darśanaṃ khalv apratīyamānam anaṅgam iti yuktaṃ tatra smaraṇādhānaṃ vacanam । adarśanaṃ tu darśanābhāvaḥ <I,094> । sa darśanena bādhyate । tadabhāve tu siddha evety apārthakaṃ tatsiddhaye vacanam ॥

[I,094,i]

nānupalabhamānasya tāvatā nāstīti bhavati । tadarthaṃ vacanam । yady anupalabhamāno 'pi nāstīti na pratīyāt, vacanād api naiva pratyeṣyati । tad api hy anupalambham eva khyāpayati । na caikānupalambho 'nyābhāvaṃ sādhayati, atiprasaṅgāt । na sa tena sādhyate, api tv anupalambhena svayam । yukto dṛśyasyādarśane 'bhāvaḥ, sa tadabhāve na yuktaḥ । kvacid yadṛcchayā tathābhāve 'pi tayor apratibandhād vyāptyasiddheḥ । nāpi tena nāstīti vacanāt tathā bhavati, atiprasaṅgāt । tasmād vyāvṛttim icchatā tatra nyāyo vaktavyaḥ, yato 'sya vyāvṛttam iti bhavati ॥

[I,094,ii]

	na ca nāstīti vacanāt tan nāsty eva yathā yadi /
	nāsti sa khyāpyate nyāyas tadā nāstīti gamyate // <2.68>
iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ ॥

[I,094,iii]

nanu tadabhāve 'nupalambhāt siddhā vyāvṛttiḥ । uktam atra kiñcit ॥

<I,095>

[I,095,i]

api ca yady adṛṣṭyā nivṛttiḥ syāc cheṣavad vyabhicāri kim । yathā pakvāny etāni phalāny evaṃrasāni vā rūpāviśeṣād ekaśākhāprabhavatvād vā, upayuktaphalavat । atrāpy upayuktavyatiriktapakṣīkaraṇe hetoḥ sādhyābhāve 'nupalambho 'stīti kathaṃ vyabhicāraḥ ॥

[I,095,ii]

pratyakṣabādhāśaṅkāvyabhicāra ity eke । na, pakṣīkṛtaviṣaye 'bhāvāt । kadācid bhaved iti cet, tathā śaṅkāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ, anyatrāpy abhāvaniyamābhāvāt । vṛttaṃ pramāṇaṃ bādhakam । avṛttabādhane sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ । vyatirekas tu siddha eva sādhanam iti tathābhāve niścayam apekṣate । anupalambhāt tu kvacid abhāvasiddhāv apy apratibaddhasya tadabhāve sarvatrābhāvāsiddheḥ saṃśayād avyatireko vyabhicāraḥ śeṣavataḥ ॥

[I,095,iii]
