kiṃ ca vyatireky api hetuḥ syāt । nedaṃ nirātmakaṃ jīvaccharīram aprāṇādimattvaprasaṅgād iti । nirātmakānāṃ ghaṭādīnāṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭānāṃ prāṇādyabhavena vyāptes tannivṛttau vyāpyanivṛtter ātmagatiḥ syāt । adṛśyānupalambhād <I,096> abhāvāsiddhau ghaṭādīnāṃ nairātmyāsiddheḥ prāṇāder anivṛttiḥ । abhyupagamāt siddham iti cet, katham idānīm ātmasiddhiḥ । parasyāpy apramāṇikā nairātmyasiddhiḥ । abhyupagamena ca sātmakānātmakau vibhajya tatrābhāvena gamakatvaṃ kathayatā āgamikatvam ātmani pratipannaṃ syāt, nānumeyatvam ॥

[I,096,i]

yāpy asiddhiyojanā — tathā sapakṣe sann asann ityevamādiṣv api yathāyogam udāhāryam iti, sāpi na vācyā, anupalambha eva saṃśayāt, upalambhe tadabhāvāt । anupalambhāc ca vyatireka iti saṃśayito 'nivāryaḥ syāt । yathāyogavacanād anivārita eveti cet, na, ya eva tūbhayaniścitavācītyādivacanāt । tenānupalambhe 'pi saṃśayād anivṛttiṃ manyamānas tatpratiṣedham āha ॥

[I,096,ii]

śrāvaṇatvasyāpi nityānityayor adarśanāt tadvyāvṛttir iti tadvyavacchedahetutā syāt । na hi tadvyāvṛtter anyat tadvyavacchedanam । avyavacchedas tu kutaścid vyāvṛtter evāniścayāt । yo hi yatra nāstīti niścitaḥ, sa bhavan kathaṃ tadabhāvaṃ na gamayet । pramāṇāntarabādhanān nobhayavyavacchedaḥ । <I,097> anyonyavyavacchedarūpāṇām ekavyavacchedenānyavidhānād apratiṣedhaḥ, vidhipratiṣedhayor virodhāt । na tarhīdānīm adarśanaṃ pramāṇam, bādhāsambhavāt । tathānyatrāpi pramāṇāntarabādhā sambhāvyate । lakṣaṇayukte bādhāsambhave tallakṣaṇam eva dūṣitaṃ syād iti sarvatrānāśvāsaḥ । anumānaviṣaye 'pi pratyakṣānumānavirodhadarśanād anāśvāsaprasaṅga iti cet, na, yathokte 'bhāvāt । viruddhāvyabhicāry avacanam iti cet, anumānaviṣaye 'vacanād iṣṭam । viṣayaṃ cāsya nivedayiṣyāmaḥ ॥

[I,097,i]

yad apy āha — yady adarśanamātreṇa dṛṣṭebhyaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate, na ca so 'pi yukta iti । katham ayuktaḥ, anupalambhād abhāvasiddheḥ । nanūpalabdhilakṣaṇaprāpteḥ sparśasya yukta eva pratiṣedhaḥ । na yuktaḥ, dṛśyatatsvabhāvaviṣayamātrāpratiṣedhāt । pṛthivyādi sāmānyena gṛhītvāyaṃ pratiṣedham āha । tatra ca tūlopalapallavādiṣu tadbhāve 'pi sparśabhedadarśanāt । kvacid viśeṣasyāpi sambhavāc chaṅkayā bhavitavyam iti sarvatrādarśanamātreṇāyuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ ॥

<I,098>

[I,098,i]

api ca yadi kathañcid vipakṣe 'darśanamātreṇāpratibaddhasyāpi tadavyabhicāraḥ, kvacid deśe kānicid dravyāṇi kathañcid dṛṣṭāni punar anyatrānyathā dṛśyante । yathā kāścid oṣadhayaḥ kṣetraviśeṣe viśiṣṭarasavīryavipākā bhavanti, nānyatra । tathā kālasaṃskārabhedāt । na ca taddeśais tathā dṛṣṭā iti sarvās tattvena tathā bhavanti, sambhavadviśeṣahetūnāṃ guṇāntarasambhavāt । viśeṣahetvabhāve tu syād anumānam । yathādṛṣṭakartṛkam api vākyaṃ puruṣasaṃskārapūrvakam iti, vākyeṣu viśeṣābhāvāt, sarvaprakārāṇāṃ puruṣaiḥ karaṇadarśanāt । naivam asambhavadviśeṣahetavaḥ puruṣāḥ, yena vacanādeḥ kiñcinmātrasādharmyāt sarvākārasāmyam anumīyeta, sarvaguṇeṣu viśeṣadarśanāt, saṃskārabhedena viśeṣapratipatteḥ, tadvad anyasyāpi sambhavād asambhavānumāne ca bādhakahetvasambhavāt, vairāgyādṛṣṭer adṛṣṭena ca bādhyabādhakabhāvāsiddheḥ, rāgādyavyabhicārikāryāsambhavāt, sambhave 'pi viśeṣāṇāṃ draṣṭum aśakyatvāt teṣāṃ cāpratikṣepārhatvāt ॥

[I,098,ii]

naivaṃ vākyāni, dṛśyaviśeṣatvāt । adṛśyatve 'py adṛṣṭaviśeṣāṇāṃ vijātīyatvopagamavirodhāt <I,099> , tadviśeṣāṇām anyatrāpi śakyakriyatvāt, pratyakṣāṇāṃ śabdānām apratyakṣasvabhāvābhāvāt । bhrāntinimittābhāvāt, bādhakābhāvād bhrāntyasiddheḥ । puruṣeṣu viśeṣadarśanasya bādhakatvād asamānaṃ parabhūtasya ca vākyaviśeṣasyātadviśeṣatvāt । tad abhinnasvabhāvānāṃ sarveṣāṃ puruṣakriyā na vā kasyacit ॥

[I,099,i]

	tasmāt tanmātrasambaddhaḥ svabhāvo bhāvam eva vā /
	nivartayet	...
yathā vṛkṣaḥ śiṃśapām, śākhādimadviśeṣasyaiva kasyacit tathāprasiddheḥ । sa tasyāḥ svabhāvaḥ । svabhāvaṃ ca parityajya kathaṃ bhāvo bhavet, svabhāvasyaiva bhāvatvād iti tasya svabhāvapratibandhād avyabhicāraḥ ॥

[I,099,ii]

				... kāraṇaṃ vā kāryam avyabhicārataḥ // <2.69>
nivartayet । kāraṇam api nivartamānaṃ kāryaṃ nivartayati । anyathā tat tasya kāryam eva na syāt । ataḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvo 'pi svabhāvaṃ niyamayatīty ubhayathā svabhāvapratibandhād eva nivṛttiḥ ॥

<I,100>

[I,100,i]

	anyathaikanivṛttyānyavinivṛttiḥ kathaṃ bhaved /
	nāśvavān iti martyena na bhāvyaṃ gomatāpi kim // <2.70>
	sannidhānāt tathaikasya katham anyasya sannidhiḥ /
	gomān ity eva martyena bhāvyam aśvavatāpi kim // <2.71>
ity antaraślokau । tasmāt svabhāvapratibandhād eva hetuḥ sādhyaṃ gamayati । sa ca tadbhāvalakṣaṇas tadutpattilakṣaṇo vā । sa evāvinābhāvo dṛṣṭāntābhyāṃ pradarśyate ॥

[I,100,ii]

ata eva vaidharmyadṛṣṭānte 'vaśyam ihāśrayo neṣṭaḥ । dṛṣṭānte hi sādhyadharmasya tadbhāvas tanmātrānubandhena khyāpyate । yaḥ kṛtakasvabhāvaṃ janayati, so 'nityaṃ svabhāvaṃ santaṃ janayatīti pramāṇaṃ dṛṣṭāntenopadarśyate । tena ca pramāṇena sādhyadharmasya tanmātrānubandho gamyate । hetubhāvo vā tasmin saty eva bhāvād ity arthāntarasya । tathā prasiddhe tadbhāve hetubhāve vānityatvābhāve kṛtakatvaṃ na bhavati dahanābhāve ca dhūmaḥ । tathā hi sa tasya svabhāvo hetur vā । kathaṃ svabhāvaṃ hetuṃ vāntareṇa bhaved ity āśrayam antareṇāpi vaidharmyadṛṣṭānte prasidhyati vyatirekaḥ ॥

<I,101>

	hetusvabhāvābhāvo 'taḥ pratiṣedhe ca kasyacit /
	hetuḥ	...
tāv eva hi nivartamānau svapratibaddhaṃ nivartayata iti kasyacid arthasya pratiṣedham api sādhayitukāmena hetor vyāpakasya vā svabhāvasya nivṛttir hetutvenākhyeyā । anyathāpratibaddhanivṛttyānyanivṛttyasiddheḥ ॥

[I,101,i]

			... yuktopalambhasya tasya cānupalambhanam // <2.72>
pratiṣedhahetuḥ । pratiṣedhaviṣayavyavahārahetus taddhetur ity uktaḥ, svayaṃ tathābhūtānupalambhasya pratiṣedharūpatvāt । hetuvyāpakānupalabdhir ubhayasyāpi hetur iti । eṣa trividha eva pratiṣedhahetur upalabhyasattvasya hetos tathābhāvaniścaye vyāpakasya svātmanaś cānupalabdhir iti sa tattadviruddhādyagatigatiprayogabhedenānekaprakāra uktaḥ ॥

<॥ svārthānumānaparicchedo dvitīyaḥ>

<II,001>

{3.I}

<§ 3.I.1>

[II,001,i]

	parārthamanumānaṃ tu svadṛṣṭārthaprakāśanam /
yathaiva hi svayaṃ trirūpālliṅgālliṅgini jñānamutpannam , tathā paratra liṅgijñānotpipādayiṣayā trirūpaliṅgākhyānaṃ parārthamanumānam । kāraṇe kāryopacārāt ॥

<§ 3.I.2>

<§ 3.I.2.1>

[II,001,ii]

atra svadṛṣṭārthagrahaṇam
	āgamātparadṛṣṭaṃ na sādhanaṃ nāpyanarthataḥ // <1>
siddhiriti jñāpanārtham ॥

<§ 3.I.2.1.1>

<§ 3.I.2.1.1.i>

[II,001,iii]

yathāhureke — parasya pratipādyatvātsvayamadṛṣṭamapi parairdṛṣṭaṃ sādhanam , yathā — acetanāḥ sukhādayo buddhirvā , utpatteranityatvādvā , rūpādivaditi । tadayuktam , anumānaviṣaye vācaḥ prāmāṇyābhāvāt । <II,002> prāmāṇye vā nānumānapravṛttiḥ syāt , vacanamātreṇārthasiddherhetvādivaiyarthyāt ॥

[II,002,i]

vacanaviśeṣasya prāmāṇyādadoṣa iti cet , uktamatrāgamaprāmāṇyacintāyām । nāpyasya kaścidviśeṣaḥ pramāṇāsaṃvāde । saṃvāde vā na tatsiddhaṃ parasyaiva siddham । tannābhyupagamātparīkṣāvṛttiḥ , api tu parīkṣāyā abhyupagama iti na paropagatena sādhanam ॥

[II,002,ii]

tadāgamabādhanāya paraṃ prati sādhanoktestadāsyāprāmāṇyāttatsiddhamasiddhamiti kathaṃ tataḥ siddhiḥ । tadāgamavatastatsiddhamiti cet , kasya ka āgamaḥ । bādhyamānaśca pramāṇena sa kathamāgamaḥ ॥

<II,003>

[II,003,i]

	riktasya jantorjātasya guṇadoṣamapaśyataḥ /
	vilabdhā vata keneme siddhāntaviṣamagrahāḥ // <2>
ityantaraślokaḥ ॥

[II,003,ii]

tadāgamaviruddhābhyupagamaśca tenaiva kathaṃ bhavet , tadupagama āgamasya tyāgāṅgasyāpramāṇatvenāpratipattiyogyatvāt । tadupagamādāgamaḥ , tataḥ sādhanadharmaḥ , tasmādvastusthitiriti ca suvyavasthitāni vastūni । puruṣecchayā ca hetutadābhāsayostattvavyavasthāne ka idānīṃ heturaheturvā vastutaḥ , tasyā vastuvṛttiniyamābhāvāt । sankhalvapyarthaḥ pratītyapekṣaḥ sādhanam । nāsanpratītimātreṇa , yataḥ paropagatena siddhiḥ syāt । sato 'pyavastukṛtā pratipattirasatpratipattiṃ nātiśete , apratyayatvāt ॥

<II,004>

[II,004,i]

uktaṃ ca — na kāryasvabhāvānupalambhaviśeṣebhyo 'paraṃ pratipattyaṅgamastīti । tadvastutaḥ siddhalakṣaṇamasiddhaṃ kimātmanaḥ । pareṇāpyanyataḥ pratipattumayuktameva ॥

<§ 3.I.2.1.1.ii>

[II,004,ii]

yastu paraparikalpitaiḥ prasaṅgaḥ , yathā — deśakālāvasthāviśeṣaniyataikadravyasaṃsargāvyavacchinnasvabhāvāntaravirahādanekavṛtterekasya na deśādiviśeṣavatānyena yogaḥ , tathābhūtasvabhāvasya virodhādbhinnadeśādiyogena , sa ekadharmopagame 'paradharmopagamasandarśanārthaḥ । tadanabhyupagame cobhayanivṛttiḥ , vivekasya kartumaśakyatvāt , tasyānyatra vastutaḥ pratibandhāt ॥

[II,004,iii]

kathamidānīmasambhavino 'rthasya pratipattiriti cet , so 'pi tatrāsambhavī yo 'sambhavinā vyāpta iti tadabhyupagame 'paro niyataprāptiriti durnivāraḥ ॥

<II,005>

[II,005,i]

nanu tathāpyasiddhirhetoḥ pratijñāyāścābhyupetādibādhā , svayamabhyupagamāntarāvasthānāt । na , parīkṣākāle kasyacidanabhyupagamāt । sa yamarthaṃ pratipadyate , taṃ pratipadyamāno 'paramapi sāmarthyāyātamabhyupagacchati , prabhābhyupagame pradīpābhyupagamavaditi pratipattireva sā , na darśanāntarāvasthitasya doṣodbhāvanam । sa hi tasyopagamakālaḥ । tatra yāvānartho yuktisāmarthyādāpatati , sa sarvo 'bhyupagantavyaḥ , na vā kaściditi । nāpyasiddhyādayaḥ , yadyevamidamapi syānna vobhayamiti dharmayoḥ sambandhopadarśanāt । ekāntaparigrahe syādeṣa doṣaḥ । na vā sati hetau , yuktiprāptasyāvaśyaṃ parigrahārhatvāt । na cābhyupagamo yuktibādhane samartha iti vakṣyāmaḥ । abhyupagataikadharmaṇo 'vaśyamaparābhyupagamo yuktikṛta iti । asati tu hetau maulasya hetorvyāpyavyā<II,006>pakabhāvasādhanaprakāra eṣaḥ । na viparyayasādhanam , hetorapramāṇatvāt ॥

[II,006,i]

ihāpi yadi viparyayeṇaivamanityatotpattiniṣedhaḥ kriyate , na kaścidevaṃ karoti । na ca śakyamevaṃ kartum , caitanyenānayorvirodhāsiddheḥ prasaṅgaviparyayasādhanayoragamakatvāt । ekasya bhāve 'vikalakāraṇasya prāgbhavato 'bhāvādvirodhaḥ , parasparaparihārasthitalakṣaṇatayā vā । na cāyamutpattivināśābhyāṃ caitanyasya prasidhyati । ekasya tu yathoktasvabhāvāntaravirahopagamādeva bhinnadeśādibhiryogābhāvaḥ , tadabhāvasya tadbhāvasya cānyonyaparihārasthitalakṣaṇatvena virodhāt ॥

[II,006,ii]

ayameva cācāryairavayavipratiṣedhādiṣu bahumukhairupanyāsairekatvānekavṛttyorvirodhāttathāvidhasvabhāvaniṣedhaḥ kriyate । viruddhayorekopagamasyāparatyāganāntarīyakatvānnobhayadharmāstīti । siddhāntopagamanibandhaneṣu vicāraprastāveṣu , anyathābhyupagamya vicārāyogāt ॥

<II,007>

<§ 3.I.2.1.2>

<§ 3.I.2.1.2.i>

[II,007,i]

anarthaḥ khalvapi kalpanāsamāropito na liṅgam , yathā — pakṣasapakṣānyataratvādanityaḥ śabdo nityo veti । na hyatra śabdaghaṭayoḥ śabdākāśayorvā vāstavī pratyāsattiḥ , api tu vakturvivakṣākṛtā , tadabhāve vivakṣitetarayorāsattiviprakarṣābhāvāt । vastusvabhāvatve ca punarvivakṣāntare parāvṛttyayogāt । yugapadekatra viruddhaguṇopasaṃhārāyogācca । tasmādete karturicchāmātrānurodhino dharmā na vastusvabhāvamanuvidadhati , tasyaivamavṛtteḥ । tasmānna tato 'rthasiddhiḥ , vasturūpayoḥ pratyāsattiviprakarṣayorasiddheḥ । siddhau tu syāt , yathā tādṛśaṃ rūpasādharmyaṃ kvacidabhisamīkṣyāhuḥ — eṣa piṇḍo viṣāṇī gogavayayoranyataratvāditi ॥

<§ 3.I.2.1.2.ii>

[II,007,ii]

atha punarmayaivaṃvivakṣitatvādityāha , tadā sidhyatyarthaśūnyaṃ vivakṣāmātram । tato nārthasiddhiḥ , tadicchāyā vastuni vṛttiniyamābhāvāt । <II,008> tathā hyaśakyadarśanametat — yatra tadicchā tatra vastubhāva iti vyāptyasiddhervyabhicāraḥ । etena madupagamādayo hetuprayogā vyākhyātāḥ , āgamasiddhāśca । vacanasya vakturicchāmātreṇa pravṛtteḥ ॥

[II,008,i]

	kalpanāgamayoḥ karturicchāmātrānurodhataḥ /
	vastunaścānyathābhāvāttatkṛtā vyabhicāriṇaḥ // <3.3>
iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ ॥

<§ 3.I.2.2>

[II,008,ii]

trirūpaliṅgākhyānaṃ parārthamanumānamityarthānna pakṣavacanaṃ sādhanamityuktaṃ veditavyam । kathaṃ na sādhanam । sākṣātpāramparyeṇa vā tataḥ siddheranutpatteḥ ॥

<§ 3.I.2.2.1>

[II,008,iii]

sākṣāttāvat —
	arthādarthagateḥ śaktiḥ pakṣahetvabhidhānayoḥ /
<II,009>
	nārthe tena tayornāsti svataḥ sādhanasaṃsthitiḥ // <3.4>
artha eva hyarthaṃ gamayati , nāntarīyakatvāt । nābhidhānam , sambandhaniyamābhāvāt । tato na pakṣasya hetorvā vacanaṃ sādhanaṃ svato 'rthasiddheḥ । saṃśayastu pakṣavacanādarthe dṛṣṭaḥ , na niścaya iti sākṣānna sādhanam ॥

<§ 3.I.2.2.2>

[II,009,i]

	sādhyābhidhānātpakṣoktiḥ pāramparyeṇa nāpyalam /
	śaktasya sūcakaṃ hetuvaco 'śaktamapi svayam // <3.5>
nāpi pāramparyeṇa , sādhyasyaivābhidhānāt । hetuvacanaṃ tu svayamaśaktamapi śaktasya vācakamiti sādhanamiṣṭamupacāreṇa ॥

[II,009,ii]

tato hetuvacanapravṛttestadapi śaktameveti cet , saṃśayena jijñāsoḥ prakaraṇapravṛttesteṣvapi prasaṅgaḥ । vipakṣavacanamātrādapi saṃśaye pratipakṣa<II,010>hetuvacanapravṛtteḥ sambhavāttadapi tena saha sādhanaṃ syāt । tasmāttriṣveva rūpeṣvantaraṅgamarthasiddhau sāmarthyamavasthitam , tatra ca smṛtisamādhānaṃ tadvacasīti tadeva sādhanam ॥

[II,010,i]

akhyāpite viṣaye hetupravṛtterasambhavādviṣayakhyāpanādeva sāmarthyamiti cet , uktamatra । api ca vināpyanena yāvānkaścitkṛtakaḥ sa sarvo 'nityaḥ , śabdaśca kṛtaka ityukte 'pi śabdo 'nitya ityarthādgamyata eva । tannāvaśyamasya nirdeśaḥ । tenānuktāvapi pakṣasya siddherapratibandhāttriṣvanyatamarūpasyaivānuktirnyūnatāsādhanadoṣa ityuktaṃ veditavyam ॥ ॥

<II,011>

{3.II}

<§ 3.II.1>

[II,011,i]

na tarhīdānīṃ sādhanasyātannirdeśanāntarīyakatvātpakṣasya lakṣaṇaṃ vācyam । vācyam , sādhyāsādhyaviparyayeṇa vipratipattidarśanāttannirāsārtham ।

[II,011,ii]

sa cānumeyaḥ
	svarūpeṇaiva nirdeśyaḥ svayamiṣṭo 'nirākṛtaḥ /

<§ 3.II.2>

<§ 3.II.2.1>

[II,011,iii]

atra caturbhiḥ svarūpanipāteṣṭasvayampadaiḥ ,
	asiddhāsādhanārthoktavādyabhyupagamagrahaḥ // <3.6>
veditavyaḥ । tena siddhaṃ yathā — śrāvaṇaḥ śabda iti , asiddhamapi sādhanatveneṣṭaṃ yathā'siddhau hetudṛṣṭāntau , aprakaraṇāśrayaḥ , anāntarīyakābhyupagamaśca śāstropagame 'pi vādino nirastaḥ ॥

<II,012>

<§ 3.II.2.2>

<§ 3.II.2.2.1>

<§ 3.II.2.2.1.i>

[II,012,i]

kathamidānīmaśrūyamāṇaḥ sādhyatveneṣṭa iti gamyate । prakaraṇāt , yathā saṃhatānāṃ pārārthyaṃ sādhya ātmārthatvam । tadanuktamapīcchayā vyāptaṃ sādhyamiti darśanārthamiṣṭagrahaṇam । ayameva dharmadharmiṇorviśeṣa ukto vyapekṣātaḥ । asaṃhataviṣayaṃ pārārthyameṣāmiti vacane dharmaviśeṣaṇatvenopādānāttasya viśeṣaḥ । parārthāḥ santaścakṣurādayo 'saṃhatārthā iti dharmiṇo viśeṣa iti vyavasthāmātraṃ bhidyate , nārthaḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.2.1.ii>

[II,012,ii]

arthāntare ca prakṛtādviśeṣe sādhye kastayoḥ sambandhaḥ ; yenaivamuktaḥ sādhyadharmo 'nvākarṣati , atiprasaṅgāt । tathā ca sarvo heturviruddho dṛṣṭāntaśca sādhyavikalaḥ syāt , tāvato dharmakalāpasya kvacidananvayāt । tato na kutaścidgatiḥ syāt ॥

<II,013>

<§ 3.II.2.2.1.iii>

[II,013,i]

uktadharmānanvaya eṣa doṣo nānyatreti cet , na , sādhyatvāviśeṣāt । adoṣe ceṣṭavighāto 'pi na syāt । tasya sādhyavipakṣa eva vṛttyā tadviparyāsanalakṣaṇatvāt । yathokte tu dharmadharmiviśeṣa iṣṭa evānanvayadoṣaḥ । yadāha — ātmā paraścetso 'siddha iti । tasyaiva ceṣṭasya vighātakṛdviruddhaḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.2.1.iv>

[II,013,ii]

tadapi na sādhyamanuktatvāditi cet , yadvivādena sādhanamupanyastaṃ taccenna sādhyam , kimidānīṃ sādhyam । tathā ca viparyayasiddhirvaiphalyameva vā । yathā prāksañjñinābhisambandhādarthavacchabdarūpaṃ vibhaktidarśanātsādhyam । na ca svarūpamātrārthavat । arthavacca । tato bāhyenārthenārthavattvamaniṣṭaṃ syāt । tathā parārthāścakṣurādayaḥ saṅghātatvātsiddhā <II,014> api pārārthyāviśeṣe nātmārthāḥ । saṃhataparārthakriyopagamādeṣāṃ sādhanavaiphalyam ॥

[II,014,i]

tasmādanukto 'pīcchayā vyāptaḥ sādhyaḥ । tadvaikalyādayaśca dṛṣṭāntādidoṣāḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.2.2>

<§ 3.II.2.2.2.i>

[II,014,ii]

etena sadvitīyaprayogeṣu niranvayadoṣo vyākhyātaḥ , yathā — abhivyaktacaitanyaśarīralakṣaṇapuruṣaghaṭānyatarasadvitīyo ghaṭaḥ , anutpalatvāt , kuḍyavaditi । tathābhūtena puruṣeṇa sadvitīyatvāsiddheḥ kuḍyasya ॥

<§ 3.II.2.2.2.ii>

[II,014,iii]

atha sāmānyena sādhyamiṣṭamiti na viśeṣākṣepaḥ । uktamatra — tadanākṣepe kiṃ sādhanaphalam , aniṣṭaṃ ceti । yadi ca na viṣayīkṛtameva tatsādhanena , kathamatastatsiddhiḥ । sidhyanvā kathamaviṣayaḥ । viṣa<II,015>yaścet , svāśrayāṃ doṣagatiṃ kathaṃ na spṛśet । sa ca nāma tadāśrayāṃ siddhiṃ sādhanādupajīvati , na paro dūṣaṇamiti vyaktamiyaṃ rājakulasthitiḥ । tasmādyāvatīmarthagatiṃ sādhanaṃ sāmarthyena vyāpnoti siddherākṣepāt , tāvatīṃ taddūṣaṇamapi ॥

<§ 3.II.2.2.2.iii>

[II,015,i]

tathāvidhasya ca dehasya ghaṭādarthāntarabhāvānabhyupagame sāmānyenāpi sādhanaṃ na sambhavati , anyatarārthāntarabhāvābhāvāt । dvayorhi tathābhāvasambhave 'nyataroktiḥ samarthā bhavati , yathā — devadattayajñadattayoranyataraṃ bhojayeti , naikasya bhojanāsambhave 'nākāṅkṣāyāṃ vā । ito 'pi nānyatarārthāntarabhāvaḥ , ghaṭasya svato 'rthāntarabhāvasyānabhyupagamādvirodhācca deha evārthāntarabhūta iti sāmarthyena vākyārthavyavasthāpanādapārthakamanyataragrahaṇam । anyathā vipratiṣiddhametadvacanaṃ syāt , ghaṭasyātmanā tadbhāvārthāntarabhāvavirodhāt । yadi dehādevārthāntarabhāvaḥ syāt , sa eva tathocyeta । anyataravacana<II,016>sāmarthyāddhaṭasyāpi sa iti virodhaḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.2.2.iv>

[II,016,i]

itaśca na sāmānyāśrayaḥ , sarvavyaktisambhavābhāve tatsāmānyāyogāt , yathā'brāhmaṇāditve varṇatvasyaindriyakatvasyeva vā nitīraṇājñāne । tathā hi na taccākṣuṣaṃ tajjñānavat , tadarthāpratipatteḥ , tadvikārānanukārāt , tadabhāve bhāvācca । tathā śrāvaṇādyapīti naindriyam । tathā ghaṭaśarīrayoranyataradarthāntarabhūtamiti sāmānyenānyatarārthāntarabhāvastayorekasya tathābhyupagame syāt । sa ca na śarīrasya , ananvayaśaṅkayā , na ghaṭasya , virodhāditi sāmānyenāpi na sambhavati । asti nāmedṛśasya sambhavaḥ — devadattayajñadattayoranyataro bhojanīyaḥ , na devadatto na yajñadatta iti । na devadatta evetyabhiprāyādadoṣa iti cet , na , anyataragrahaṇenāprasaṅgāt । tasmādidamanyataragrahaṇamekaparigrahe 'pyavirodhe samarthaṃ bhavati , yathānyatarabhojanacodanāyāmekabhojane । vikalpaviṣayatvādasya । tatra hi ghaṭenaiva sadvitīyo dehenaiva veti neṣyate । <II,017> vidherayogācca dvayorekasya vidhīyamānasya vikalpasamuccayāyoge kimidānīṃ vidheḥ sāmarthyamiti riktā vācoyuktiḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.2.2.v>

[II,017,i]

etena pakṣasapakṣānyataratvamapi pratyuktam । api ca dvayorapi sambhavāvirodha etadevaṃ syāt । anyathā tvasiddhameva tacchabde । tathā hi pakṣa eva sa tathāvidhaḥ śabdaḥ , na pakṣasapakṣayoranyataraḥ , vikalpaikapratiniyamayorvirodhāt ॥

<§ 3.II.2.2.2.vi>

[II,017,ii]

sāmānyena vihiteṣvapyartheṣu sāmarthyādviśeṣasthiteśca deha eva pratyayaḥ , na ghaṭe । yathā ko 'pyāyāta iti na parvate vṛkṣe vā śaṅkā bhavati । na hi viśeṣaśabdasannidhireva sāmānyaśabdānāṃ viśeṣāvasthitihetuḥ , api tu prakaraṇasāmarthyādikamapīti ॥

<§ 3.II.2.2.2.vii>

[II,017,iii]

tasmānnānyataratsāmānyenārthāntarabhūtam , arthāntarabhūtadvayāyogāt । na vā kaścidarthāntarabhūtaḥ , dvayorekasyāpyanabhyupagamāt । śabdaghaṭabhedena kalpane 'nityatāyāmapi tulyamiti cet , na , siddhayā<II,018>nityatayā tadvataḥ śabdasya sādhanāt । tathā kasyacidarthāntarabhūtasyopagame syādanyatarārthāntarabhāvaḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.2.3>

[II,018,i]

eteneṣṭasādhyatvavacanena dharmidharmābhyāṃ viśiṣṭau dharmadharmiṇau nirākurvanpratyākhyātaḥ , yathā — nānityaśabdaḥ śabdo na śabdānityatvavānveti , samudāyāpavādasya dharmiṇyavirodhāt । anityo hi śabdaḥ , nānityaśabdaḥ śabdaḥ । tadbhāveṣṭau nānityaḥ śabdaḥ syāt , śabde 'nityaśabdatvaprasādhanāt , anityaśabdaḥ śabdaḥ syāt । sa ca neṣṭa iti neṣṭavighātaḥ kaścit ॥

[II,018,ii]

tasmātkevala eva dharmo dharmiṇi sādhyo viparyāsanīyo vā । tatheṣṭasamudāyasya siddhirvighāto vā kṛto bhavati । sarvatra hi tatsamudāyaviparyāsādeva viruddhaḥ । sa kadāciddharmamukhena dharmimukhena ta<II,019>dviśeṣamukhena vā kriyata iti tena vyapadiśyate ॥

<§ 3.II.2.3>

<§ 3.II.2.3.1>

[II,019,i]

svayaṃśrutiḥ punarekasya dharmiṇaḥ śāstre nānādharmavyavasthāyāmapi svayamātmanaiveṣṭaḥ sādhyaḥ , śāstropagame 'pi netara iti darśanārthā । tatra sarvānyeṣṭanirākaraṇe 'pyāśaṅkāsthānavāraṇaṃ svavṛttau svayaṃśruterāha sūtrakāraḥ — svayamiti śāstrānapekṣamabhyupagamaṃ darśayatīti ॥

<§ 3.II.2.3.2>

<§ 3.II.2.3.2.i>

[II,019,ii]

śāstropagamātsarvastaddṛṣṭaḥ sādhya iti syādāśaṅkāsambhavaḥ । vipratipattistu dṛśyata eva । bhavatyeva śāstradṛṣṭaṃ sādhyam , tatprabādhane ca hetupratijñayordoṣa ityeke । teṣāṃ kṛtakatvena śabdanāśe sādhye gandhe pṛthivīguṇatvaviparyāsanāddheturviruddhaḥ syāt । aprakaraṇānneti cet , <II,020> tadanyatrāpi samānam । na , atra dharmiṇaḥ prakṛtatvāditi cet , na , dharmiprakrame 'pi vastupratibandhābhāvāt । kevalaṃ śāstropagamadvāreṇaiṣāmanuṣaṅgaḥ , sa ca sarvatra tulya iti nānayorbhedaḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.3.2.ii>

[II,020,i]

atha vādino 'pīṣṭiṃ sādhayetsādhyadharmavat , sādhyasamudāyaikadeśaviśeṣatvāt । na sādhyasamudāyaikadeśaviśeṣa ityevāprakaraṇecchā bhavati , tadbhāvāparityāgādarthasyecchāpravṛttyoravirāmaprasaṅgāt । tasmādiyaṃ kutaścitprakaraṇādbhavantī tenaiva gamyate । tāmaprakaraṇāmapi viparītānubhavapratiṣiddhavṛttiṃ balādastīti sādhayannadhyakṣaviruddhamācarati ॥

[II,020,ii]

	kaiścitprakaraṇairicchā bhavetsā gamyate ca taiḥ /
	balāttaveccheyamiti vyaktamīśvaraceṣṭitam // <3.7>
	vadannakāliṅgo tāṃ vyabhicāreṇa bādhyate /
<II,021>
	anāntarīyake cārthe bādhite 'nyasya kā kṣatiḥ // <3.8>
	uktaṃ ca nāgamāpekṣamanumānaṃ svagocare /
	siddhaṃ tena susiddhaṃ tanna tadā śāstramīkṣyate // <3.9>
	vādatyāgastadā syāccenna tadānabhyupāyataḥ /
	upāyo hyabhyupāye 'yamanaṅgaṃ sa tadāpi san // <3.10>
	tathā viśuddhe viṣayadvaye śāstraparigraham /
	cikīrṣoḥ sa hi kālaḥ syāttadā śāstreṇa bādhanam // <3.11>
	tadvirodhena cintāyāstatsiddhārtheṣvayogataḥ /
	tṛtīyasthānasaṅkrāntau nyāyyaḥ śāstraparigrahaḥ // <3.12>
	tatrāpi sādhyadharmasya sambaddhasyaiva bādhanam /
	parihāryaṃ na cānyeṣāmanavasthāprasaṅgataḥ // <3.13>
	keneyaṃ sarvacintāsu śāstraṃ grāhyamiti sthitiḥ /
	kṛtedānīmasiddhāntairgrāhyo dhūmena nānalaḥ // <3.14>
<II,022>
	yadi sādhana ekatra sarvaṃ śāstraṃ nidarśane /
	darśayetsādhanaṃ syādityeṣā lokottarā sthitiḥ // <3.15>
	asambaddhasya dharmasya kimasiddhau na sidhyati /
	hetustatsādhanāyoktaḥ kiṃ duṣṭastatra sidhyati // <3.16>
	dharmānanupanīyaiva dṛṣṭānte dharmiṇo 'khilān /
	vāgdhūmāderjano 'nveti caitanyadahanādikam // <3.17>
	svabhāvaṃ kāraṇaṃ vārtho 'vyabhicāreṇa sādhayan /
	kasyacidvādabādhāyāṃ svabhāvānna nivartate // <3.18>
	prapadyamānaścānyastaṃ nāntarīyakamīpsitaiḥ /
	sādhyārthairhetunā tena kathamapratipāditaḥ // <3.19>
	yadi kiñcitkvacicchāstre na yuktaṃ pratiṣidhyate /
	bruvāṇo yuktamapyanyaditi rājakulasthitiḥ // <3.20>
	sarvānarthānsamīkṛtya vaktuṃ śakyaṃ na sādhanam /
	sarvatra tenotsanneyaṃ sādhyasādhanasaṃsthitiḥ // <3.21>
<II,023>
ityantaraślokāḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.3.2.iii>

[II,023,i]

tasmātsādhyabādhaka eva viruddhaḥ । abādhyabādhakayorekataḥ siddhiraviruddhāpi śāstrabādhāyāṃ yadi viruddheṣyate , sānyaviṣaye 'pi tulyeti viruddhaḥ syāt । tena tatraiva bādhane bhavati , nānyatreti cet , na , hetoḥ sarvasya guṇadoṣayoḥ svasādhye cintyatvāt । tasya svasādhyānuparodhe 'pi śāstroparodhādvirodhe so 'nyakṛte 'pi tulya iti virodhaḥ syāt । bhavatyevānyakṛte 'pi pratijñādoṣa iti cet , astu , viṣayāntare 'pi kiṃ na bhavati । bādhanīyadharmaṇo dharmiṇo 'bhidhānādihaiva bhavati , nānyatreti cet , bādhanīyārthasya śāstrasyopagamādanyatrāpyastu । tasmānnedaṃ pratijñādoṣalakṣaṇaṃ nyāyyam , atiprasaṅgāt ॥

<§ 3.II.2.3.3>

<§ 3.II.2.3.3.i>

[II,023,ii]

api ca śāstropagamātsarvaḥ śāstradṛṣṭaḥ sādhyatvenepsitaścet , asiddhahetvabhidhānamapi pratijñā syāt । nipātavacanena sādhanatveneṣṭasya <II,024> pratikṣepādadoṣa iti cet , na , nyāyaprāptasya sādhyasya vacanena nivartayitumaśakyatvāt ॥

<§ 3.II.2.3.3.ii>

<§ 3.II.2.3.3.ii.a>

[II,024,i]

pakṣalakṣaṇabāhyārthaḥ svayaṃśabdo 'pi nārthaṃ kañcana puṣṇāti । śāstreṣvicchayā pravṛttyartha iti cet , kutaḥ punariyaṃ śaṅkā , yena tadarthaṃ yatnaḥ kriyate । so 'nivāritaḥ pramāṇena pravartamānaḥ kena nivartyate । nivārito vā pramāṇena vācā kena pravartyate ॥

<§ 3.II.2.3.3.ii.b>

[II,024,ii]

samayalakṣaṇāhitabhedasya dharmiṇaḥ parihāreṇa prasiddhadharmiparigrahārthāṃ svayaṃśrutimaparaḥ prāha । tatrāpi vicāraprastāvādevāśrayaḥ prasiddhaḥ siddha iti na kiñcidetat । na hi svecchākalpitabhedeṣvanarthatantropayogiṣu padārtheṣu vyavasthāmuparacayankaścinnivāryate । na hi tathoparacito 'prasiddharūpasāmānyo viśeṣāśrayaṃ vicāramāśrayate ॥

<II,025>

<§ 3.II.2.3.3.ii.c>

[II,025,i]

atha prasiddhāpadeśena dharmiṇaḥ siddhasyāsādhyatāmāha । na , svarūpeṇaiva nirdeśya ityanenaiva gatatvāt । siddhasādhanarūpeṇa hi nirdeśasambhave sādhyatvenaiva nirdeśya itīdaṃ phalavatsyāt । svayaṃsiddhasya dharmiṇaḥ parigrahāvacane dharmiṇameva sādhyaṃ kuryāditi cet , na , anumānasya sāmānyaviṣayatvenaiva gatārthatvāt । dharmisattāyāṃ sādhyāyāṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ sādhyaṃ syāt , tacca pratikṣiptamiti nātraivamavacane 'pi pakṣe kiñcidvirudhyate । atha dharmiṇameva sādhyaṃ kuryāt , tataḥ kiṃ syāt । aśakyametat । kasmāt । hetorviśeṣeṇānvayābhāvāt । nanvayaṃ hetudṛṣṭāntayordoṣaḥ , na pakṣasya , uttarāvayavāpekṣatvāt । anyathā sarve hetvādidoṣāḥ pakṣadoṣāḥ syuḥ । sarvatra pakṣasyaivoparodhāt । tasmāttanmātrānuṣaṅgiṇa eva pakṣadoṣāḥ , pratyakṣādivirodhavat ॥

[II,025,ii]

	hetvādilakṣaṇairbādhyaṃ muktvā pakṣasya lakṣaṇam /
	ucyate parihārārthamavyāptivyatirekayoḥ // <3.22>
<II,026>
	svayaṃnipātarūpākhyā vyatirekasya bādhikāḥ /
	sahānirākṛteneṣṭaśrutiravyāptibādhanī // <3.23>
	sādhyābhyupagamaḥ pakṣalakṣaṇaṃ teṣvapakṣatā /
	nirākṛte bādhanataḥ śeṣe 'lakṣaṇavṛttitaḥ // <3.24>
	dṛṣṭervipratipattīnāmatrākārṣītsvayaṃśrutim /
	iṣṭākṣatimasādhyatvamanavasthāṃ ca darśayan // <3.25>
ityantaraślokāḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.4>

[II,026,i]

atra svayamiṣṭaśrutibhyāṃ gatārthe 'pyavadhāraṇe kṛtyāntenābhisambandhānmā bhūnnirdekṣyamāṇe 'pi prasaṅga iti tadvyavacchedārthamāha । tenānaṅgamiṣerniṣṭhātra , īpsitapade punaraṅgameva । tayāsiddhahetvādiḥ pratiṣidhyate ॥

<II,027>

<§ 3.II.2.5>

<§ 3.II.2.5.1>

[II,027,i]

etena svayaṃ vādineṣṭasyānumeyatvavacanenāniṣṭasaṃsṛṣṭasyeṣṭasyāpyasādhyatvam , tadbādhāyāṃ cādoṣaḥ pakṣahetvorukto veditavyaḥ , yathāsādhyamabādhanāt । yathākāśaguṇatvaikārthasamavāyyanityatvābhāvamapi sādhayatīti ॥

<§ 3.II.2.5.2>

[II,027,ii]

anenaiva cānumānakāle śāstrānāśrayavacanenāprakaraṇāpannapakṣīkaraṇamapi pratyuktam । yathā'nityaḥ śabdo nityo veti prakaraṇe vyatiriktendriyagrāhyasāmānyaikārthasamavāyyanityatvayuktaḥ śabda iti । sati hi śāstrāśraye tadarthapakṣīkaraṇaṃ yuktaṃ syāt , tadavabodhārthitve vā prativādinaḥ , anyathā'sambaddhapralāpa evāyamityanavadheyaḥ syāt । dvayoranāśritaśāstrayoḥ kasyacitparīkṣāyāṃ kaḥ prastāvo 'prastutapakṣīkaraṇasya ॥

<§ 3.II.2.5.3>

[II,027,iii]

nanu viśeṣasya sāmānyākṣepāttatsiddhau siddhameveṣṭaṃ bhavati । na , pratipattṛvāñchāyāḥ prakaraṇāt । ata eva prakaraṇena sādhyadharmeṣṭi<II,028>gatirityucyate । na hyavaśyaṃ sāmānyārthī viśeṣapratiniyamārthī bhavati , viśeṣāntare vivādāsambhavācca । na ca śāstradvāreṇa vivādaḥ , tadā tasyānāntarīyakatvāt । na caivaṃvidhā dharmāḥ kvacidasamayasthāyinaṃ pratyanvayinaḥ , avyabhicārī vā heturasti । sadvitīyaprayogāśca pratyuktāḥ । śāstrāśraye 'pi prastāvātikrame 'tiprasaṅga uktaḥ । tasmātprakaraṇāpannamevāviśeṣaṇaṃ dharmamātraṃ sādhyamākarṇanīyaṃ vā । anyathārthāntaragamanādavasādaḥ syāt ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6>

<§ 3.II.2.6.1>

<§ 3.II.2.6.1.i>

[II,028,i]

sa cāyaṃ sādhyābhyupagamaḥ
	pratyakṣārthānumānāptaprasiddhanānirākṛtaḥ /
nirdeśyaḥ । yadi nāma nirdeśyaḥ , pratyakṣārthenānumānenāptābhyāṃ prasiddhena cānirākṛto 'bhyupagamo hetumapekṣate । pratyakṣe 'rthagrahaṇamindriyajñānasya kasyacidvitathārthatvāttatparihāreṇa pramāṇaviṣayaparigrahārtham ॥

<II,029>

<§ 3.II.2.6.1.ii>

[II,029,i]

kiṃ punarnirākṛto na pakṣaḥ ।
	sandigdhe hetuvacanādvyasto hetoranāśrayaḥ // <3.26>
vyastaḥ pramāṇābhyāṃ nirākṛto viparyaye pramāṇavṛtteranāśrayaḥ pratipramāṇasya । viruddhayorekatra samyagjñānāyogāt । viṣayopadarśanārthaṃ ca pakṣa ucyate । sa nirākṛte viṣayiṇo 'sambhavādapakṣa eva । tasmātsandigdho hetuvyāpāraviṣayaḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.1.iii>

[II,029,ii]

	anumānasya bhedena sā bādhoktā caturvidhā /
seyaṃ pakṣasya bādhā caturvidhā darśitā vidhānumānaṃ bhittvā ।
	tatrābhyupāyaḥ kāryāṅgaṃ svabhāvāṅgaṃ jagatsthitiḥ // <3.27>
āptavacanaṃ kāryalakṣaṇaṃ liṅgam , svabhāvalakṣaṇaṃ prasiddhiḥ ॥

<II,030>

<§ 3.II.2.6.2>

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.i>

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.i.a>

[II,030,i]

ātmāparo vā yathārthadarśanapravṛttavāgabhimata āptaḥ । tadvacanaṃ nāntareṇārthatathābhāvaṃ pravartata iti kāryaṃ tasya । sa svakāryasaṃsūcitaḥ svaviparyayopagamaṃ pratibadhnāti । tadevaṃ svavacanaṃ śāstraṃ cābhisamasya sāmyādekamuktam । yathātmano 'prāmāṇye vacanasyāpravṛttiḥ , tathā śāstrānāśraye tatprasiddhe vicārasyeti prastāvāśrayatve śāstraṃ bādhakamityamumarthaṃ vaktuṃ svavacanenāsya sahoktiḥ sāmyadṛṣṭaye kṛtā । ata evodāharaṇamapyatra sadṛśamāha — na santi pramāṇāni prameyārthānīti , pramāṇānāmabhāve śāstrasvavacanayorayogāt । svavacanavirodhe spaṣṭamudāharaṇam , āgame tu diṅmātradarśanametat । atrodāharaṇam — pretyāsukhaprado dharma iti ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.i.b>

[II,030,ii]

dharmivyavasthitestadāśrayāttatprabādhane 'dhikaraṇapratyastamayānna viśeṣa<II,031>cintāpravṛttirityavaśyamevaṃvidhe viṣaye śāstraṃ pramāṇayitavyam । kathamidānīṃ na tīrthasnānādiradharmaśodhana iti nābhyupetabādhā । sarveṣāmadṛṣṭapratipattiśāstrāṇāmevamavacanānna pratiṣedhe doṣaḥ । svopagamāśrayaṃ hi śāstraṃ virundhāno vihanyate , nāparam , anabhyupagamāt । tasyāpi snānācchuddhivādinaḥ śāstrasya svavacanenāpyasyārthasya pratibādhanāt । lobhādimūlo 'dharma iti sarvaśāstreṣu vyavasthā , alubdhādviṣṭāmūḍhānāṃ pāpānabhyupagamāt । sā vyavasthā snānādīnāṃ pāpaśodhanavādaṃ bādhate , nidānāpraśamanena nidānino 'vicchedāt , madhuraśītalasnigdhairiva vyādheḥ ślaiṣmikasyeti । ata eva śāstradṛṣṭeṣvartheṣu virodhodbhāvanaprāyā cintā । yacchāstraṃ vastubalapravṛttena pramāṇena svavacanena cābādhitaṃ dṛśyādṛśyayorviṣayayoḥ । tadgrāhyamiti ॥

<II,032>

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.i.c>

[II,032,i]

śāstravato 'pyatadālambane vastuni viruddhoktāvapi na bādhā , pratibandhastu syāt , dvayostulyakakṣatvāt , yathā svavacane । tadā cāsya svavacanena virodhaḥ , na śāstreṇa । tayoryasya pramāṇamasti , tadaparasya bādhakaṃ bhavati । anyathā kathaṃ pratijñāṃ tulyakakṣyāmanumānaṃ vā yathārthamapetayuktikā pratijñā bādheta । pratiṣiddhaṃ cāgamānāṃ prāmāṇyam । tasmādabhyupetya vicāreṣvayaṃ doṣaḥ ॥

[II,032,ii]

ata eva viṣayabhedapradarśanārthaṃ pṛthakkṛto 'numānādabahirbhūto 'pyabhyupāyaḥ , bādhanābhyupagamāt । anyathātiprasaṅgaḥ syāt , vyarthatā vā pṛthakkaraṇasya । svavacanasyāpi pṛthakkaraṇanimittaṃ vāṅmātravacane pratibandhaḥ ॥

[II,032,iii]

apramāṇatvaṃ śāstre 'pi tulyamiti tatrāpi pratibandho 'stu । pratibandho hyadhikaraṇe sati bhavati , yathā siddhe vacane prāmāṇyetarayoranyonyam , <II,033> siddhāyāṃ vā yoṣiti prasavetaradharmatvayoḥ sa dharmagataḥ । yatra tu dharmyevāsiddhastatra kva kena kiṃ pratibadhyate , prastāvasyaivābhāvāt । tasmāddharmiṇaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayañśāstraṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati । tatastadbādhakamiti ॥

[II,033,i]

tattarhi śāstramapramāṇakaṃ kathaṃ dharmiṇaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati । prāmāṇyenābhyupagamāt । svopagama eva tarhi prāmāṇyamādadhaddharmiṇaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati । dharmāntaraṃ ca sa eva punaḥ prativahatīti na bhidyate svavacanavirodhācchāstravirodhaḥ । tataḥ pratibandha eva , na bādhā ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.i.d>

[II,033,ii]

kastarhīdānīmanayorbhedaḥ । na kaścit । kathaṃ tarhi pṛthagvacanam । vākyabhedādetatsyāt । pūrveṇa pratiṣṭhāpitamuttaraṃ pratihantītyabhyupagamavirodhaḥ । ata eva pūrvābhyupagamenetyāha । tadeva vākyaṃ svārthaṃ virundhānaṃ svavāgviruddham , yathā — nānumānaṃ pramāṇamiti ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.i.e>

[II,033,iii]

pratibandho 'pi kathamapramāṇasya । ata eva tulyakakṣatvāt । yadi hi ta<II,034>traikasya prāmāṇyaṃ syātsiddhireva , na pratibandhaḥ , pramāṇenāpramāṇasya bādhanāt । tenopagamātpramāṇaṃ sarvavastuṣu śāstraṃ bādhakameveti cet , kathaṃ punarupagamāviśeṣa ekaṃ pramāṇaṃ bādhakaṃ ca nāparamiti yatkiñcidetat । puruṣecchākṛtā cāsya paripūrṇā pramāṇatā ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.i.f>

[II,034,i]

yadi svavacanābhyupagamavirodhayoḥ pratibandho doṣaḥ , tathāpyato 'rthasaṃśaya eva । so 'navadyapakṣanirdeśe 'pi tulya iti kathaṃ pakṣadoṣaḥ । na vai tadvacanādaniścayotpatterdṛṣṭavacanaḥ , kiṃ tarhi yadyāvatā vacanena samarthanīyaṃ tasyāsamarthanāt । sambhavī svābhiprāyaḥ pratijñāvacanena darśanīyaḥ । sa ca yathā pramāṇabādhāyāṃ na sambhavati , tathaikatra viruddhayorupasaṃhāre 'pi । vacanaguṇadoṣau hi parārthe 'numāne 'dhikriyete , nārthasya , vakturupālambhādayathārthābhidhānena ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.i.g>

[II,034,ii]

yadi svavacanopagamavirodhayorna kaścidbhedaḥ , kastarhi viṣayabhedaḥ pūrvopagamavirodhasya । yatrānāśrite kasmiṃścitsamaye na pravartate vicāraḥ , so <II,035> 'vaśyamāśrayaṇīyaḥ , nāntarīyakatvāditi sa eva tasya pratibandhaviṣayaḥ , sarvatra svavāgviruddhābhidhānam । atrāpi ko 'yamavaśyaṃ parāśrayaḥ । sa eva tamarthaṃ paramukhena vyavasthāpya punarvyutthāpayatīti ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.ii>

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.ii.a>

[II,035,i]

prasiddhiḥ khalvapi virodhinaṃ pratijñārthaṃ bādhate , puruṣecchānurodhino 'rtheṣvaśakyapratiṣedhatvādiṣṭaśabdābhidheyatvasya । sa dharmo vyavahārajaḥ prasiddhiśabdenoktaḥ । yogyaṃ hi viśvaṃ svabhāvataḥ kṛtākṛtānāṃ śabdānām , icchāmātravṛtteḥ । tayārthamātrānurodhinyā bhāvinyā bhūtayā vā śabdayogyatayā tāṃ pratirundhāno bādhyate ॥

[II,035,ii]

tadyogyatābalādeva vastuto ghaṭito 'syāṃ sarvaḥ śabda ityapratīte 'pi tasmiṃstatsiddhatāmāha — yatrāpyasādhāraṇatvādanumānābhāve śābdaprasiddhena viruddhenārthenāpodyate , na sa pakṣa iti ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.ii.b>

[II,035,iii]

tata eva bādhāhetorasādhāraṇatvam , kvacidacandre 'siddheḥ । aśakya<II,036>niṣedhatāmasya darśayannevamāha , apratipramāṇatayā niścayaṃ vā । tanniṣedho hyanumānātsyāt , pratyakṣeṇa yogyatā'niścayāt । tatra ca sarvahetūnāmasādhāraṇatā , yatra sattvameva nānvayītyudāharaṇamevamphalam ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.ii.c>

[II,036,i]

saṅketāśrayāḥ śabdāḥ , sa cecchāmātrāśrayaḥ । tannāsiddhiḥ śabdasiddhānāmiti darśayan , śābdaprasiddhenetyāha । śaṅkitapratibandhānāṃ saṃśayādasiddheḥ , ciramadṛṣṭānāmapi punaḥ pratibhotpattidṛṣṭeḥ sati sambhave tadabhāvasya puruṣamātreṇāniścayāt , ataḥ pramāṇānniścayābhidhānādanumānaviṣaye viruddhāvyabhicāriṇo 'sambhavamarthāpattyā darśayati ॥

[II,036,ii]

etena pratyakṣānumāne vyākhyāte , dvayorapi prāmāṇyāviśeṣāt । ekasya tallakṣaṇayoge 'pi pratidvandvidarśanātpratyakṣasyāpyevambhāvaḥ syāt । na ca pramāṇalakṣaṇavyatirikto 'nyo 'sti viśeṣaḥ pratyakṣasya , ya <II,037> ekāntasādhanatvaṃ vyavasthāpayati , yatastadviśeṣabahirbhāvādapramāṇamanumānaṃ syāt । ekasaṅkhyāvivakṣayāpradarśitapratidvandvinaḥ prāmāṇyādadoṣa iti cet , asti nāmedṛśasya viniścaye sambhavo nāsya pratidvandvī vidyata iti । aviśiṣṭalakṣaṇe dṛṣṭasyāparatra vyatirekaniścayasya kartumaśakyatvādityuktam । na ca puruṣapratibhāvaśātpramāṇayorlakṣaṇamucyate , kiṃ tarhi vastusthityā । sā caivamaśakyaniścayeti na tatsandigdhalakṣaṇaṃ vyavahārayogyam , pakṣadharmatvādisandehavat । lakṣaṇe jñānagrahaṇācca । uktalakṣaṇe 'numāne tallakṣaṇasya pratiyogino 'sambhavādasambhavo 'numāne viruddhāvyabhicāriṇaḥ । tadekasaṅkhyāvivakṣāpyatra viṣaye neṣṭaiva । viṣayaṃ cāsyā nivedayiṣyāmaḥ । tadevaṃ pramāṇe bādhake bruvāṇastato niścayamāha । tataḥ sapratipakṣasambhāvanāmastaṅgamayati । tato <II,038> 'numānaviṣaye viruddhāvyabhicāriṇo 'bhāvaṃ sūcayatīti ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.ii.d>

[II,038,i]

atha vā lokasya bruvato 'numānābhāvamāha । tena bhinnaviṣayā pratītiranumānādityuktaṃ bhavati । tenānumānādvastusadasattānurodhino bhinnaviṣayāyāḥ pratīterna vastuvaśādvṛttiriti sūcitaṃ bhavati । sa hi śaśinaścandratvamanicchankāmanyāṃ pratītimicchediti taṃ pratyadṛṣṭāntamanumānam । tenāsādhāraṇamāha ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.ii.e>

[II,038,ii]

yasmānnaitadevaikamudāharaṇamadhikṛtyedamucyate , sarvapratītivirodhānāṃ sāmānyena lakṣaṇatvāt । tathā na vṛkṣaḥ śiṃśapetyuktāvapi bādhanāt । atrāpi loke karpūrarajatādiṣu dṛṣṭatvānnāsādhāraṇatā syāt । na ca samayādvartamānasya kācidasādhāraṇatā । yadi hi tasya kvacitsi<II,039>dhyet , siddhaṃ vastubalena tat , pratītisiddhābhyupagame śaśinyapyanivāraṇāt । tadvastuni siddhaṃ śaśinyapyanivāryameva । tadvastvabhāve śaśini nivāraṇe 'pi na kaściddoṣaḥ । tasmādavastuniyatasaṅketaśabdabhāvināṃ dharmāṇāṃ yogyāḥ sarvapadārthāḥ , icchāyā nirodhābhāvāt ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.ii.f>

[II,039,i]

etena saṅketānuvidhāyināṃ śabdānāṃ na kaścidarthaniyamaḥ , atra caiṣāṃ pratiṣedhe virodha ityuktaṃ bhavati ॥

[II,039,ii]

	naimittikyāḥ śruterarthamarthaṃ vā pāramārthikam /
	śabdānāṃ pratirundhāno na bādhyastena varṇitaḥ // <3.28>
	tasmādviṣayabhedasya darśanāya pṛthakkṛtā /
	anumānābahirbhūtā pratītirapi pūrvavat // <3.29>
ityantaraślokau ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.iii>

[II,039,iii]

pratyakṣavirodhe 'pi nānārūpasya yadeva śrutau rūpaṃ pratibhāsate <II,040> 'dvayaṃ sambandhyantarābhāvācchabalābhāsāyā buddheradṛṣṭeḥ । tasyaiva pratikṣepe virodhaḥ , yathā — aśrāvaṇaḥ śabda iti । tadarthā cārthoktiḥ ॥

[II,040,i]

	tadeva rūpaṃ tatrārthaḥ śeṣaṃ vyāvṛttilakṣaṇam /
	avasturūpaṃ sāmānyamatastannākṣagocaraḥ // <3.30>
	tena sāmānyadharmāṇāmapratyakṣatvasiddhitaḥ /
	pratikṣepe 'pyabādheti śrāvaṇoktyā prakāśitam // <3.31>
	sarvathā'vācyarūpatvātsiddhyā tasya samāśrayāt /
	bādhanāttadbalenoktaḥ śrāvaṇenākṣagocaraḥ // <3.32>
ityantaraślokāḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.iv>

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.iv.a>

[II,040,ii]

anumānavirodhe 'pi , yathā — nityo ghaṭa iti । abhighātasahatvaṃ paśyato bhrāntyaitatsyāt । tacca dṛṣṭāvarugṇaghaṭavadutpattyāderna sambhavati ॥

[II,040,iii]

na kaścidanityo ghaṭaḥ , tatrāpi vyaktitirodhānāditi cet , a<II,041>tādavasthyamanityatāṃ brūmaḥ , tādavasthyaṃ ca tattvam । tadavarugṇe 'sti , vināśāttirodhānādveti nātra nirbandhaḥ । taccopalabhyamadhyarūpaṃ pūrvāparayoḥ koṭyorastīti bruvāṇaḥ padārthavyavasthāṃ bādhate । sattvarajastamasāṃ caitanyasya caivaṃ paraspararūpavivekena vyavasthā'yogāt । na hi tatrāpyanupalambhamantareṇānyaḥ kaścidvyavasthāśrayaḥ । tadidamupalabhyalakṣaṇaṃ dadhyādi kṣīrādiṣvanupalabhyamānaṃ kṣīraṃ vā tatra nāstīti nyāyya eṣaḥ ॥

<§ 3.II.2.6.2.iv.b>

[II,041,i]

astyevopalambho dadhyādīnāṃ kṣīrādiṣvanumānam , aśaktādanutpatteḥ । na tādṛśāṃ bhāvo 'numānaviṣayaḥ । sa hi sandṛśya eva bhavati । sa cedbhavenmadhyāvasthāvadupalabhyeta । tallakṣaṇatyāga eva hi tasya vināśaḥ , aparabhāvaśca vailakṣaṇyam , viruddhasvabhāvalakṣaṇatvādbhedasyetyuktaprāyam । tasmādutpattestatkāraṇasya tajjananasvabhāvaḥ sidhyet , na tadbhāvaḥ ॥

[II,041,ii]

yadyasata utpattiḥ kiṃ na kṣīrācchaśaviṣāṇam , ko hi viśeṣo 'bhā<II,042>vāviśeṣa iti cet , na , hetoḥ svabhāvabhedāt । atadātmatve 'pi kṣīrasya sa tasya svabhāvaḥ , yo dadhijanano na śaśaviṣāṇajananaḥ । sa tasya kuta iti cet , svahetusamuttha ityanādihetuprakṛtiparamparā । tasmāttajjananasvabhāvasya hetorabhāvācchaśaviṣāṇānutpattiḥ , tadbhāvāditarasyeti ॥

[II,042,i]

atha keyaṃ śaktiḥ । sa eva bhāva utānyadeva kiñcit । sa eva cet , tathaivopalabhyeta , viśeṣābhāvāt । viśeṣe coktam । anyaccet , kathamanyabhāve so 'sti , upacāramātraṃ tu syāt । etenāparabhāvaḥ pratyukta iti ॥ ॥

<II,043>

{3.III}

<§ 3.§ 3.3.1>

[II,043,i]

pakṣadharmaprabhedena sukhagrahaṇārthaṃ hetuprakaraṇasya sūtrasaṅkṣepa ucyate —
	sapakṣe sannasandvedhā pakṣadharmaḥ punastridhā /
	pratyekamasapakṣe 'pi sadasadvividhatvataḥ // <3.33>

<§ 3.3.1.1>

[II,043,ii]

pakṣo dharmī । prayojanābhāvādanupacāra iti cet , na , sarvadharmidharmapratiṣedhārthatvāt । tadekadeśatvāttadupacārayogyadharmipratipattyartham । tathā ca cākṣuṣatvādiparihāraḥ ॥

[II,043,iii]

dharmavacanenāpi dharmyāśrayasiddhau dharmigrahaṇasāmarthyātpratyāsattyā sādhyadharmisiddhiriti cet , na , dṛṣṭāntadharmiṇo 'pi pratyāsatteḥ । sapakṣe sattvavacanena dṛṣṭāntadharmiṇi sattvasiddherdharmidharmavacanātsādhyadharmiparigrahaḥ । karaṇīyo 'yaṃ vyākhyāne yatnaḥ sa pakṣavacanena samāhitaḥ । sāmarthyādarthagatau pratipattigauravaṃ ca parihṛtaṃ bhavati ॥

<II,044>

[II,044,i]

pakṣasya dharmatve tadviśeṣaṇāpekṣasyānyatrānanuvṛtterasādhāraṇateti cet , na , ayogavyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt , yathā — caitro dhanurdharaḥ , nānyayogavyavacchedena , yathā — pārtho dhanurdhara ityuktaprāyam ॥

<§ 3.3.1.2>

[II,044,ii]

sa eṣa pakṣadharmastridhā bhidyate — sapakṣe sannasandvedhā ceti । sa trividhaḥ pratyekaṃ punastridhā bhavati — asapakṣe sannasandvedhā cetyevam ॥

<§ 3.3.1.3>

[II,044,iii]

sādhyadharmasāmānyena samāno 'rthaḥ sapakṣaḥ । tadabhāvo 'sapakṣaḥ ॥

[II,044,iv]

kathamidānīmabhāve sannityucyate । na vai tanniṣedhamātramasapakṣaḥ , kiṃ tarhi sarvaḥ pratiyogī niṣedhaḥ paryudastaśca , atattvalakṣaṇatvādasapakṣasya । tadvivakṣite pratiyogini ca tulyam , vyatirekagateḥ sarvatra tulyatvātsākṣādarthāpattyā vā ॥

<II,045>

<§ 3.3.1.4>

<§ 3.3.1.4.1>

[II,045,i]

tasyāsya pakṣadharmasya tattvaṃ sapakṣavipakṣayoḥ sadasattvaṃ ca yathāyogaṃ hetvādiṣu yathāsvaṃ pratipattisādhanairniścitaṃ grāhyam , sandigdhaviparyastarūpayoriṣṭāniṣṭaprakāśanayorapratipattisādhanatvāt , viparītasandigdhapratipattiśrutivat ॥

<§ 3.3.1.4.2>

<§ 3.3.1.4.2.i>

[II,045,ii]

anaikāntikasya tu pakṣadharmatvameva , asambaddhādvimarśāyogāt । na tu sapakṣavipakṣayoḥ sattvamasattvaṃ vā niścayāpekṣam , niścaye 'pi sandehamukhenaiva doṣāt । so 'niścaye 'pi tulya iti tathāvidhodbhāvanamapyatra dūṣaṇameva । anyatra tu saṃśaye dvayorekasya vā viparyaye caikasya na sādhanaṃ na dūṣaṇam । tathāpratipattyaṅgasyāsāmarthyāt ॥

<§ 3.3.1.4.2.ii>

[II,045,iii]

asādhāraṇo 'pyubhayavyāvṛtterniścayāyogāt , ubhayabahirbhūtasyābhāvāt । ubhayorekatra bhāve ca pratītisādhanābhāvātpravṛttinivṛttyoḥ saṃśa<II,046>yādeva saṃśayahetuḥ , viniścitāparabhāvasamānaguṇapuruṣasambhāvitastrīgarbha iva puruṣeṣu । yathāha — yo hyasādhāraṇaḥ sādhyadharmaḥ , sa yāvatā bhedena sarvasaṅgrahastatra saṃśayahetuḥ , tadvatāṃ tatsaṅgrahādekāntavyāvṛtteśceti । tadvatāṃ tatsaṅgrahāditi prabhedabāhyasyābhāvamāha , yamayaṃ vastudharmastṛtīyamāśrayet । ekāntavyāvṛttyā caikabhāve pratītisādhanābhāvamāha । asya hi dvayasyaikatra samuccayātsarveṣu prabhedeṣu saṃśayaḥ । uktaṃ ca — vyāvṛttiniścaye viśeṣasya vyavacchedahetutāsya kena nivāryata iti ॥

<§ 3.3.1.4.2.iii>

[II,046,i]

niścayahetāvapyapratibhānātsyātsaṃśayaḥ । sa ca naikāntenānaikāntikaḥ । tanniścitatadbhāvo nirdiṣṭaguṇaniścayādevetyaniścito nānaikānti<II,047>kaḥ syāt । na vai vastudharmasamāśrayeṇaiva parārthe 'numāne sādhanadoṣodbhāvanam , api tu vaktṛdoṣeṇāpi , nyūnatānanvayaviparītānvayavat । tena hi nirṇītaguṇe vaktavye 'nyathābhidhānāddoṣa eva । pakṣadharme 'pi tarhi sandehānyatarāsiddherdūṣaṇaṃ syāt । evametat , iṣṭāprāpteḥ । nanu viparyayaprāptirapi naivāsti । na vai viparyayaprāptyaiva dūṣaṇam , kiṃ tarhi sādhanasāmarthyavighātāt । tathā hi na prameyatvādiṣvapi viparyayaprāptirasti , cākṣuṣatve vā ko viparyayaḥ । ubhayasiddhyā nirdeṣṭavyasyānubhayasiddhiḥ । ihāpi tarhi niścayena nirdeṣṭavyasyāniścayo 'stu viparyayaḥ ॥

[II,047,i]

tasmāddhetuviruddhayoreva niścayātsādhanaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ vā ॥

<§ 3.3.1.5>

[II,047,ii]

ta ete nava pakṣadharmā nirdiśyante — prameyatvānnityaḥ , kṛtakatvādanityaḥ , anityatvātprayatnānantarīyakaḥ , kṛtakatvānnityaḥ , sātmakaṃ jīvaccharīraṃ prāṇādimattvāt , prayatnānantarīyakatvānnityaḥ , <II,048> anityatvādaprayatnānantarīyakaḥ , anityaḥ prayatnānantarīyakatvāt , nityo 'sparśatvāditi ॥

<§ 3.3.1.6>

[II,048,i]

kathamasapakṣāpekṣayā bhede 'sato 'nadhikaraṇatvādasattvaṃ sattvaṃ veti cet । uktamatra — yathā'sati niṣedhaḥ , asapakṣaścātattvalakṣaṇa iti । nanvetasminnasapakṣe hetvabhāvaprasaṅgaḥ , sarvasyānyadharmayogāt । na bhavati , yathā — abrāhmaṇa iti । na hi sa eva brāhmaṇastajjātiyogādabrāhmaṇaśca dharmāntarasamāveśālloke pratīyate , kiṃ tarhi vivakṣitadharmānāśrayo vastu । anyaviṣaye 'pi nañi vibhāgena niyogavṛtteḥ । sapakṣalakṣaṇavirodhācca naivaṃ pratītiḥ । sādhyadharmasāmānyena samāna ityatra yadi sādhyadharmasāmānyenaiveti , syāttadā naiva kaści<II,049>tsapakṣaḥ , tathāvidhasyāsambhavāt । tasmādapratikṣiptadharmāntaraṃ sādhyadharmasāmānyaṃ samāviśadghaṭādikaṃ sapakṣayati । tenāsapakṣa iti na sarvānyadharmayogini pratītiḥ । kiṃ tarhi taddharmavirahiṇītyadoṣo 'nyagrahaṇe 'pi ॥

<§ 3.3.2>

[II,049,i]

kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇamevaṃ navadhā pakṣadharmo vibhajyate ।
	svabhāvakāryasiddhyarthaṃ dvau dvau hetuviparyayau /
	vivādādbhedasāmānye śeṣo vyāvṛttisādhanaḥ // <3.34>

<§ 3.3.2.1>

<§ 3.3.2.1.1>

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.i>

[II,049,ii]

svabhāvakāryayorevātmapratibandhādgamakatvaṃ viparyaye vā viparyāsanamiti darśanārthamanityaḥ kṛtakatvātprayatnānantarīyakatvācceti dvau hetū , nityaḥ kṛtakatvātprayatnānantarīyakatvācceti viruddhau dvau ca nirdiṣṭau । na hi svabhāvādanyasya sarvatra sapakṣe sattvam , kāryavyabhicārātkāraṇasya । <II,050> tasmātsapakṣe dvidhāvṛtti kāryam । na hyanityā ityeva sarve prayatnānantarabhāvijñānakāryārambhiṇaḥ । tena tatsapakṣe dvidhā vartate ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.ii>

[II,050,i]

kathamidamavagamyate — prayatnānantarabhāvijñānamanityakāryamiti । prayatnānantaraṃ jñānasya prāksato niyamenāyogāt , prayatnasyāvaraṇendriyaśabdeṣvanupayogāt ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.ii.a>

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.ii.a.1>

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.ii.a.1.1>

[II,050,ii]

na hi tasyopalambhāvaraṇaṃ sambhavati । sato 'pi vā kasyacittadātmānamakhaṇḍayataḥ sāmarthyatiraskārāyogāt । na hi tatrātiśayamanutpādayatkiñcitkaraṃ nāma । akiñcitkaraṃ ca kiṃ kasyāvaraṇamanyadvā ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.ii.a.1.2>

[II,050,iii]

kuḍyādayo ghaṭādīnāṃ kamatiśayamutpādayanti khaṇḍayanti vā , yenāvaraṇamiṣyante । na brūmaḥ — te kiñcidatiśāyayantīti । api tu na sarve ghaṭakṣaṇāḥ sarvasyendriyajñānasya hetavaḥ । parasparasahitāstu viṣayendriyālokāḥ parasparato viśiṣṭakṣaṇāntarotpādādvijñānahetavaḥ । anupakāryasyāpekṣā'yogāt । śaktasvabhāvasya nityaṃ janana<II,051>majananaṃ vānyathā syāt । te cāvyavahitāḥ pratighātinānyenānyonyasyopakāriṇaḥ , avyavadhānadeśayogyatāsahakāritvātteṣām । vyavadhāne hetvabhāvātsamarthakṣaṇāntarānutpatterjñānānutpattiḥ । pūrvotpannasamarthanirodhādvā sati vyavadhāne 'nyasyotpitsoḥ kāraṇābhāve 'nutpatteḥ kāraṇavaikalyājjñānānutpattiriti kuḍyādaya āvaraṇamucyante । na prāgyogyasya pratibandhāt , tasya svabhāvāpracyuteḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.ii.a.1.3>

[II,051,i]

atha vā sambhavatyapi bhāvānāṃ kṣaṇikānāmanyonyopakāraḥ , acintyatvāddhetupratyayasāmarthyasyāsarvavidā । tena yadindriyaviṣayamadhyasthitamāvaraṇam , tau vijñānotpādanavaiguṇyatāratamyenātiśāyayedapi , āvaraṇabhedena śabdādau śrutimāndyapāṭavadarśanāt । anyathā kvacida<II,052>pyakiñcitkarasya sannidhānasyāpyasannidhānatulyatvādasyedamityupasaṃhāro 'pi vikalpanirmita eva syāt , na vastvāśrayaḥ । na ca samāropānuvidhāyinyo 'rthakriyāḥ । na hi māṇavako dahanopacārādādhīyate pāke । tasmātsatyāmapi kalpanāyāmatatparāvṛttayo bhāvā yathāsvabhāvavṛttaya eva । tatsatyapyāvaraṇe jñāpayeyurevendriyādayaḥ , na ca tathā । tasmāttenādheyaviśeṣā iti gamyante ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.ii.a.1.4>

[II,052,i]

na tvevaṃ nityānāṃ śabdānāṃ kasmiṃścitsatyatiśayahānirutpattirvā । tadyadi teṣāṃ jñānajananaḥ svabhāvaḥ , sarvasya sarvadā sarvāṇi svaviṣayāṇi jñānāni janayeyuḥ । na cet , na kadācitkasyacitkiñcidityekānta eṣaḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.ii.a.2>

[II,052,ii]

syādetat , nāvaraṇānnityaṃ sarve śabdā na śrūyante , api tu kiñcideṣāṃ pratipattau sahakāri pratiniyatamastīndriyopakāryanyadvā । tatkadācitkasyacidbhavatīti tatkṛtameṣāṃ kadācitkvacicchravaṇamiti । na <II,053> vai vayaṃ kāraṇānāṃ sahakārīṇi pratikṣipāmaḥ , kiṃ tvapekṣanta eva kāraṇāni tadavasthopakāriṇamartham , tato labhyasyātiśayasya kāryopayogāt । tathā śabdo 'pi yadi kiñcidapekṣya kāryaṃ kuryāt , karotu । pūrvasvabhāvaniyata ityetanna syāt , tasya pracyuteḥ , apekṣyācca prayatnātprayatnasaṃskṛtādindriyādanyato vā svabhāvāntarapratilambhāt । na hyanupakāryapekṣyata ityuktaprāyam । tadupakārasya cārthāntaratve tasyeti sambandhābhāvādayo 'pyuktāḥ । tasya cājñeyatvam , upakārādeva jñānotpatteḥ । tasmādeṣa śabdo nendriyaṃ na sannikarṣaṃ nātmānamanyadvā kiñcijjñānotpattisamāśrayaṃ svavijñānajanane 'pekṣeta , sarvasya tatrākiñcitkaratvāt । etena prayatnasyendriyaśabdopayogātsāphalyaṃ pratyuktam । indriyopakāreṇāpi sahakārikāraṇaṃ śabdasyopasaṃharet । taccānapekṣatvādasya nirastam ॥

<II,054>

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.ii.a.3>

[II,054,i]

tadayamupalabhyasvabhāvaḥ svasmātsvabhāvātkadācinnāpaitīti nityamupalabhyeta । evaṃ hi sa nityaḥ syādyadi na kutaścitsāmarthyaṃ labhyeta pracyaveta vā , tato jñānajananasāmarthyasyānantaratvāt , arthāntaratve ca doṣāt ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.ii.b>

[II,054,ii]

na cāsya prayatnānārambhavirāme kadācidupalambhaḥ । tena tadātmānaṃ pratyasya kaścidupakāraḥ sambhāvyate , kāraṇadharmadarśanāt ॥

[II,054,iii]

ataḥ prayatnānantarabhāvijñānamanityasvabhāvakāraṇakāryamiti siddham ॥

[II,054,iv]

	prayatnānantaraṃ jñānaṃ prāksato niyamena na /
	tasyāvṛtyakṣaśabdeṣu sarvathānupayogataḥ // <3.35>
	kadācinnirapekṣasya kāryākṛtivirodhataḥ /
	kādācitkaphalaṃ siddhaṃ talliṅgaṃ jñānamīdṛśam // <3.36>
iti saṅgrahaślokau ॥

<II,055>

<§ 3.3.2.1.1.iii>

[II,055,i]

etenaivodāharaṇena nidarśite 'pi hetulakṣaṇaviṣaye svabhāvasya pṛthakkaraṇaṃ kāryodāharaṇātsarvasya tādātmyapratītirmā bhūditi । vyutpattyarthaṃ ca hetuvacanamuktārthamapyanumāne 'dhikriyate । teneha prabhedamātramākhyātam , lakṣaṇaṃ tu tadeva । etena kāryaliṅgodāharaṇena svabhāvo 'pyekadeśabhāgukto veditavyaḥ । tenaiva ca sadṛśamudāharaṇamāha , prayatnānantaraṃ vyaktijanmanostathābhidhānāt ॥

[II,055,ii]

	yannāntarīyakā sattā yo vātmā svo 'vibhāgavān /
	sa tenāvyabhicārī syādityarthaṃ tatprabhedanam // <3.37>
	saṃyogyādiṣu yeṣvasti pratibandho na tādṛśaḥ /
	na te hetava ityuktaṃ vyabhicārasya sambhavāt // <3.38>
<II,056>
	sati vā pratibandhe 'stu sa eva gatisādhanaḥ /
	niyamo hyavinābhāvo 'niyataśca na sādhanam // <3.39>
ityantaraślokāḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2>

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.i>

[II,056,i]

nanu yathoktalakṣaṇānupalabdhirapi kācittṛtīyo hetuḥ , sa kiṃ nodāhṛtaḥ । so 'pi svabhāvahetāvantarbhavatītyudāhṛta eva । tathā hi —
	na hyanyānupalabhyeṣu nāstitānupalambhanāt /
	tajjñānaśabdāḥ sādhyante tadbhāvāttannibandhanāḥ // <3.40>

[II,056,ii]

uktametat — nānyaivānupalabdherdṛśyasvabhāvāsattā , tayā siddhayāsajjñānaśabdāstannimittāḥ sādhyanta iti ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.ii>

[II,056,iii]

kathaṃ nimittabhāve 'pi naimittikabhāvāniyamādevampratītiḥ ।

<II,057>

[II,057,i]

	siddho hi vyavahāro 'yaṃ dṛśyādṛṣṭāvasanniti /
	tasyāḥ siddhāvasandigdhau tatkāryatve 'pi dhīdhvanī // <3.41>

[II,057,ii]

na hyeṣa pravartanīyo vyavahāro yenāniyataḥ syāt , kiṃ tarhi siddha eva dṛśyasya svabhāvasyādṛṣṭāvasanniti । sa tu pratipannatadvyavahāro 'pi prasiddheṣu nirupākhyeṣu satyapi viṣaye kathañcidviṣayiṇamasmaransmāryate । na hyasadvyavahārasya kvacidaparaṃ kiñcinnibandhanamasti । sa cānenāsakṛdācaritapūrva iti nānayoḥ sambandhaḥ sādhanīyaḥ । tasmāddṛśyādṛṣṭisiddhāvasandigdhaiva tannimittatve 'pyasajjñānaśabdayostadyogyatā , sāsnādisiddhāviva govyavahāraḥ ॥

[II,057,iii]

	vidyamāne 'pi viṣaye mohādatrānanubruvan /
	kevalaṃ siddhasādharmyātsmāryate samayaṃ paraḥ // <3.42>
<II,058>
	kāryakāraṇatā yadvatsādhyate dṛṣṭyadṛṣṭitaḥ /
	kāryādiśabdā hi tayorvyavahārāya kalpitāḥ // <3.43>
	kāraṇātkāryasaṃsiddhiḥ svabhāvāntargamādiyam /
	hetuprabhedākhyāne na darśitodāhṛtiḥ pṛthak // <3.44>
ityantaraślokāḥ ॥

[II,058,i]

asadvyavahārayogyatā vānupalabdhervyāpakaḥ svabhāvaḥ sādhyate । vyāptiścānyatra vyavahārasya tanmātrasiddhyā , viśeṣābhāvāt । siddhenānupalambhātmanāsattvenāsadvyavahāraḥ sādhyata ityuktam ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.iii>

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.a>

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.a.1>

[II,058,ii]

sa evānupalambhaḥ kathaṃ siddhaḥ , kathaṃ vā so 'bhāvaḥ kasyacitkāraṇam । naiṣa doṣaḥ , yasmāt —
	ekopalambhānubhavādidaṃ nopalabhe iti /
	buddherupalabhe veti kalpikāyāḥ samudbhavaḥ // <3.45>

<II,059>

[II,059,i]

na hi bhāvānāṃ svaviṣayajñānābhāvādevaṃ bhavatīdaṃ nopalabha iti yato 'bhāvavyavahāraḥ , kiṃ tarhi svaviśiṣṭajñānabhāvāt , sarvāpratipattau kvacidabhāvāpratipatteḥ । tasmātkasyacitpratyakṣatāyāṃ tatpramāṇabalena dvau vikalpau bhavataḥ — idamupalabhe , aparaṃ nopalabhe ceti ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.a.2>

[II,059,ii]

yasmādarthaviśeṣagatiḥ saṃvedanaviśeṣāt । saṃvedanasya tu tathāvidhātmasaṃvedanādeva bhedapratītiḥ । tatsvayaṃ svataḥ siddhaviśeṣamarthamarthādviśeṣayati । anyathā saṃvedanasyāpi saṃvedanāntaraviśeṣādviśeṣasiddhiḥ , tasyāpyanyata ityanavasthānānna kasyacidviśeṣasiddhiḥ syāt । arthasya tu svasattāviśeṣābhyāṃ na tatsiddhiḥ । kiṃ tarhi svajñānasattāviśeṣābhyāmiti na svatantrā siddhiḥ । naivaṃ saṃvedanasya saṃvedanāntara<II,060>sattāviśeṣābhyāṃ tatsiddhiḥ । sarvāpratipattiprasaṅgāt ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.a.3>

[II,060,i]

tasmāt —
	viśiṣṭarūpānubhavādanyā nānyanirākriyā / <3.46>
	tadviśiṣṭopalambho 'tastasyāpyanupalambhanam /
	tasmādanupalambho 'yaṃ pratyakṣeṇaiva sidhyati // <3.47>
na hyekākārapratiniyatādasaṃsargiṇo 'nubhavādanyo 'nyapratikṣepaḥ । sa eva hi tanniyamāttadevāstīti niścāyayannāparo 'styaparānubhavo veti niścāyayati sāmarthyāt ॥

[II,060,ii]

tasmādekaniyatopalambho 'nyānupalambhastadabhāvavyavahārasiddhihetuśca । sa ca svasaṃvedanapratyakṣasiddhaḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.b>

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.b.1>

[II,060,iii]

nanu svaviśiṣṭapratyayamantareṇāpi bhavatyabhāvabuddhiḥ , yathā santamase ha<II,061>stasañcāreṇa । na , tatrāpi tathāsañcāriṇo hastasyā''ntarasparśaviśeṣopalambhādanyābhāvagateḥ । yato hi sparśaviśeṣopalambhātsatyasati vā prayatne sañcarati me hasta iti bhavati , tata evānyābhāvagatiḥ , tadabhāve 'bhāvāpratipatteḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.b.2>

[II,061,i]

nanu satsūpalambhakāraṇeṣvanyeṣūpalabhyasyānupalambhādabhāvasiddhiḥ । tanmā bhūtsvāpādyavasthāyāṃ kasyacidabhāvapratītiḥ , tatrendriyasādguṇyāderupalambhapratyayasyaivābhāvāt । tanna viśiṣṭopalambhābhāvāttatra kasyacidabhāvāpratipattiḥ , kiṃ tarhi tādṛśo 'nupalambhasyaivābhāvāt ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.b.2.1>

[II,061,ii]

atrāpi satsūpalambhakāraṇeṣviti teṣāmindriyādīnāṃ vṛttisādguṇyenopalambhavṛttiṃ darśayati । tadā hi tānyaviguṇāni bhavanti , yadaiṣāṃ kāryavṛttiḥ syāt । sā copalabdhireva । upalabhyasyānupalambhenāpi tasyā eva viśiṣṭopalabdherekākārapratiniyamaḥ । tasmādviśiṣṭopa<II,062>labdhirevānyānupalabdhiḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.b.2.2>

[II,062,i]

	anyathārthasya nāstitvaṃ gamyate 'nupalambhataḥ /
	upalambhasya nāstitvamanyenetyanavasthitiḥ // <3.48>
anyathā yadi svaviṣayajñānābhāvenābhāvasiddhiḥ syāt , tadabhāvo 'pyanyenānupalambhena sādhanīya ityanavasthānādapratipattirevābhāvasya । na hi saṃvedanābhāvaḥ svataḥ sidhyati , tadaviśeṣādviṣaye 'pi prasaṅgāt । saṃvedanaṃ hyātmaviśeṣādaparasādhanam , naivamabhāvaḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.b.3>

[II,062,ii]

na svaviṣayajñānābhāvādabhāvasiddhiḥ , yato 'yaṃ doṣaḥ । nāpi svaviśiṣṭajñānabhāvāt , kiṃ tarhi yo 'yamupalambho nāsti ghaṭa iti , tata evābhāvopalambhāt , tacca svatantraṃ pramāṇamiti ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.b.3.1>

[II,062,iii]

sa tarhyabhāvapratyayaḥ kuto bhavati । na hyabhāvaḥ kasyacinnimi<II,063>ttam । asāmarthyāt , sāmarthyalakṣaṇatvācca bhāvasya । tadapāyābhāvāttanmātrabhāvino nityaṃ bhāvaprasaṅgāt । anapekṣatvāt , apekṣāyā viśeṣapratilambhalakṣaṇatvāt , tallakṣaṇatvācca bhāvasyābhāvo na syāt । abhāva ityapi bhāvapratiṣedhaḥ । tadabhāvādbhavatīti bhāvānna bhavatīti hetupratiṣedho 'sya kṛtaḥ syāt । tataścāhetukatvam । anyathā'bhāva iti bhāva eva kaścinnāmāntareṇoktaḥ syāt । tasmānnāsya pratyayasya sambhavaḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.3.b.3.2>

[II,063,i]

darśanānantaryaṃ ca svatantrasya na syāt । tadbalotpattau ca tasyaiva tatra sāmarthyamiti tadeva pramāṇaṃ syāt । tadākāraniyamasāmarthyenāparapratikṣepāt , ākārāntarasaṃsarge tasyābhāvāt । tasmādayaṃ pramāṇāntarabalotpanno 'nakṣaliṅgāśrayo 'nupalambhavikalpo na pramāṇam । darśanameva hi tattathotpannam , yenānantaraṃ vidhipratiṣedha<II,064>vikalpau bhavataḥ , yathā nīlaṃ paśyato nīlametanna pītamiti । tasmānna
tau pramāṇam ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.iv>

[II,064,i]

	adṛśye niścayāyogātsthitiranyatra vāryate /
	yathā'liṅgo 'nyasattveṣu vikalpādirna sidhyati // <3.49>
	aniścayaphalā hyeṣā nālaṃ vyāvṛttisādhane /
	ādyādhikriyate hetau niścitenaiva sādhanāt // <3.50>
ityantaraślokau ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.v>

[II,064,ii]

	tasyāḥ svayaṃ prayogeṣu svarūpaṃ vā prayujyate /
	arthabādhanarūpaṃ vā bhāve bhāvādabhāvataḥ // <3.51>

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.v.a>

[II,064,iii]

seyamabhāvaniścayaphalā vyatirekasādhanyanupalabdhiryadā svayamabhāvasādhanāya prayujyate , tadā svarūpeṇa vā prayujyate , yathā — nāstīha dhūmo 'nupalabdheḥ , nāstīha śiṃśapā vṛkṣābhāvāt , nāstīha dhūmo 'nagneriti ॥

<II,065>

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.v.b>

[II,065,i]

pratiṣedhyārthabādhakarūpopanyāsena vā prayujyate , yathā — nātra śītasparśo 'gnerityudāharaṇāni pūrvavat ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.v.b.1>

[II,065,ii]

sa punarayaṃ virodhaḥ kathaṃ gamyate । kvacidavikalakāraṇasya bhavato 'nyabhāve 'bhāvādvirodhagatiḥ , yathā śītoṣṇasparśayoḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.v.b.2>

[II,065,iii]

	anyonyabhedasiddhervā dhruvabhāvavināśavat /
anyonyaparihārasthitalakṣaṇatayā vā virodhaḥ , nityānityatvavat ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.v.b.3>

[II,065,iv]

	pramāṇabādhanādvāpi sāpekṣadhruvabhāvavat // <3.52>
pramāṇaṃ vā yadi tattve bādhakaṃ syāttalliṅgenāpi virodhaḥ , yathā sāpekṣadhruvabhāvayoḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.v.b.3.1>

[II,065,v]

pramāṇaṃ punaḥ — na vināśaniyatāstatkāraṇavādinotpattimanto 'bhyupeyāḥ , tadbhāve parāpekṣatvenopagatatvāt । ye yadbhāve parāpekṣa<II,066>tvenopagamyante , na te tadbhāvaniyatā iṣyante , vāsāṃsīva rāge । taddhetūnāmapi tatra niyamādadoṣa iti cet , na , teṣāṃ sākalyāpratibandhaniyamāsambhavāt । na hi tasminbhavati svakāraṇasāmagryadhīnairanyairapi tadunmukhairbhavitavyam , anāyattatvāt । taddharmatāyāṃ vā tataḥ kṣaṇikatā tasyeṣṭā syāt । tattve viśeṣābhāvādapūrvabhāvinaḥ paścādapyabhāvaprasaṅgāt । sa ca taddheturvānityatāhetuniyamanasvabhāvastatsvabhāvastatsvabhāvajananasvabhāvo vā kiṃ neṣyate । kiṃ pāramparyeṇa , ante 'pi tatsvabhāvasyaiva tadbhāve sāmarthyāt । etena kādācitkasvabhāvatānapekṣatayorvirodho vyākhyātaḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.v.b.3.2>

[II,066,i]

nanvevamapi virodhinoḥ parasparaparihārasthitalakṣaṇatayaiva virodhaḥ , aniyamena niyamabādhanāt । pramāṇaṃ pratiyoginaṃ sādhayati , bādhā pu<II,067>nastata eveti na pramāṇabādhanādvirodhaḥ । satyam , virodhivyāptenāpi svabhāvenārthato virodhāt । tadupanyāsenānupalabdheḥ prayogaḥ syāditi darśanārthametaduktam , yathāyamevānantarodāhṛtaḥ prayogaḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.vi>

[II,067,i]

atha yadidaṃ na santi pradhānādayo 'nupalabderiti । tatra kathamasadvyavahāravidhiḥ sadvyavahārapratiṣedho vā । kathaṃ ca na syāt । tadarthapratiṣedhe dharmivācino 'prayogādabhidhānasya , tasya pratiṣedhāt , nirviṣayasya ca pratiṣedhasyāyogāt । naiṣa doṣaḥ , yasmāt —
	anādivāsanodbhūtavikalpapariniṣṭhitaḥ /
	śabdārthastrividho dharmo bhāvābhāvobhayāśrayaḥ // <3.53>
	tasminbhāvānupādāne sādhye 'syānupalambhanam /
	tathā heturna tasyaivābhāvaḥ śabdaprayogataḥ // <3.54>

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.vi.a>

[II,067,ii]

naite śabdāḥ svalakṣaṇaviṣayāḥ , anādikālavāsanāprabhavavikalpapra<II,068>tibhāsinamarthaṃ viṣayatvenātmasātkurvanti । vaktuḥ śrotuśca tadvikalpabhājaḥ , yathāpratibhāsivastupratipādanasamīhāprayogāt , tadākāravikalpajananācca । na copādānakāryapratyayāpratibhāsi rūpaṃ śakyaṃ tadviṣayatvenādhyavasātum । sa tu vikalpaḥ sadasadubhayapratyayāhitavāsanāprabhava iti tatpratibhāsyākārādhyavasāyavaśena ca bhāvābhāvobhayadharma ityucyate । tadatra dharmiṇi vyavasthitāḥ sadasattvaṃ cintayanti — kimayaṃ pradhānaśabdapratibhāsyartho bhāvopādāno na veti । tasya bhāvānupādānatve sādhye sa ca pratyātmavedyatvādapratikṣepārho 'rtho dharmī । na ca sa evārthaḥ svalakṣaṇamiti śakyaṃ vaktum , asamprāptavinaṣṭayorapyarthayostasyānapāyāt । vastuviparītākāraniveśiṣvapi tīrthāntarīyapratyayeṣu bhāvāt ॥

[II,068,i]

	paramārthaikatānatve śabdānāmanibandhanā /
	na syātpravṛttirartheṣu darśanāntarabhediṣu // <3.55>
	atītājātayorvāpi na ca syādanṛtārthatā /
<II,069>
	vācaḥ kasyāścidityeṣā bauddhārthaviṣayā matā // <3.56>
iti saṅgrahaślokau ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.vi.b>

[II,069,i]

tasya ca yathāsamīhitarūpānupādānatve sādhye tathānupalambho dharmo 'stīti na sādhanadharmāsiddhiḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.vi.c>

[II,069,ii]

na tu punaratrāyameva śabdavikalpapratibhāsyartho 'pahnūyate , tasya buddhāvupasthāpanāya śabdaprayogāt , tadabhāve tadayogāt । kiṃ ca ,
	sadasatpakṣabhedena śabdārthānapavādibhiḥ /
	vastveva cintyate hyatra pratibaddhaḥ phalodayaḥ // <3.57>
na hi śabdārthaḥ sannasanvā kañcitpuruṣārthamuparuṇaddhi samādadhāti vā , yathābhiniveśamatattvāt , yathātattvaṃ cāsamīhitatvāt । tasmādayaṃ pravartamānaḥ sarvadā sadasaccintāyāmavadhīritavikalpapratibhāso vastvevādhiṣṭhānīkaroti , yatrāyaṃ puruṣārthaḥ pratibaddhaḥ , yathāgnau śītavi<II,070>nodanādiḥ । na hyatra śabdārthaḥ samarthaḥ । tadanubhavāptāvapi tadabhāvāt । tadayamarthakriyārthī tadasamarthaṃ prati na dattānuyogo bhavituṃ yuktaḥ । na hi vṛṣasyantī ṣaṇḍhasya rūpavairūpyaparīkṣāyāmavadhatte ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.2.vi.d>

[II,070,i]

yatpunaretaduktaṃ kalpitasyānupalabdhirdharma iti tasya ko 'rthaḥ । kalpanāviṣayatvācchabdārtha eva kalpitaḥ । tasya vastvāśrayānupalambho dharma ityayamatrābhiprāyaḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3>

[II,070,ii]

sthitametat — svabhāvānupalabdhiḥ svabhāvahetāvantarbhavatīti , sā tadudāharaṇenaivodāhṛtā । sa punarupādhibhedāpekṣaḥ kevalo vā kṛtakatvasattvavannāśe nirdiśyata ityuktam ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.i>

[II,070,iii]

tatra ,
	sattāsvabhāvo hetuścenna sattā sādhyate katham /
	ananvayo hi bhedānāṃ vyāhato hetusādhyayoḥ // <3.58>

<II,071>

[II,071,i]

yadi sattvamanityatve 'nyatra vā hetuḥ syāt , sādhyamapi kasmānneṣyate । tatkilaivaṃ prasādhyamānaṃ viśeṣībhavati । na ca viśeṣaḥ sādhayituṃ śakyate , ananvayāt । yathāha — pramāṇaviṣayāparijñānāditi । so 'yaṃ viśeṣo na sādhya eva vyāhanyate , kiṃ tarhi hetāvapi , tulyadoṣatvāt । na hi heturananvayaḥ siddheraṅgam , tataḥ saṃśayāt ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii>

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.a>

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.a.1>

[II,071,ii]

naiṣa doṣaḥ । yasmāt —
	bhāvopādānamātre tu sādhye sāmānyadharmiṇi /
	na kaścidarthaḥ siddhaḥ syādaniṣiddhaṃ ca tādṛśam // <3.59>

[II,071,iii]

na sarvathā sattāsādhane viśeṣaḥ sādhito bhavati । bhāvamātraviśeṣaṇo 'rtho 'sti kaściddharmīti prasādhayato 'nirdiṣṭasvabhāvaviśeṣasya kasya<II,072>citsattāmātre virodhābhāvānneha sattāsādhane pratiṣedhaḥ , kiṃ tu tathāsti kaściditi kañcanāsya bhedamaparāmṛśanbruvāṇaḥ kaṃ svārthaṃ puṣṇāti । tasmādanenopāttabheda eva sādhyaḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.a.2>

[II,072,i]

	upāttabhede sādhye 'sminbhaveddheturananvayaḥ /
	sattāyāṃ tena sādhyāyāṃ viśeṣaḥ sādhito bhavet // <3.60>

[II,072,ii]

sa hi dharmī pradhānalakṣaṇa eko nityaḥ sukhādyātmako 'nyo veti , yathākathañcidapi viśeṣitastatsvabhāvaḥ sādhito bhavati । sa ca tathā nānveti । yadapi sattāmātramanveti , na tena siddhena kiñcit ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.b>

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.b.1>

[II,072,iii]

nanvevamagnyādiṣvapi prasaṅgaḥ । tatrāpi hi nāgnisattāyāṃ kaścidvivādaḥ । viśiṣṭādhāraviśeṣaṇasya tvabhimatasyānanvayādasiddhiḥ । na vai sa ādhārastaṃ viśeṣīkaroti , ayogavyavacchedena viśeṣaṇādityuktam । tasmāttatra sāmānyameva sādhyate tadayogavyavacchedena ॥

<II,073>

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.b.2>

[II,073,i]

na tathehāpi kvacitsattāyāḥ sādhanam । pradhānādiśabdavācyasyaiva kasyacidarthasyābhāvānnirviśeṣaṇaiva sā । kathamabhāvo jñeyābhidheyaprameyatvaiḥ so 'pi siddha eva । tatkimidānīṃ jñeyamastīti siddhirastu । tathāpi kiṃ siddhaṃ syāt । nanu bauddho vikalpapratibhāsaḥ śabdārthaḥ , tasya ca svalakṣaṇopādānatā sādhyate । sādhyatām , kiṃ tvasāvapi pradhānādilakṣaṇabhedānāśrayaḥ śabdārthamātratāyāmavatiṣṭhate । tathā ca pūrvavadabhidheyaṃ kimapyastīti sādhyaṃ syāt । na hi śabdārthāḥ svataḥ kañcidguṇaviśeṣamāviśanti । upādānadharmasteṣūpacaryate । tadasiddhopādāneṣu na sambhavati । tadime nirviśeṣaṇāḥ । teṣvarthopādānatvasādhanamarthasattāmātrasādhanameva , nārthaviśeṣasādhanamityapārthakam । anyatra tu tadevāgnisāmānyaṃ tatrāsiddhamiti sādhyate ॥

<II,074>

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.b.3>

[II,074,i]

nanu cātrāpi tadayogavirahiṇā sāmānyenānvayo na siddha eva । na vai kaścittathābhūtenātmanānvayaṃ karoti । pratipādayatā hi paraṃ dhūmo 'gnināntarīyako darśanīyaḥ — yatra dhūmastatrāgniriti । sa tathāgnimātreṇa vyāptaḥ siddhaḥ — yatraiva svayaṃ dṛśyate , tatraivāgnibuddhiṃ janayati । tatra sādhyanirdeśena na kiñcit , tatra darśanasambandhākhyānamātrādiṣṭasiddheḥ । tadanirdeśe vā kathaṃ tadviśiṣṭenānvayaḥ । tadayamagnināvinābhāvī siddhaḥ । arthādevāgnestatpradeśāyogaṃ vyavacchinattīti sa tathā sādhya ucyate । na punastathāsyopanyāsapūrvako 'nvayaḥ , sādhyokterihānaṅgatvāt । tatpūrvakatve vā kaḥ pratijñāṃ sādhanādapākaroti । tathā cāha —
	liṅgasyāvyabhicārastu dharmeṇānyatra darśyate /
	tatra prasiddhaṃ tadyuktaṃ dharmiṇaṃ gamayiṣyati //
iti । tasmānnāgnyādisādhanavatsattāsādhanamapyanavadyam ॥

<II,075>

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.c>

[II,075,i]

	aparāmṛṣṭatadbhede vastumātre tu sādhane /
	tanmātravyāpinaḥ sādhyasyānvayo na vihanyate // <3.61>

[II,075,ii]

sādhane punaḥ sattve svabhāvaviśeṣāparigraheṇa vastumātravyāpini sādhyadharme nānvayavyāghātaḥ । na hi tatrāvaśyaṃ viśeṣaparigrahaḥ kāryaḥ , sanmātrāśraye 'pi sādhanasāmarthyāt । na sādhyatve , vaiphalyāt ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.d>

[II,075,iii]

api ca ,
	nāsiddhe bhāvadharmo 'sti vyabhicāryubhayāśrayaḥ /
	dharmo viruddho 'bhāvasya sā sattā sādhyate katham // <3.62>

[II,075,iv]

sattāyāṃ hi sādhyāyāṃ sarvastaddheturna trayīṃ doṣajātimativartate , asiddhiṃ vyabhicāraṃ virodhaṃ ca ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.d.1>

[II,075,v]

tatra yadi bhāvadharmo heturucyate , sa kathamasiddhasattāke syāt । yo hi bhāvadharmaṃ hetumicchati , sa kathaṃ bhāvaṃ necchet । svabhāva <II,076> eva hi kayācidapekṣayā dharma iti vyatirekīva dharmiṇo nirdiśyate । na hi dharmadharmivācinoḥ śabdayorvācye kaścidviśeṣo 'stīti nirloṭhitametatpramāṇavārttike ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.d.2>

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.d.2.1>

[II,076,i]

atha punarubhayadharmaṃ brūyāt , anāśritavastuno 'paryudāsena vyatirekamātrasyābhāve 'pyavirodhāt , yathā na bhavati mūrta ityamūrtatvaṃ nirupākhye 'pi syāt । nirupākhyasyābhāvādapratiṣedhaviṣayateti cet , tatkimidānīṃ vidhiviṣayo 'stu । tadapi neti cet , kathamidānīṃ na pratiṣedhaviṣayaḥ , vidhinivṛttirūpatvātpratiṣedhasya । parisaṅkhyāteṣveva pratiṣedhavṛttiriṣṭā , tannānupākhyeṣvamūrtatvādikamiti cet , duḥkhaṃ vatāyaṃ tapasvī sāṅketikamicchāmātrānurodhinamarthaṃ niyantukāmo jīvati , tasya sorastāḍaṃ krandato 'pi lokasyānivṛtteḥ । yathāsaṅketaṃ pratipatteḥ , tanmātraprayojanatvācchabdaprayogasya । iṣṭāviśeṣā<II,077>dubhayatrāpratītiprasaṅgāt । tato 'pi pratīteḥ samāśrayāt । tasyānyatrāpi tulyatvāt । tadetadvyavacchedamātraṃ dvayorapi sambhavadvipakṣapracāraśaṅkāvyavacchedena labhyaṃ gamakatvaṃ kathamātmasātkuryāt ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.d.2.2>

[II,077,i]

avyavacchedarūpā api khalu jñeyatvādayo dharmāḥ kathañcidavastūnāmapi buddhyā vyavasthāpanātsādhāraṇāḥ santi । te 'pyetena vyākhyātāḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.d.2.3>

[II,077,ii]

sa ca svavācobhayadharmatāṃ bruvāṇaḥ sato 'nyatrāpyasya vṛttiṃ bhāṣate sattāyāṃ cāvyabhicāramiti kathaṃ nonmattaḥ । vipakṣavṛttyā vyabhicāraḥ । tatpakṣasapakṣānyataratvādīnāmavipakṣavṛtterubhayadharmatve 'pyadoṣaḥ । na hi <II,078> pakṣa eva vyabhicāraviṣayaḥ । kaṃ punaratra bhavānvipakṣaṃ pratyeti । sādhyābhāvam । kathamidānīṃ heturavipakṣavṛttirubhayadharmaśca । na hi pakṣavipakṣapravibhāgāpekṣayā hetoravyabhicāraḥ , vāstavatvāt । na hyavinābhāvo hetorvyavasthayā darśyate — sarvo 'pakṣaḥ kṛtako 'nitya iti , kiṃ tarhi vastubalāyātaiva khalu vyāptiḥ pramāṇairupadarśyate — sarvaṃ kṛtakamanityamiti । tathāsiddhāveva hi sa dharmastasya gamakaḥ syāt , nānyathā । puruṣapravṛtteravastupāratantryāt । yaṃ hi puruṣaḥ sādhayitumicchati , sa pakṣaḥ । sa yamevaṃ vyabhicāraviṣayaṃ paśyati , tameva pakṣīkuryāt । na cānumānaviṣaye pratyakṣādibādhāsti , pramāṇasya pramāṇāntareṇa bādhāyāṃ tasyāprāmāṇyaprasaṅgāt । lakṣaṇayukte bādhāsambhave <II,079> tallakṣaṇameva dūṣitaṃ syādityuktam । abādhanasyāpi lakṣaṇatve tasyāniścayalakṣaṇatā । tathā cāgamakatvamiti kiṃ kasya sādhanaṃ , yadarthamavyabhicāraścintyate । tasmādvastuto yadyena vyāptamavyāptaṃ vā , tattasya gamakamagamakaṃ ceti na puruṣecchayā vastudharmo vyavatiṣṭhate । yadāyaṃ pakṣīkaroti , tadā na vyabhicāraḥ । anyadā tena vyabhicāra iti suvyavadātaṃ prāmāṇyam ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.d.3>

[II,079,i]

abhāvadharmaṃ tu bhāvamātravyāpino 'rthasya vyavacchedaṃ hetuṃ sattāyāṃ vadato 'sya viruddho hetuḥ syāt , tasya bhāve kvacidasambhavāt , abhāve ca sarvatra bhāvavyavacchedasya bhāvāt ॥

[II,079,ii]

tadayaṃ triprakāro 'pi dharmaḥ sattāsādhane na hetulakṣaṇabhāk , na cānyā <II,080> gatirasti । tasmānna sattā sādhyate ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.3.ii.e>

[II,080,i]

sādhanatve punarasyāḥ sāmānyena tanmātravyāpini vastudharme siddhasattāke dharmiṇi nāsiddhiḥ । tena ca sādhyadharmeṇa vyāptiryadi kathañcinniścīyeta , tadā na virodhavyabhicārāviti nāyaṃ prasaṅga iti ॥

<§ 3.3.2.1.4>

[II,080,ii]

eṣa dvividho hetuḥ svabhāvalakṣaṇaḥ kāryalakṣaṇaśca । sa eva svavyāpakaviparyaye sādhye viruddha iti darśayaṃścaturaḥ pakṣadharmānāha ॥

<§ 3.3.2.2>

<§ 3.3.2.2.1>

[II,080,iii]

bhedasāmānyayoścānaikāntikayoraikāntikatāṃ bruvāṇaṃ prativahandvau । tacca hetvābhāseṣvevāvasaraprāptaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.2.2>

<§ 3.3.2.2.2.i>

[II,080,iv]

vyāvṛttiprādhānyasādhanārthaṃ hetostrīnpakṣadharmānāha । tathā hi nānvayamukhena heturgamakaḥ , anityatvādaprayatnānantarīyakatvasyāgateḥ । mā <II,081> bhūdato gatiḥ , kevalatvādavyatirekatayānvayasyeti cet , iha tarhi bhavatvasparśatvānnitya iti । na , atrāpyanvayasyāprādhānyāditi cet , iha tu balavānanvayo vyatirekaśca durbalaḥ , hetoḥ sapakṣavyāptervipakṣe ca kvacidabhāvāt , yathā — prayatnānantarīyako 'nityatvāditi । na bhavati , sarvato vipakṣādavyāvṛtteriti cet , evaṃ tarhi yaḥ kṛtakaḥ so 'nitya eveti nityavyavacchedena gamakateṣṭā syāt , anyathā sarvato vipakṣādvyāvṛtterdarśayitumaśakyatvāt । tadasya na bhāvamātreṇa na sāmyena na prādhānyena gatiḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.2.2.2.ii>

[II,081,i]

aprādhānye 'pyanvayasya vyatirekavyāptāvasti , yathā — anityaḥ prayatnānantarīyakatvāditi । tasmādevameva heturgamakaḥ — yaḥ prayatnānantarīyaḥ so 'nitya eveti nityavyavacchedena , asya vākyasya śabdapradeśādiṣu nityānagnivyavacchedena vyatirekagatau sāmarthyaparisamāpteḥ ॥

<II,082>

<§ 3.3.2.2.2.iii>

[II,082,i]

na caiteṣāṃ bhedamātraṃ gamyate , kiṃ tu tadeva sāmānyamapratipakṣam — idameveha nānyaditi । yadyavaśyamete 'nanyasaṃsargiṇo gamyāḥ , sa evaiṣāmasaṃsargo gamyo 'stu , tāvatā kāryaparisamāpteḥ । kimantargaḍunā sāmānyeneti vyāvṛttisādhanena darśayati ॥

<§ 3.3.3>

<§ 3.3.3.1>

[II,082,ii]

yastarhi samarthena hetunā kāryotpādo 'numīyate , sa kathaṃ trividhe hetāvantarbhavati ।
	hetunā yaḥ samarthena kāryotpādo 'numīyate /
	arthāntarānapekṣatvātsa svabhāvo 'nuvarṇitaḥ // <3.63>

<§ 3.3.3.1.1>

[II,082,iii]

asāvapi yathāsannihitānnānyamapekṣata iti tanmātrānubandhī svabhāvo bhāvasya । tatra hi kevalaṃ samagrāṇāṃ kāraṇānāṃ kāryotpādanayogyatānumīyate । yogyatā ca sāmagrīmātrānubandhinīti svabhāva<II,083>bhūtaiva । kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ sāmagryāḥ kāryameva nānumīyate । yena na samagrāṇītyeva kāraṇadravyāṇi svakāryaṃ janayanti , sāmagrījanmanāṃ śaktīnāṃ pariṇāmāpekṣatvātkāryotpādasya । atrāntare ca pratibandhasambhavānna kāryānumānam । yogyatāyāstu dravyāntarānapekṣatvādaviruddham । uttarottaraśaktipariṇāmena samartheyaṃ kāraṇasāmagrī kāryotpādane , śaktipariṇāmapratyayasyānyasyāpekṣaṇīyasyābhāvāditi । pūrvasvajātimātrahetutvācchaktiprasūteḥ sāmagryā yogyatānanyāpekṣaṇītyucyate ॥

<§ 3.3.3.1.2>

[II,083,i]

samagrāṇyeva kāraṇāni yogyatāmapyanumāpayanti , asamagrasyaikāntāsāmrthyāditi na tataḥ kāryānumānam । vipakṣe vṛttyadarśane 'pi śeṣavat , yathā dehendriyabuddhibhyo rāgādyanumānam । ātmātmīyābhiniveśapūrvakā hi rāgādayaḥ , ahaṃ mameti cāpaśyato 'nunayapratighā<II,084>bhāvāt । ayoniśomanaskāramantareṇa doṣāṇāmanutpatteḥ । dehādīnāṃ hetutve 'pi na kevalānāṃ sāmarthyamastīti vipakṣavṛtteradṛṣṭāvapi śeṣavadetadvyabhicāri liṅgam ॥

<§ 3.3.3.2>

<§ 3.3.3.2.1>

[II,084,i]

yā tarhyakāryakāraṇabhūtenānyena rasādinā rūpādigatiḥ , sā katham । sāpi
	ekasāmagryadhīnasya rūpāderasato gatiḥ /
	hetudharmānumānena dhūmendhanavikāravat // <3.64>
tatrāpi hetureva tathābhūto 'numīyate । pravṛttaśaktirūpopādānakāraṇasahakāripratyayo hi rasahetū rasaṃ janayati , indhanavikāropādānahetusahakāripratyayāgnidhūmajananavat । tathā hi svakāraṇasya phalotpādanaṃ pratyābhimukhyena vinā na rasaḥ । tadeva ca rūpopādānahetūnāṃ pravṛttikāraṇam । sāpi rasopādānakāraṇapravṛttī rūpo<II,085>pādānakāraṇapravṛttisahakāriṇī । tasmādyathābhūtāddheto rasa utpannastathābhūtamanumāpayanrūpamanumāpayati । tatrāpyatītaikakālānāṃ gatiḥ , nā'nāgatānām , vyabhicārāt । tasmādiyamapi kāryaliṅgajā ॥

<§ 3.3.3.2.2>

[II,085,i]

etena pipīlikotsaraṇamatsyavikārādervarṣādyanumānaṃ vyākhyātam । tatrāpi bhūtapariṇāma eva kaścidvarṣahetuḥ pipīlikāsaṅkṣobhādihetuśceti ॥

[II,085,ii]

rūpātsparśānumānaṃ kāryaliṅgajam , rūpādīnāṃ bhūtāśrayatvāt ॥

<§ 3.3.3.3>

[II,085,iii]

yattarhīdaṃ viṣāṇī gotvāditi tatkatham । tatrāpi ,
	samudāyavyavasthāyāḥ kāraṇaṃ samudāyinaḥ /
	asatsu teṣu sā na syāditi gotvādviṣāṇitā // <3.65>

<II,086>

[II,086,i]

sāsnāviṣāṇādisamudāyo hi gauḥ । tadiyaṃ samudāyavyavasthā samudāyinibandhanatvāttadabhāve na syāt । bhavantī svanimittasannidhiṃ sūcayatīti gotvādviṣāṇitāpratipattiḥ kāryaliṅgajā ॥

<§ 3.3.3.4>

<§ 3.3.3.4.1>

[II,086,ii]

	ādhārato 'bhinirvṛtterātmanastādṛśo 'mbhasaḥ /
	kāryaṃ tasya	...

[II,086,iii]

yo 'pi sthiramambho dṛṣṭvādṛṣṭo 'pyadhastādādhārasambhavo 'numīyate , tadapi kāryaliṅgajameva , tādṛśasyātmano 'mbhasastata ādhārādabhinirvṛtteḥ । na hi tasmādupakāramananubhavatastato 'vasthāviśeṣapratilambho yuktaḥ । upakārasyārthāntaratve 'pyuktam ॥

<§ 3.3.3.4.2>

[II,086,iv]

na vai tata ātmaviśeṣotpatterambhasastathāsthitiḥ , kiṃ tarhi saṃyogāt । kiṃ punaḥ sa tayoḥ saṃyogaḥ , tābhyāṃ jananātsamavāyādvā । sa ki<II,087>mekatra na samavaiti janyate vā । tasyāsāmarthyāt । tadasamarthaṃ pṛthaktatra sahitamapi tādṛśamevetyanupakārakatvānna saṃyogena tadvatsyāt । sahitasya tadanyopakārādviśeṣotpatteḥ sāmarthyam । ko 'yamajanyajanakabhūtānāmupakāraḥ , svarūpasya siddherakāryatvāt । pararūpakriyāyāmapi tatrānupakārāt । ubhayathā'kārakasyākiñcitkaratvenānupakārakatvādityuktaprāyam । tasmātsarva eva vastusambandhā janakasyaivopayogaviśeṣavaśātpravibhāgena kāryakāraṇabhāvādvyavasthāpyante । tadayaṃ kuṇḍabhūtalādīnāmapyādhārabhāvo badarodakādiṣu jananaśaktireva । tasmādeteṣu tadātmanā vyapadeśādayo janyajanakabhāvakṛtā eva bhavantu , satyapi saṃyoge tannāntarīyakatvādeṣām , paramparākalpanāyāśca vaiyarthyāt ॥

<II,088>

<§ 3.3.3.4.3>

[II,088,i]

sthāpakatvādādhāraḥ , na janakatvāditi cet , sthiterarthāntarānarthāntaratve upakāreṇa vyākhyāte । pātapratibandhātsthāpaka iti cet , kaḥ pratibandhaḥ । sa hi tasya pātapratibandho nārthāntarameva , yaḥ sthāpayitrā kriyate । arthāntaratve tatraivopayoga iti kaḥ patataḥ pratibandhaḥ । pratibandhādapāte 'pi tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ — kṛto nāma sa tena pratibandhākhyaḥ padārthaḥ , sa tu bhāvaḥ prasarpaṇadharmāpracyutānutpannātmabhūtaviśeṣaḥ kiṃ na patatīti । pratibandhādatiśayapratipattau tasyāpyātmāntaratve tadeva vastunastādātmyātpatanamanavasthā ca । na ca tathābhūtātmakriyāṃ pratibandhamabhyupaiti । tasmātpātābhāvaḥ pratibandhaḥ sa kathaṃ kenacitkriyate । abhāvaṃ karotīti hi nābhāvo nāma kaścitkāryaḥ , tasya kathañcitkāryatve <II,089> 'bhāvāyogāt , pūrvavatprasaṅgācca । tasmādbhāvakriyāpratiṣedha eṣa bhāvaṃ na karotīti yāvat । tenāyamevaṃ vācyaḥ syāt — pātaṃ na karotīti । tadapīṣṭameva । na hi tasya tatkṛtaḥ pātaḥ , svayaṃ patanadharmatayā pātāt , ākāśakṣiptavat । tathā cāyamatrākiñcitkaraḥ kathamasya sthāpayitā । tadayaṃ na kenacitpratibaddha iti na kadācittiṣṭhet । tasmātpātapratibandha ityapi kṣaṇikānāṃ bhāvānāmupādānasamānadeśotpāda ucyate ॥

[II,089,i]

tasmātsiddhā tādṛśo 'mbhasa ādhārādutpattiḥ ॥

<§ 3.3.3.5>

[II,089,ii]

					... balākāpi vṛttestoyasamāśrayāt // <3.66>

[II,089,iii]

kāryaṃ tasyetyanuvartate । toyāśritā hi balākāyā vṛttiḥ । tataḥ śarīrasthitiṃ pratilabhamānā tatkāryatayā pratibandhena toyaṃ gamayati deśādyapekṣayā ॥

<II,090>

[II,090,i]

anayā diśānyeṣvapi gamakeṣu pratibandhaḥ sādhyaḥ । tanna trividhāddhetoranyo gamako 'sti , apratibaddhasvabhāvasyāvinābhāvaniyamābhāvāditi ॥ ॥

<II,091>

{3.IV}

<§ 3.IV.1>

[II,091,i]

	asiddhajñāpanāṅgasya jñāpanaṃ pratyaśaktitaḥ /
	trairūpyāsiddhisandehe prapattṝṇāmasādhanam // <3.67>

[II,091,ii]

jñāpako hi heturyadātmatayā jñāpayati , tadasiddhau sandehe vā na jñāpakaḥ , śabdavat । trairūpyācca heturarthaṃ gamayati , asambaddhādapratipatteḥ , mahānasādidṛṣṭadhūmādivodadhāvagneḥ , apratibandhācca , sarvataḥ sarvapratipattiprasaṅgāt । tasmātpratipādyapratipādakayorasiddhasandigdhadharmisambandhānvayavyatirekā dharmā hetvābhāsāḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2>

[II,091,iii]

tatra ,
	ekāprasiddhisandehe 'prasiddho vyabhicārabhāk /
	dvayorviruddho 'siddhau ca sandehe vyabhicārabhāk // <3.68>

<§ 3.IV.2.1>

[II,091,iv]

ekaikasya rūpasyāsiddhau sandehe vāsiddho 'naikāntikaśca hetvābhāso bhavati ॥

<II,092>

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1>

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.i>

[II,092,i]

dharmisambandhāsiddhāvasiddhaḥ , yathā — anityaḥ śabdaścākṣuṣatvāt ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.ii>

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.ii.a>

[II,092,ii]

cetanāstaravaḥ sarvatvagapaharaṇe maraṇāditi prativādyanabhyupagataḥ , vijñānendriyāyurnirodhalakṣaṇatvānmaraṇasya । kathaṃ ca maraṇamabhyupayanna caitanyamabhyupeyāt । maraṇaśabdapravṛtteḥ siddhameveti cet , icchātaḥ śabdāḥ pravartante । na tadvaśādvastusthitiḥ , atiprasaṅgāt । tasmācchoṣamayaṃ taruṣu maraṇamāha । na cedṛśaṃ prāṇimaraṇamiti nedaṃ taruṣu sidhyati । na hyanapekṣitavastukaṃ śabdamātramicchāvṛtti vidyata iti vastugamyaṃ vastu sidhyati ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.ii.b>

[II,092,iii]

etenānityatvasaṃsthānaviśeṣādayo 'cetanatvaviśiṣṭabuddhipūrvakatvādisādhanā buddhibhuvanādīnāṃ vyākhyātāḥ । tatrāpi hi śabda eva kevalaḥ siddhaḥ , nārthaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.ii.b.1>

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.ii.b.1.1>

[II,092,iv]

na hi pare 'pracyutātmana upalayanamanityatāmicchanti । nanvaviva<II,093>kṣitaviśeṣaṃ sāmānyaṃ siddhameva । tatsiddhau viśeṣavikalpenāsiddhicodanā mithyottarameva bhavati । syānmithyottaraṃ yadi dvayorapīṣṭaṃ kiñcidvastu sāmānyaṃ syāt , yannibandhano 'yamanityaśabdaḥ , kṛtakatvādivat । nanvastyeva tirodhānam । na vai parastadanityatvamāha , kiṃ tarhi vināśam । nanu vinaṣṭatirohitayordvayorapyavyaktistulyetyastyeva sāmānyam । atha keyamavyaktiḥ । adṛśyātmatā । nanvanena lakṣaṇena pradhānapuruṣādayo 'pyanityāḥ prasajanti । prāganyadharmaṇo 'vyaktiranityateti cet , anyadharmā ca prāgapracyutātmeti ca suvyāhṛtam ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.ii.b.1.2>

[II,093,i]

etena tadavasthānivṛttirvyākhyātā । yo 'pyavasthānivṛttiṃ tirodhānasadṛśīṃ śabdaviṣayamāha , tasyāpi sā kathaṃ nivṛttā'pracyutā ca । avasthā nivartate , nāvasthāteti cet , keyamavasthā । yeyamudakadhāraṇādyarthakriyāyāmupanidhīyate , yāmayaṃ janturadhyakṣamadhyavasyati ghaṭo <II,094> 'yamiti , tannivṛttāvanivṛttāvapyaparasyāsya sarvasyābhāvāt । evaṃ tarhi saivāvasthā ghaṭo 'stu , yathoktalakṣaṇatvādasya । sa ca nivṛtta ityanivṛtto 'vasthātāvasthitaḥ paryanuyojyaḥ । sanvā na ghaṭo bhāvikaḥ , atallakṣaṇatvāt । vastvekamevāvasthāntarāveśādbhedadṛṣṭiriti cet , sa evāvasthābhedo vastubhedalakṣaṇaṃ kiṃ neṣyate । evaṃ hi sukhādīnāmasandigdho bhedo bhavati । kasyacidrūpasyānukārādavasthābhede 'pyabheda iti cet , nanvetatsukhādīnāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ ca tulyam । bhede kramābhivyaktivirodhādaikyamiti cet , tatkimidānīmakramābhivyakterghaṭadadhyādiranekaḥ , ko vā virodhaḥ kramābhivyakterabhedavyāpanāsiddhau । kramastu tatkāryatvāttasya tadaniṣpattāvaniṣpatteḥ । abheda evātitarāmakramatvaprasaṅgaḥ , ekātmatvavat । kāryatvādevābheda iti cet , yukto yadi pratibandhaḥ sidhyet । sa cānanvayasya na sidhyatīti vakṣyāmaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.ii.b.1.3>

[II,094,i]

sarvathā nāsti samāno dharmo dhvastetarayorabhedakalpanāyāmapi , yamayama<II,095>nityaśabdaḥ samāviśet , yathotpattiṃ hetubhyaḥ kṛtakaśabdaḥ sambandhibhedavyudāse 'pi ॥

[II,095,i]

tathā maraṇasāmānyaṃ vṛkṣapuruṣayoḥ । yaddarśanātprāṇyantare mṛtapratipattiḥ , tādṛśaṃ yadi taruṣūpalabhyeta , syādetat । atha śoṣādikameva maraṇaśabdena vadet , tasyāpi pratibandhaścaitanyena sampradhāryaḥ , yataḥ sidhyet ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.ii.b.2>

[II,095,ii]

tathā saṃsthānamapi , yādṛśaṃ prāsādādibhedeṣvanuvṛttimadbuddhipūrvakaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yaddṛṣṭerakriyādarśino 'pi kṛtabuddhirbhavati , yadi tādṛśaṃ syāt , sarva eva hetavastathā syuḥ ॥

[II,095,iii]

api ca ,

<II,096>

[II,096,i]

	siddhaṃ yādṛgadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvābhāvānuvṛttimat /
	sanniveśādi tadyuktaṃ tasmādyadanumīyate // <3.69>
	vastubhede prasiddhasya śabdasāmyādabhedinaḥ /
	na yuktānumitiḥ pāṇḍudravyādiva hutāśane // <3.70>
	anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛdvikārasya kasyacit /
	ghaṭādeḥ karaṇātsidhyedvalmīkasyāpi tatkṛtiḥ // <3.71>
	sādhyenānugamātkārye sāmānyenāpi sādhane /
	sambandhibhedādbhedoktidoṣaḥ kāryasamo mataḥ // <3.72>
	jātyantare prasiddhasya śabdasāmānyadarśanāt /
	na yuktaṃ sādhanaṃ gotvādvāgādīnāṃ viṣāṇivat // <3.73>
	vivakṣāparatantratvānna śabdāḥ santi kutra vā /
	tadbhāvādarthasiddhau tu sarvaṃ sarvasya sidhyati // <3.74>
<II,097>
	vastusvarūpe 'siddhe 'yaṃ nyāyaḥ siddhe viśeṣaṇam /
	adoṣakṛdasiddhāvapyākāśāśrayavaddhvaneḥ // <3.75>
	asiddhāvapi śabdasya siddhe vastuni sidhyati /
	aulūkyasya yathā bauddhenoktaṃ mūrtyādisādhanam // <3.76>
ityantaraślokāḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.ii.c>

[II,097,i]

yā punaḥ śāstrāśrayeṇānyatarāsiddhirudbhāvyate , yathābhivyaktivādinaḥ kṛtakatvamasiddhamiti , na tatsarvatrānumāne , pramāṇadṛṣṭasya pratijñayā'siddhicodanā'yogāt , anadhikārācca śāstrasyānumāne । pramāṇenaiva bādhane tadbhāvapramāṇāpratītau vā kimabhivyaktivādena । tasmācchāstrāśraya evānumāne 'nyatarāsiddhiḥ śāstreṇa । anyatra tvajñānāditi na vādodā<II,098>haraṇam । udāharaṇadiśaṃ tvācāryaḥ prāha ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.iii>

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.a>

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.a.1>

[II,098,i]
