yaḥ punaḥ pratijñārthaikadeśo 'siddha ucyate , yathā — anityaḥ śabdaḥ śabdatvāditi , so 'pi , sādhyasādhanayorbhedātsādhyasya dharmiṇaḥ svasādhane sādhanatvāsiddherhetubhāvenāsiddha ucyate । na hi sa eva tasya sādhanaṃ bhavati , tadbhāvamātrānuṣaṅgiṇi punastannirdeśasya vaiyarthyāt । na hi tatrāparo viśeṣo nirdiśyate । sa śabdatayā tathābhavanpakṣanirdeśa eva tathā sidhyati , punarapi svata eva tathābhāvāt । tasmātsa svayamātmano heturasiddhaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.a.2>

[II,098,ii]

kathaṃ vai śabdo 'siddhaḥ । siddhaḥ śabdaḥ । sa ātmani heturūpo na siddha ityasiddha ucyate । sa ca śabdaḥ pakṣīkṛtaḥ , na cāparaḥ śabdaḥ , yo hetuḥ syāt । tasyaiva ca hetutve 'punarnirdeśya ityuktam ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.a.3>

[II,098,iii]

avivādaśca , nityaṃ tadbhāvasiddheḥ । anvayādṛṣṭerasiddhiriti cet , tatki<II,099>midānīṃ dharmī dharmyantare 'nvayībhavitā । pradīpādayastu svabhāvayogyatayātmani jñānamutpādayantastathāprakāśamānāḥ svātmaprakāśakā ityucyante । naivaṃ liṅgaliṅginoḥ , bhedāśrayatvāttadbhāvasya । na hi svayaṃ jñānaviṣayatā liṅgasya liṅgipratipādanam । dharmiṇastu svasādhane 'yaṃ prasaṅgaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.a.4>

[II,099,i]

sarvabhāveṣu dharmidharmabhedāsiddheḥ sarvatraiṣa doṣastulya iti cet , uktamatra — bhāvānāṃ vyāvṛttisamāśrayavyavahārabhedātsādhyasādhanabheda iti । paramārthavicāreṣu tathābhūtāsiddhestattvānyatvaṃ padārtheṣu sāṃvṛteṣu pratiṣidhyate । anumānānumeyavyavahāraḥ punaḥ pratyayasiddhaṃ bhedamavalambya praka<II,100>lpyate ॥

[II,100,i]

	yathāsvaṃ bhedaniṣṭheṣu pratyayeṣu vivekinaḥ /
	dharmī dharmāśca bhāsante vyavahārastadāśrayaḥ // <3.77>
	vyavahāropanīto 'tra sa evāśliṣṭabhedadhīḥ /
	sādhyaḥ sādhanatāṃ nītastenāsiddhaḥ prakāśitaḥ // <3.78>
iti saṅgrahaślokau ॥

[II,100,ii]

tasmānna dharmī hetuḥ , ubhayāsiddheḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.b>

[II,100,iii]

etena dharmo 'pi vyākhyātaḥ । tatrāpi yadi tata eva siddhiḥ , sa prāgeva nirdiṣṭa iti pūrvavatprasaṅgo vācyaḥ । anvayāsiddhivacane 'pi , na hi sa evātmānamanvetītyasambaddham ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.c>

[II,100,iv]

yadā tarhi vipakṣavyatireko heturucyate , tadā katham । tatrāpi sādhyābhāvo vipakṣa iti tadvyatirekaḥ sādhyadharma evetyasiddhaḥ ।

<II,101>

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.c.1>

[II,101,i]

nanu pakṣādīnāṃ parasparato bhedādavipakṣatvaṃ pakṣe 'styeva । kaḥ pakṣaḥ ko vā vipakṣaḥ । yatra kaściddharmaḥ sādhayitumiṣṭaḥ , sa pakṣaḥ । tadvyatireko vipakṣaḥ । sa tarhīcchayā vyavasthitalakṣaṇaḥ kathaṃ vipakṣasya vastuvaśādvyavasthāmapanudet । hetuścaivaṃ na kaścidanaikāntikaḥ syāt । vipakṣasyāpīcchākṛtatvādityuktaprāyam । sādhyavyatireke ca vipakṣe tadvyatireko yadi dharmiṇi siddhaḥ , kimasiddham , yadarthaṃ heturucyate ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.c.2>

[II,101,ii]

na vai sādhyāsiddhimātreṇa sarvo vipakṣaḥ , kiṃ tarhi tadvyatirekeṇobhayaniścita ityaniścayātsiddhamavipakṣatvaṃ dharmiṇi । sandigdhasādhyadharmāpyevamavipakṣa iti tadavipakṣatvamaniścitasādhyavyatirekavyāvṛttirūpaṃ kathaṃ sādhanam , aniścitatallakṣaṇatvāt । tenaiva niścayaḥ kriyata iti cet , kathamaniścayānniścayaḥ । vyatirekāniścayo hyavipakṣaśabdenocyate । tata eva ka<II,102>thamabhāvaniścayaḥ । yasmādidamiha sandigdham , tasmādidamiha nāstīti ca subhāṣitam ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.c.3>

[II,102,i]

tasmādanapekṣitapakṣavyavasthau dharmāṇāṃ vṛttivyatirekau parasparaparihārasthitalakṣaṇau na tṛtīyaṃ rāśiṃ vyatirecayataḥ । tayorekasya nivṛttiraparasya vṛttiriti kathamanityābhāvavyatireko 'nitye sādhye dharmiṇi sidhyet । tatkimidānīṃ pakṣo 'pi vipakṣaḥ । syādapi paryāyeṇa । lakṣaṇabhedastu kathita eva । na hyavipakṣaśaṅkāyāṃ sādhyābhāvavyavacchedārthaṃ heturucyate । na ca hetoḥ sambandhopadarśanakāle pakṣādivikalpo 'sti , yato 'yaṃ doṣaḥ syāt । sa hi kevala eva kasyacidbhāvābhāvayorvṛttivyatirekavānupadarśitaḥ svayaṃ bhavatsāmarthyena tattathābhūtamāpādayatīti sa tasya pāścātyaḥ sāmarthyaviṣayaḥ pakṣa ucyate । tena tallakṣaṇamukhenāyāto dharmo na pratyāyanakālabhāvītyanaṅgam ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.d>

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.d.1>

[II,102,ii]

yattarhīdamitaratadviparītavinirmuktatvāditi । na tatraiṣa doṣaḥ , itaragra<II,103>haṇāt । kevalo hi tadviparītavirahaḥ sādhyadharmaḥ syāt , na punaḥ kutaścidasata ityasti sādhyasādhanayorviśeṣaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.d.2>

[II,103,i]

atrāpi viśeṣaṇopādānamiṣṭasyaiva bādhakam । na hi tasyāsattānabhyupagama itaragrahaṇaṃ samarthaṃ bhavati , yathā — māṭharāditaro brāhmaṇo bhojanīya iti । māṭharasyābrāhmaṇye brāhmaṇo bhojanīya ityeva vācyaṃ syāt ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.d.3>

[II,103,ii]

parasyāyamabhiprāyo 'saditi । tadabhiprāyavaśādevamuktam । tenetarāsadviraheṇa tvayopagatatvādityarthaḥ । tatrāpi kaḥ pāramārthiko 'satāṃ parasparato vibhāgaḥ । ekasya hi rūpamanyatrāpaśyantī buddhiridamasmādvibhaktamiti pratyeti । tadarūpāṇāṃ kutaḥ । bhāve vā nāsantaḥ syuḥ , tallakṣaṇatvātsattvasya । kevalaṃ vikalpaviracitamasantamapyeṣāmātmānaṃ vibhāgavantamivānyānyairvyapadeśairvaktāraḥ pradarśayanti । na ca tatkṛ<II,104>to vibhāgo vastuvyavasthāyāḥ samāśrayaḥ , atiprasaṅgādityuktam । itaretaravibhāgaṃ cānena sattānuṣaṅgiṇaṃ prathayatāsattaiva sarvatrotsāditā bhavati । tathāpīdamasiddhamevāsato virahāditi , vyabhicāri vā ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.d.4>

[II,104,i]

athāpi tadabhimatātkutaścinnānābhāva evambhāvaḥ syāt । na tarhi tato nānābhāvādevambhāvo bhavati , kiṃ tarhi tanmateḥ , punaricchāparāvṛttāvanyatrāpyevambhāvasyābhimateḥ । tadihecchāyāmeva sāmarthyamavasthitamiti saiveṣṭavastusvabhāvānukarṣiṇī proktā syāt । tatkimeṣāṃ parasparaviraheṇa । saiva heturvācyaḥ syāt । tatra ca vastupratibandho vācyaḥ , anyathā'siddheḥ । etenātmaparopagamādayaḥ puruṣavyavasthāsamāśrayāḥ sarve hetavo vyākhyātāḥ , yathā — avipakṣatvāt , tatsamudāyaikadeśatvādityādayaḥ । anayā diśā sarvaprayogeṣu vacana<II,105>parāvṛttikṛtaṃ vibhramamutsṛjyārthavyavasthāpananītiranusartavyā ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.3.e>

[II,105,i]

anityaḥ prayatnānantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ , prayatnānantarīyakatvādityeṣa kathaṃ na pratijñārthaikadeśaḥ । tasyaivābhinnavyāvṛttisamāśrayatvādabhinnapratyayaviṣayasya vyavahāropanītasya sādhyadharmiṇaḥ sādhanatve pratijñārthaikadeśatvamuktam । viśeṣaṃ punaḥ sādhyadharmiṇaṃ kṛtvā sāmānyaṃ hetuṃ bruvāṇasya dharmabhedādaṅgāṅgitā na virudhyate ॥

[II,105,ii]

	bhedasāmānyayordharmabhedādaṅgāṅgiteṣyate /
	yathā'nityaḥ prayatnotthaḥ prayatnotthatayā dhvaniḥ // <3.79>
	pakṣāṅgatve 'pyabādhatvānnāsiddhirbhinnadharmiṇi /
	yathāśvo na viṣāṇitvādeṣa piṇḍo viṣāṇavān // <3.80>
	sādhyakālāṅgatā vā na nivṛtterupalakṣya tat /
	tata evāpratijñārtho viśeṣo dharmabhedataḥ // <3.81>
<II,106>
ityantaraślokāḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.iv>

[II,106,i]

tathā svayaṃ tadāśrayasya vā sandehe 'hetuḥ , yathā bāṣpādibhāvena sandigdho bhūtasaṃhāto 'gnisiddhau । yathā ca — iha nikuñje mayūraḥ , kekāyitāditi tadāpātadeśavibhrame ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.1.v>

[II,106,ii]

dharmyasiddhāvapi , yathā — sarvatra sukhādisambhavādvibhurātmeti ॥

[II,106,iii]

evamekasya pakṣadharmasya heturūpasyāsiddhau sandehe vāsiddho hetvābhāsaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2>

[II,106,iv]

tathaikasya rūpasyāsiddhau sandehe vānaikāntikaḥ । katamasyaikasya । vyatirekasya ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.i>

[II,106,v]

asiddhau , yathā caturvidhaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ pakṣadharmaprabhede nirdiṣṭaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii>

[II,106,vi]

sandehe , yathā — asarvajñaḥ kaścidvivakṣitaḥ puruṣo rāgādimānvā , va<II,107>canāderiti ।

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii.a>

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii.a.1>

[II,107,i]

sandigdho 'tra vyatirekaḥ , sarvajño vaktā nopalabdha ityevamprakārasyānupalambhasyādṛśyātmaviṣayatvena sandehahetutvādityuktam । ko hyatra virodho yadi vaktā ca syātsarvajñaśca । yadyatra bhavato mandabuddhicakṣuṣo 'nupalabdhirarthānapākuryāt , hanta hato 'si , pitṛvyapadeśanibandhanasyāpyapāvṛttiprasaṅgāt । vacanasarvajñatvayordvividhasyāpi virodhasyābhāvāt , yaḥ sarvajñaḥ , sa vaktā na bhavatīti vyatireko 'darśane 'pi na sidhyati , sandehāt । bādhakabhāve hyaparābhāvo niścīyate । na cāviruddhalakṣaṇamatīndriyaṃ sujñānabādhanam । tanna vyāptisiddhiḥ sarvo vaktāsarvajña iti ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii.a.2>

[II,107,ii]

sarvavaktṛdharmatāparicchedasya ca kartumaśakyatvāt । sa eva hyevaṃ sarvajñaḥ syādityapratiṣedhaḥ । svātmani svasaṃviditenānenāparatra pari<II,108>ccheda iti cet , nanvevamātmani dṛṣṭasyāparatropanaye 'tiprasaṅgaḥ । dṛṣṭaviruddhasyānupanaya iti cet , tulye nyāye kiṃ nopanayaḥ । na caiṣa nyāyaḥ , lakṣaṇayukte virodhasambhavāt । na darśanamātreṇa , kiṃ tarhi vyatirekādapi । tadabhāvādananyopanaya iti cet , tulyā vṛttitatsandehābhyāmabhāvāsiddhirityanupanayaḥ । dṛśyatayā ca tayorātmanorvirodhopalabdhirityasādhyatvam । adṛśyātmanāṃ tu svapratiyogibhirvirodho 'pi mā bhūt , yena nirastapratipakṣā niyamena niścīyante । tadayaṃ puruṣa ātmānamāntaraiḥ kaiścidananyavedyairdharmairyuktaṃ pratisaṃvedayamānastadupasaṃhāreṇa sarvatra vyavaharanprakāmamāsāditavidyāśramaphalaḥ , yaḥ strīśūdrasādhāraṇamapi vivekaṃ nāvagāhate । tasmādātmani darśanamātreṇānupasaṃhāraḥ , tāvatā vyāptyasiddheḥ । ataḥ sandigdho vyatirekaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii.a.3>

[II,108,i]

pūrvoktāccānupalabdhilakṣaṇādīdṛśāṃ prayogāṇāṃ sandehahetutvamunneyam ॥

<II,109>

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii.b>

[II,109,i]

rāgādīnāmapyarthāntaratvādagatirvacanādanumānalakṣaṇādabhyūhyā , apratibandhāt । asati rāge vacanaṃ nāstītyaniścito vyatirekaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii.b.1>

[II,109,ii]

na hi rāgādīnāmeva kāryaṃ spandavacanādayaḥ , vaktukāmatāsāmānyahetutvāt । saiva rāga iti cet , iṣṭatvādadoṣaḥ । nityasukhātmātmīyadarśanākṣiptaṃ sāsravadharmaviṣayamabhūtaguṇābhinandanaṃ rāgamāhuḥ । tadānandaviṣayoparodhini tatkṛtaścetaso vyāroṣo dveṣaḥ । sa evobhayāśrayaḥ pūrvako viparyāso mohaḥ । naivaṃ karuṇādayaḥ , anyathāpi bhāvāditi vyākhyātaṃ vārttike । tatra yathā rakto bravīti , tathā virakto 'pīti vacanamātrādapratītiḥ । nāpi viśeṣāt , abhiprāyasya durbodhatvādvyavahārasaṅkareṇa sarveṣāṃ vyabhicārāt ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii.b.2>

[II,109,iii]

prayojanābhāvādavyāhāra iti cet , na , parārthatvāt । na yuktaḥ , <II,110> vītarāgatvāditi cet , na , karuṇayāpi vṛtteḥ । saiva rāga iti cet , iṣṭaṃ na nāma nivāryate । rūpaṃ tu bhinnam , aśubhābhinandinaḥ pratisandhibandhāt । ata evāviparyāsodbhavā sā na doṣaḥ । asatyātmagrahe duḥkhaviśeṣadarśanamātreṇābhyāsabalotpādinī bhavatyeva karuṇā । tathā hi dharmālambanādayo maitryādayaḥ sūtre deśitāḥ । etāśca sajātīyābhyāsavṛttayaḥ । naivaṃ rāgādayaḥ , viparyāsābhāve 'bhāvāt । kāruṇikasyāpi niṣphala ārambho viparyāsāditi cet , na , parārthasyaiva phalatveneṣṭatvāt , tallakṣaṇatvācca phalasya ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii.b.3>

[II,110,i]

vaktaryātmani rāgādidarśanenānyatra tadanumāne 'tiprasaṅgo 'pyuktaḥ । vyabhicārādananyānumāna ihāvyabhicāra iti kuto niścayaḥ । adarśane 'pyuktam । dṛśyātmanornāmāyamarvāgdarśanaḥ sahabhāvamitaraṃ vā paśyet , viprakṛṣṭe punararthe 'bhāvanirṇayo 'naikāntikaḥ । ta<II,111>smātkaraṇaguṇavaktukāmate vacanamanumāpayet । nanvatrāpyeṣa tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ — nātmani darśanenānumānamiti । na , tayorihānvayavyatirekābhyāṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvasiddheranyatrānumānāt । na tvevamaśubhābhinandena viparyāsena ca vacanasya tatsiddhiḥ , ātmanyevānyathādarśanāt ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii.b.4>

[II,111,i]

rāgotpattiyogyatārahite vacanādarśanāttadanumāne vyatirekāsiddherna kāryakāraṇatāsiddhiḥ । acetanā vyatirekaviṣaya iti cet , naivaṃvidhādvyatirekātkāraṇaśaktisiddhiḥ । satsu hi samartheṣu tadanyeṣu kāraṇeṣu kāryānutpattiḥ kāraṇāntaramanumāpayati । na caivaṃvidho vyatireko 'cetaneṣu sambhavati । caitanyakaraṇaguṇādereva dṛṣṭaśakterhetosteṣvasambhavātsaṃśayaḥ । rāgasyānupayoge kathaṃ tacchaktirupayujyate , svabhāvaguṇasya śaktāvupacārāt । yatra so 'samarthaḥ , na tatra śakteḥ sāmarthyamastīti ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.1.2.ii.b.5>

[II,111,ii]

tasmānnāntarīyakameva kāryaṃ kāraṇamanumāpayati , tatpratibandhāt । nānyadvipakṣe 'darśane 'pi । sarvadarśino hi darśanavyāvṛttiḥ sa<II,112>rvābhāvaṃ gamayet । kvacittathādṛṣṭānāmapi deśakālabhedenānyathādarśanāt , yathāmalakyaḥ kṣīrāvasekena madhuraphalā bhavanti , na caivaṃ bahulaṃ dṛśyante । tenaivaṃ syādyuktaṃ vaktum — mādṛśo vaktā rāgīti , rāgotpattipratyayaviśeṣeṇātmadarśanāyoniśomanaskāreṇa yogāt । tadāpyapārthako vacanodāhāraḥ । tasmānnāsyāpi vipakṣe 'dṛṣṭimātreṇa vyāvṛttirasandigdhā । tenāyamapyekasya rūpasya sandehādanaikāntikaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.1>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.1.i>

[II,112,i]

dvayorviruddho 'siddhau ca , yathā kṛtakatvaprayatnānantarīyakatve nityatvasādhane । tayoḥ sapakṣe 'sattvaṃ vipakṣe bhāvaśceti dvayo rūpayorasiddhirviparyayasiddhiriti yāvat । tadetau dvau hetū viparyayasādhanādviruddhau ॥

<II,113>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.1.ii>

[II,113,i]

nanu tṛtīyo 'pīṣṭavighātakṛdviruddho 'sti , yathā — parārthāścakṣurādayaḥ saṅghātatvācchayanāsanādyaṅgavaditi । tadiṣṭāsaṃhatapārārthyaviparyayasādhanādviruddhaḥ । sa kasmānnoktaḥ । sādhyatā'bhedāt । na hyayamābhyāṃ sādhyaviparyayasādhanatvena bhidyate । na hīṣṭoktayoḥ sādhyatve kaścidviśeṣa ityuktam । viśeṣe tu viruddhavaddheturapi pṛthagiṣṭasādhano vācyaḥ syāt । ekasyaiva tu vacanena sādhyatā'viśeṣo darśitaḥ । tata eva tadviparyayasādhano viruddho 'pyeka eva । prayogabhedāttu tadbhedaḥ , kvaciduktisāmarthyābhyām , kvacidvivakṣayā , dharmadharmiṇorviśeṣaṇatvenopādānāt । viruddhavaddheturapyevaṃ kiṃ na bhinna iti cet , kaḥ pratiṣeddhā vibhettuḥ । anuktasāmarthyākṣiptamiṣṭaṃ paro 'bhipraitīti tadabhiprāyavaśādiṣṭavighātakṛdityucyate , na punarlakṣaṇabhedāt । ata evāpṛthagnirdeśa ityuktam ॥

<II,114>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.1.iii>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.1.3.a>

[II,114,i]

nanu saṃhatānāmasaṃhataparopakāraniyamābhāvādanaikāntika evetyaviruddhaḥ । ko hyeṣa niyamaḥ — saṃhatāḥ paropakāriṇa iti । yadyapi kvacitkārye 'vadhānavatāmarthānāṃ sāmagrī saṅghātaḥ , tathāpi nāvaśyaṃ kāraṇāni kāryavanti bhavanti , pratibandhādisambhavāditi vyabhicāra eva । apratibaddhopakārāścakṣurādayaḥ paropakāriṇaścet , atrāpi saṃhatopakāriṇa eveti kaḥ pratibandhaniyamaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.1.3.b>

[II,114,ii]

pratyupayogaṃ tebhya upakāryasya svabhāvāntarotpattestathopayogināṃ nānāsvabhāvopakārasādhanametat । naikakālānekopakārasādhanam । upakārasyārthāntaratve 'tadupakārādayo 'pyuktāḥ । anubhayakāriṇāmā<II,115>narthakyāttādarthyasādhanaṃ vipratiṣiddham । tasmādupakurvāṇāścakṣurādaya ādheyātiśayamevopakurvate । sa tasmādekasvabhāvo na bhavatīti viruddhaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.2>

[II,115,i]

caśabdo dvayorekasyāsiddhāvaparasya ca sandehe vyabhicārabhāgiti sūcanārthaḥ । yathā — vītarāgaḥ sarvajño vā vacanāditi । vyatireko 'trāsiddhaḥ , sandigdho 'nvayaḥ । sarvajñavītarāgayorviprakarṣādvacanādestatra sattvamasattvaṃ vā sandigdham ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3>

[II,115,ii]

sandehe vyabhicārabhāk । dvayoriti vartate । yatrānvayo vyatirekaśca sandigdhaḥ , yathā — sātmakaṃ jīvaccharīraṃ prāṇādimattvāditi ।

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.i>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.i.a>

[II,115,iii]

na hi sātmakānātmakābhyāmanyo rāśirasti , yatra prāṇādirvarteta , ātmavṛttivyavacchedābhyāṃ sarvasya saṅgrahāt । nāpyanayorekatra vṛttiniścayaḥ , tādātmyena prasiddhe 'siddheḥ । tasmājjīvaccharīrasambandhī prāṇādiranubhayātmatābahirbhāvāttābhyāṃ na vyatiricyate । na tatrānveti , <II,116> ekātmanyapyasiddheḥ । ata evānvayavyatirekayoḥ sandehādanaikāntikaḥ , sādhyetarayorato 'niścayāt ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.i.b>

[II,116,i]

nāpyapratipattiḥ , kenacitsambandhāt । asambandhādvimarśo na jāyate , yathā cākṣuṣatvācchabde । sambandhātkiṃsambaddho 'yamiti kathaṃ na vimṛśet । aparijñātasambandhādgarbhātpuruṣaviśeṣasambandhe 'sambandhāyogādyathā saṃśete , tathehāpi sarvānantarbhāvāyogātsaṃśayaḥ । apratipattiranubhayapratipattisaṃśayarūpā sobhayabahirbhāve syāt , antarbhāve kathamapratipattiḥ । evaṃ tarhi cākṣuṣatvādapyastu । na , asambandhādityuktam । tasmātsaṃśayaheturasādhāraṇaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.i.c>

[II,116,ii]

viśeṣataḥ prāṇādayaḥ । viprakarṣādātmano vṛttivyatirekāsiddhestatra prāṇādīnāmapi । arthāntarādakāryabhūtādasiddheśca । na hi kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ prāṇādīnāmātmanaśca sidhyati , tasyopalambhānupalambhāśrayatvāt । tena nāpratibaddhasya bhāve bhāva iti saṃśayaḥ ॥

<II,117>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.a>

[II,117,i]

gamakā evātmanaḥ prāṇādayaḥ , tadvyatirekasyaikāntikatvādityaparaḥ । vipakṣādeva hi prāṇādayo nivartante , na sapakṣāt , asato nivṛttyayogāt । tasmādaikāntikānvayavadaikāntikavyatireko 'pi gamaka eva । na caivaṃ śrāvaṇatvam , ubhayato vyāvṛtteriti ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.b>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.b.1>

[II,117,ii]

tenaivamprakāraṃ vyatirekaṃ varṇayatāvinābhāva evokto bhavati । tathā hyātmābhāva eva na bhavatyevetyarthādananyasaṃsargiṇyātmavṛttiḥ sūcitā bhavati । saivāvinābhāvaḥ । tata evānvayasiddhiriti na vyatirekī । pratibandhaścāvinābhāvaḥ । sa cātmapratibandhastādātmyatadutpattibhyāmanyo nāstītyuktam । te ca darśanena vinā na sidhyataḥ । tannātmāvinābhāvī prāṇādiḥ । tata eva nātmanivṛttāvasya nivṛttirapi , yato vyatirekītyucyate । na hyapratibaddhaḥ kasyacinnivṛttau niyamena nivartate । tasmādviśeṣasya na vyatireko nānvayaḥ । adarśanamātramāśrityācāryeṇa śrāvaṇatve vyatireka uktaḥ । na tāvatābhāvagatirityuktam । anyathā saṃśayahetureva na syāt । na hi yo yatra na sambhavati , tadupalabdhyā tatra <II,118> saṃśayo yuktaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.b.2>

[II,118,i]

prāṇādyabhāvena nairātmyasya vyāpterātmanivṛttau prāṇādinivṛttiriti cet , na , apratibaddhābhāvenānupayogino 'bhāvasya vyāptyasiddheḥ । yadi prāṇādayastadātmatayā tadutpattyā vātmapratibaddhāḥ syuḥ , te tannivṛttyā nivarteran । tadā prāṇādyabhāvo nairātmyaṃ vyāpnuyāt । tadabhāve 'bhāvasiddhyā vyāptiriti sā na sidhyati , viparyaye pratibandhāsiddheḥ । upalambhānupalambhābhyāṃ hi tayoḥ pratibandhaṃ jānīyāt , tau cātyantaparokṣasya na sidhyataḥ । ke ca nirātmānaḥ prāṇādyabhāvena vyāptāḥ । ghaṭādayaścet , anyatrādṛṣṭaḥ sa ghaṭādau neti kutaḥ । tenājñātavyatirekasya vyāvṛttivyāptirasiddhā । prāṇādayo 'pi hi kvaciddarśanādeva sadasantaḥ pratīyante , na caivamātmeti na tasya sadasattvapratītiḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.b.3>

[II,118,ii]

yadapyāha — yadi na sātmakaṃ jīvaccharīram , prāṇādivirahaprasaṅgaḥ , nairātmyādghaṭādivaditi , tadapyakāryakāraṇabhāve na sidhyati । uktaṃ hi prāk <II,119> — nānupalabdhāvakāryakāraṇapratiṣedho gamaka iti । sa ca kāraṇabhāvo 'darśanādātmano na sidhyatītyuktam ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.b.4>

[II,119,i]

darśane 'pi vyatirekāsiddherna sidhyati । ghaṭādayo vyatirekaviṣayā iti cet , naivaṃvidhādvyatirekātkāraṇasāmarthyasiddhiḥ । satsu samartheṣvanyeṣu hetuṣu kāryānutpattiḥ kāraṇāntarabhāvaṃ gamayatītyuktam । buddhyādayo 'pi hi prāṇāderhetavo ghaṭādau na santi । tasmātsandigdhasāmarthya ātmano vyatirekaḥ । te 'pi buddhyādayo nairātmye na syuriti cet , na , tatrānyeṣāmeva sāmarthyadarśanāt । cakṣurādibuddhīnāṃ tāvadyathāsvamindriyaviṣayau hetū । pūrvakaṃ cāviguṇaṃ vijñānam , tasya viṣayāntaravikṣepapratighātādāvuttaravijñānānutpattivyākulatādidarśanāt । manovijñānasya pūrvakamaviguṇaṃ vijñānam । indriyādīnāmapi pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ sabhāgāva<II,120>sthābheda upādānahetuḥ , buddhiśca pratyaya ityetāvato 'yamātmabhāvo 'nvayavyatirekabhāgityayameva hetuḥ । anavasthānyakalpane syāt ॥

[II,120,i]

	yasminsati bhavatyeva yattato 'nyasya kalpane /
	taddhetutvena sarvatra hetūnāmanavasthitiḥ // <3.82>
iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.c>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.c.1>

[II,120,ii]

tulyaśca śrāvaṇatvena prāṇādirvyabhicāreṇa । na , tadvyatirekasya vyabhicārāt । kathaṃ vyabhicāraḥ । na hi tasyāsapakṣādeva vyatireka iti । nanvevamasya sapakṣe 'nuvṛttyabhāvaḥ kathyate । so 'parasyāpi tulya iti kathamasamaḥ prāṇādiḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.c.2>

[II,120,iii]

asapakṣa eva nāstīti cāsya sapakṣe 'stitocyate , pratiṣedhadvayena prakṛtagamanāt । anyathā vyavacchedyābhāvādavadhāraṇasya kiṃ phalaṃ syāt । anavadhāraṇe ca vākyasya vyatirekasyāvyabhicārāsiddheḥ । <II,121> tata eva sapakṣa evāsti , asapakṣa eva nāstīti dṛṣṭāntayoranyatareṇārthāpattyobhayapradarśanamāha । tasmādīdṛśo vyatirekāvyabhicāro 'nanvayeṣu na sidhyati । sidhyaṃśca balādanvayamāpādayati , pratiṣedhaniṣedhasya vidhānarūpatvāt ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.c.3>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.c.3.1>

[II,121,i]

asataḥ sapakṣānna nivṛttirityasapakṣa eva nāstīti cet , neti saiva nivṛtternivṛttirasataḥ kathamiṣṭā । abhāvapratiṣedho hi bhāvo 'satyapyasti , bhāvapratiṣedhastu na sambhavatītyaskhalitaprajño devānāṃ priyaḥ , yastadviṣayaṃ pratiṣedhaṃ necchatyasadabhāva ityevamādi ca vyavaharati । nirloṭhitaścāyamartho 'sati nāstitetyatrāntare । tena neha pratanyate ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.c.3.2>

[II,121,ii]

na cāsannātmā , sattāsādhanavṛtteḥ । sandigdhaḥ syāt । na ca pareṇa <II,122> tathopagata ityapramāṇādabhyupagamāttathaiva bhavati , atiprasaṅgāt । na copagamabalena sapakṣāsapakṣau vyavasthāpya pramāṇapravartanaṃ yuktam । evaṃ hyāgamasiddha ātmā syāt , nānumānasiddhaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.c.4>

[II,122,i]

tasmādavyatireke 'pyasataḥ sapakṣādvyatirekaḥ sandigdhaḥ syātprāṇādīnām , ātmanaḥ sandehāt । ata eva vipakṣādapi । ekatra hi niyame siddhe 'nyanivartanaṃ sidhyet । anyathā hi kvaciddṛṣṭe 'bhāvasiddhāvapi syādevādṛṣṭeṣu saṃśayaḥ । tathā hyasakalavyaktibhedavyāpino 'pyarthāḥ kecittajjātisambhavino dṛṣṭāḥ , pārthivālohalekhyavat । virodhasya cādṛṣṭeḥ sandeha eva । nairātmyena prāṇādīnāmuktalakṣaṇasya virodhasyāsiddheḥ sandigdho nairātmyādvyatirekaḥ । ātma<II,123>pratiniyame hi tatkāryātmatayā prāṇādīnāṃ nairātmyena saha virodhaḥ syāt । sa ca na sidhyatītyuktam ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.d>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.d.1>

[II,123,i]

astu nāma nirātmakebhyo vyatirekaḥ prāṇādīnāṃ tadbhāve ca nairātmyavyāvṛttiḥ , tathāpi nānairātmyādātmā jīvaccharīre sidhyati , yenāyaṃ na vyatirekasyābhāvaṃ bhāvamicchati , yathā vyatirekābhāve 'pi sapakṣe prāṇādirneṣṭaḥ ॥

[II,123,ii]

	sapakṣāvyatirekī ceddheturheturato 'nvayī /
	nānvayyavyatirekī cedanairātmyaṃ na sātmakam // <3.83>
iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.d.2>

[II,123,iii]

na prāṇādisambhavena nairātmyavyāvartanādātmagatiḥ , kiṃ tarhi vidhimukhenaiva prāṇādaya ātmānaṃ gamayantīti cet , kimidānīṃ nairātmyā<II,124>dvyatirekasya phalam । sa hi tatrāsambhavansvasambhavena tadasambhavaṃ sādhayatīti tato vyatirekī varṇyeta । anyathātmasannidhāyane ko nairātmyādvyatirekasyopayogaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.ii.d.3>

[II,124,i]

kathaṃ vāprasiddhātmaniyamāḥ prāṇādaya ātmānaṃ vidadhatīti vaktavyam । atiprasaṅgo hyevaṃ syādityasādhāraṇānaikāntika eva prāṇādiḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.iii>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.3.a>

[II,124,ii]

sādhāraṇamapi khalu prameyatvamasaṃskṛtāpavādino 'satyanvayāyogādavyabhicaritānvayaṃ sapakṣa evāstītyanvayinameva hetumāha ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.3.b>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.3.b.1>

[II,124,iii]

atrāpi kathamavyatireko vipakṣāt , kathaṃ vā sapakṣa evāstīti । kiṃ hyasyāvadhāraṇasya phalaṃ yadi na vipakṣe 'stitvaṃ vyavacchidyeta । vyavacchede vā kathamavyatirekaḥ । na hi sattāpratiṣedhādanyo vyatirekaḥ । vipratiṣiddhaṃ <II,125> caitat — nānvayo na vyatireka iti । ya eva khalu netyanvayapratiṣedhaḥ , sa eva vyatireka iti ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.3.b.2>

[II,125,i]

tatpunaridamāyātam — asato vyatirekāyogāditi । atredameva punarvācyam — kathamasato 'nvayapratiṣedha iti । vasturūpānukarṣī khalvasati pratiṣedho na sambhavet । na hi paryudāsa evaiko naño viṣayaḥ , kiṃ tarhi prasajyapratiṣedho 'pi । na hi tasyāsati virodhaḥ । so 'pi na sambhavati , adhikaraṇādyarthānāṃ pratiṣedhaviṣayopadarśanīnāṃ vibhaktīnāmayogāditi cet , uktottarametat । tasmānna hetuḥ kaścidanvayī nāma ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.3.c>

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.3.c.1>

[II,125,ii]

na ca prameyatvasya vipakṣe 'nvayāyogaḥ । trividho hi dharmo bhāvābhāvobhayāśraya ityuktam । nābhāvasya kaściddharma iti cet , nanvayamevāsya dharmaviraho dharmaḥ । na hi vasturūpameva dharmaḥ , asanto 'pi kenaci<II,126>tprakaraṇenemaṃ vyavahārapathamupanīyante । anyathā hi tatrāvyavahāra eva syāt । na ca satāmapi paramārthataḥ kaściddharmadharmibhāvaḥ । kevalaṃ buddhirevaṃsambandhamuparacayatītyuktaṃ vārttike । buddhikṛtā ca ghaṭanāsatsu kena nivāryate ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.3.c.2>

[II,126,i]

sadasadubhayānubhayavyavasthāśca tadatatsamayavatāmaniścitasādhanā naikāntagrāhiṇyaḥ syuḥ । tasmādyathā kathañcidapyanenāsato niścinvatā prameyā vaktavyāḥ । na hi bhāvaviṣayameva pramāṇam , avisaṃvādalakṣaṇatvātpramāṇasya । tatsadasatī tadbhāvena vyavasthāpayanna cetsvaviṣaye pareṇa bādhyate । tadasya pramāṇalakṣaṇamastīti prameyo 'bhāvaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.2.3.3.c.3>

[II,126,ii]

naivābhāvaḥ kaścit , sarveṣāṃ kathañcidbhāvāditi cet , yathā te na santi , sa prakāro 'bhāvaḥ । śaśaviṣāṇayoścāyaṃ bhāvācchaśaviṣāṇā<II,127>bhāvavādinamupahasannātmānamevopahasati । śaśāvayavabhūtaṃ viṣāṇaṃ nāstītyabhidhātari kaḥ prastāvaḥ śaśo 'pyasti viṣāṇaṃ cetyuttarasya । na hyayaṃ viṣāṇamātramapahnute , yatastena pratirudhyeta , kiṃ tarhi śaśasambandhi । yadyevaṃ sambandho nāstīti vaktavyam , na viṣāṇam । kiṃ vai sambandhamātraṃ viśiṣyate viṣāṇināmapi viṣāṇeṣu , na dravyasvabhāvaḥ । svabhāvo 'pi , pratikāryaṃ kāraṇasvabhāvabhedāt । tatko 'yaṃ sambandhābhāvo vācya ityupālambhaḥ । asti viṣāṇināṃ viṣāṇasvabhāvabhedaḥ , na tadvatkiñcicchaśasya bhinnasvabhāvaṃ viṣāṇamiti cet , vayamapyetadeva brūmaḥ । yo vā sambandho nāstītyucyate , sa evābhāvaḥ । sambandhī vidyate na sambandha iti ca nipuṇā vāco yuktiḥ । aṅgīkṛtasambandhaṃ dravyamapi neti cet , priyamanuṣṭhitam । yadīdameva prathamamucyeta , na parikleśito devānāṃ priyaḥ syāditi ॥

<II,128>

<§ 3.IV.2.3>

<§ 3.IV.2.3.1>

[II,128,i]

viruddhāvyabhicāryapi saṃśayaheturuktaḥ , sa iha noktaḥ , anumānaviṣaye 'sambhavāt । na hi sambhavo 'sti kāryasvabhāvayoruktalakṣaṇayoranupalambhasya vā viruddhāvyabhicāritāyām । na cānyo 'vyabhicārī । tasmādavastudarśanabalapravṛttamāgamāśrayamanumānamāśritya tadarthavicāreṣu viruddhāvyabhicārī sādhanadoṣa uktaḥ , śāstrakārāṇāmartheṣu bhrāntyā viparītasvabhāvopasaṃhārasambhavāt । na hyasti sambhavo yathāvasthitavastusthitiṣvātmakāryānupalambheṣu ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.3.2>

<§ 3.IV.2.3.2.i>

<§ 3.IV.2.3.2.i.a>

[II,128,ii]

tatrodāharaṇam — sarvagataṃ sāmānyam , sarvadeśāvasthitaiḥ svasambandhibhiryugapatsambandhāt , ākāśavaditi ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.3.2.i.b>

[II,128,iii]

tatsambandhisvabhāvamātrānubandhinī taddeśasannihitasvabhāvatā । na hi yo yatra nāsti , sa taddeśamātmanā vyāpnoti । nanu nākāśadeśe <II,129> rūpādayastaddeśāṃśca ghaṭādīnvyāpnuvanti । āstāṃ tāvadayaṃ pradeśapradeśibhāvo yaḥ saṃyogasamavāyābhyām , laukikaṃ tu pradeśamāśritya brūmo vicchinnāvicchinnāvabhāsivijñānotpādanayogyatālakṣaṇam । yutāyutasiddhayoḥ sambandhau saṃyogasamavāyāviti śāstre 'pi vyavasthā । tadiyaṃ svasattāmātrānubandhini taddeśasannidhau sādhye tatsambandhitā hetuḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.3.2.i.c>

[II,129,i]

nanu svāśrayavyāptivādināpi taddeśasannidhiriṣyata eveti kimaniṣṭam । akriyasyaikavyaktisambandhino deśāntare 'pūrvavyaktiprādurbhāve prāktatrāsatastatsambandhāyogaḥ । tasmādbhinnadeśairyugapatsambandhaḥ sarvavyāpini sidhyati । tadekasambandhino deśāntare 'gatvātaddeśairapūrvairabhisambandha ekasya tadantarālavyāptināntarīyakaḥ , ātapāderiva ghaṭādibhiriti ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.3.2.ii>

<§ 3.IV.2.3.2.ii.a>

[II,129,ii]

dvitīyo 'pi prayogaḥ — na sarvagataṃ sāmānyam , upalabdhi<II,130>lakṣaṇaprāptasya tadantarāleṣvanupalambhāt ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.3.2.ii.b>

[II,130,i]

upalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptirabhivyaktiḥ । abhedādekavyaktyā sarvavyakteravyaktarūpavirahaḥ । avyavadhānamadūrasthānaṃ dṛśyātmatendriyasya svāśrayeṇa sambandhaḥ , abhedādeva , āśrayāsamavetarūpavirahaśca । samānadeśāśrayendriyayogāpekṣāyāmāśrayasamānāsamānadeśarūpasyābhedavirodhaḥ । dṛśyādṛśyātmatādivirodhā api vācyāḥ ॥

[II,130,ii]

tadayamanupalambhaḥ svabhāvaśca parasparaviruddhārthasādhanāvekatra saṃśayaṃ janayataḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.3.3>

[II,130,iii]

śāstrakāro viruddhadharmanāntarīyakatāṃ dvayorapaśyaṃstayoravirodhadarśitayā prāheti sambhavo viruddhāvyabhicāriṇaḥ । vastvanurodhini punaranumāne yathā virodhinorekatrāsambhavaḥ , tathā tadabhivyāptayorapīti na tāvekatra staḥ । tannātra viruddhāvyabhicārī । tadayamabhyupagamabalapravṛttaḥ ॥

<§ 3.IV.2.3.4>

[II,130,iv]

ācāryeṇa punardiṅmātradarśanāyedamudāharaṇamuktam — anityaḥ śabdaḥ <II,131> kṛtakatvāt , nityaḥ śrāvaṇatvāditi । atra hi trayamapramāṇakamabhyupeyam — vyatirekiśabdatvasāmānyamindriyagamyaṃ nityaṃ ca । ato 'sya pramāṇasya vṛttiḥ । tannaitadvastubalāyātaṃ kṛtakatvaṃ pratibadhnāti । kṛtakatvaprastāve cānāgamāśrayānnāgamopanyāsaḥ । sādhyaśca pratibandho yacchrāvaṇaṃ tannityamityavyabhicāro 'pi na sidhyatīti ॥ ॥

<II,132>

{3.V}

<§ 3.V.1>

[II,132,i]

	hetostrilakṣaṇatvānna dṛṣṭāntaḥ pṛthagucyate /

[II,132,ii]

trilakṣaṇo heturuktaḥ । tāvatā cārthapratītiriti na pṛthagdṛṣṭānto nāma kaścitsādhanāvayavaḥ । tena nāsya lakṣaṇaṃ pṛthagucyate , gatārthatvāt । hetoḥ sapakṣa eva sattvaṃ vipakṣācca sarvato vyāvṛttī rūpamuktamabhedena । punarviśeṣeṇa kāryasvabhāvayorjanmatanmātrānubandhau darśanīyāvuktau । tacca darśayatā — yatra dhūmastatrāgniḥ , asatyagnau na kvaciddhūmaḥ , yathā mahānasetarayoḥ । yatra kṛtakatvaṃ tatrānityatvam , anityatvābhāve kṛtakatvasyāsambhavaḥ , yathā ghaṭākāśayoriti darśanīyam । na hyanyathā sapakṣavipakṣayoḥ sadasattve yathoktaprakāre śakye darśayitum , tatkāryatāpratiniyamaḥ svabhāvavyāptirvā । asmiṃścārthe darśite darśita eva dṛṣṭānto bhavati , etāvanmātrarūpatvāttasya ॥

<§ 3.V.2>

<§ 3.V.2.1>

[II,132,iii]

etenaiva dṛṣṭāntadoṣā api nirastā bhavanti , yathā — nityaḥ śabdo <II,133> 'mūrtatvātkarmavatparamāṇuvadghaṭavaditi sādhyādivikalāḥ । sandigdhāśca — rāgādimānvacanādrathyāpuruṣavadityādayaḥ । ananvayo 'pradarśitānvayaśca , yathā — yo vaktā sa rāgādimāniṣṭapuruṣavat । anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtakatvādghaṭavaditi । tathā viparītānvayaḥ — yadanityaṃ tatkṛtakamiti । sādharmyeṇa ॥

<§ 3.V.2.2>

[II,133,i]

vaidharmyeṇāpi — paramāṇuvatkarmavadākāśavaditi sādhyādyavyatirekiṇaḥ । tathā sandigdhavyatirekādayo vācyāḥ ॥

<§ 3.V.2.3>

[II,133,ii]

na hyebhirhetoḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ viśeṣalakṣaṇaṃ vā śakyaṃ darśayitum । tadarthāpattyaiṣāṃ nirāso veditavyaḥ ॥

<§ 3.V.3>

[II,133,iii]

yadi punarheturūpāsaṃsparśī svatantra eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhanāvayavaḥ syāt , tadā
	tadrūpāsparśane ca syādasambandhādapārthakaḥ // <3.84>

<II,134>

[II,134,i]

yadi na hetoravyabhicāradharmatā dṛṣṭāntena pradarśyeta , kaḥ sādhyasādhane tasyopayogaḥ , asambandhāt । na hi kathañcitsādṛśyamātreṇārthānāṃ kenacidātmāntarapratiniyamaḥ , yenopamānātsādhanaṃ syāt । na hyarthasya kenacitkathañcinna sāmyam । tatastadātmatāyāṃ sarvaṃ sarvātmakaṃ syāt । na caitadyuktam । tasmāttadabhivyāptadharmayogādeva bhāvāstadvantaḥ syurityabhivyāptirasya dṛṣṭāntena pradarśyate । tadayaṃ na svatantraḥ । tadasambandhī cāpārthakaḥ , tenaivārthaparisamāpteriti ॥ ॥

<II,135>

{3.VI}

<§ 3.VI.1>

<§ 3.VI.1.1>

[II,135,i]

	dūṣaṇā nyūnatādyuktiḥ	...

[II,135,ii]

ye pūrvaṃ nyūnatādayaḥ sādhanadoṣā uktāḥ , teṣāmudbhāvanaṃ dūṣaṇam , tena pareṣṭārthasiddhipratibandhāt ॥

<§ 3.VI.1.2>

[II,135,iii]

nanvanudbhāvite 'pi doṣe 'rthasyaivāsāmarthyānna bhavati prasiddhiḥ । evametat । kiṃ tu nārthānāṃ niṣpattyaniṣpattī sādhanadūṣaṇābhyāṃ kriyete , teṣāṃ sarvadā tādavasthyāt , kiṃ tarhi puruṣasāmarthyasiddhiḥ । sā vacanamantareṇa na sidhyatīti sa tathābhūtameva khyāpayaṃstasya kartetyucyate । yadi punarudbhāvite 'pi doṣe sampūrṇavacanādinā pratisamādadhīta na tadiṣṭapratibandha iti na dūṣaṇaṃ syāt । na , tasya sādhanāntaratvāt ॥

<§ 3.VI.1.3>

[II,135,iv]

yadi pūrvapakṣavādī sākāṅkṣaḥ syādasamāptavākya eveti na dūṣaṇāvasaraḥ । <II,136> sthitavacane tu tasmindoṣamudbhāvayandūṣaka eva tasya sādhanasya ॥

<§ 3.VI.2>

[II,136,i]

							... tadābhāsāstu jātayaḥ /

[II,136,ii]

	mithyottarāṇāmānantyātpratanyante na tā iha // <3.85>

[II,136,iii]

mithyottarāṇi jātayaḥ । teṣāṃ ca nāntaḥ , ayoniśovikalpānāmapratiṣṭhānāt । yathāha paraḥ — nāstyātmeti pratijñāvirodho nāma pratijñādoṣaḥ , arthāpahnave śabdaprayogāsambhavāt । prayuñjāno 'rthamupasthāpayati , apahnute ceti pratijñāpadayorvirodhātpratijñādoṣa iti । yathā cāha — dharmiviśeṣaṇatvenopādānādanityaḥ prayatnānantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ prayatnānantarīyakatvāditi pratijñārthaikadeśa iti । na hyevamādīni yathoktalakṣaṇāsu jātiṣvantarbhavanti । na ca dūṣaṇāni , śabdārthānapahnavena svalakṣaṇapratiṣedhāt , sādhyadharmibahirbhāvāccetyuktam । <II,137> tānyapi kenacilleśenāsvevāntarbhavantīti cet , āsāmapi parasparameṣa prasaṅga ityekameva kiñcitsāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ vācyaṃ syāt , viśeṣe 'nantarbhāvāt । tacca sāmānyalakṣaṇamuktameva dūṣaṇābhāsāstu jātaya iti । tāḥ sādhanadūṣaṇalakṣaṇajñānādevāviṣaye 'pravṛtteḥ , pratipatterapratibandhāt , pratibandhalakṣaṇavirahācca , uttarābhāsatvena sujñānāḥ । prabhedaḥ punarāsāmānantyādaśakyanirdeśa iti na nirdiśyate ॥ ॥

<§ 3.concluding verse>

[II,137,i]

	yukto 'yamartha iti sūtramamoghanīter draṣṭurmayāgamitamāgamamadhyupekṣya /
	tasyāpyavaśyamavadātadhiyo 'yameva bhāvo 'vibhāvitadhiyāvidito janena //

<॥ pramāṇaviniścaye parārthānumānaparicchedastṛtīyaḥ ॥>

<॥ samāptaścāyaṃ pramāṇaviniścayaḥ ॥ ॥>
